Ama-Welsh AMs akhathazwe ukuthi ‘azobukeka njengeziphungumangathe’
Bayazibuza baziphendule abanye phakathi kwama-AM ngombono wokuthi kushintshe indlela ababizwa ngayo kuthiwe ama-MWPs (Member of the Welsh Parliament).
Lokhu kususwa izinhlelo zokushintsha kokubizwa kwenhlanganyela yePhalamende lama Welsh.
Ama-AMs kuzo zonke izinhlaka zepolitiki anovalo lokuthi loku kobabizela ukuhlekwa.

Ilunga le Welsh Conservative lona lithe njengeqembu bazimisele ukwamukela ushintsho lwegama kodwa wakuphawula ukuthi uMWP useduzane kakhulu nokubizwa ngesiduphunga.

Umthetho Kahulumeni wase-Wales Act 2017 wanikeza inhlangano yama-Welsh igunya lokushintsha igama labo.
NgoJuni Ikhomishane yashicilela imiphumela yenhlolovo yomphakathi ngemibono, eyathola ukwesekwa okukhulu ukushisntshwa inhlangano ibizwe ngephalamende lama Welsh.
Odabeni lokubizwa kwama-AMs ikhomishane iseke u-WMP kanti uvo lomphakathi lona lubonakalise ukuncika ku-MWP.
Ama-AMs wona afake eyawo nayo imibono kodwa lomdonsiswano uzoba yinkinga ku-Elin Jones okunguyena owengamele ukwenziwa kohlaka lomthetho woshinstho emavikini azayo.
Imithetho yokubuyekezwa izombandakanya ukushintshwa kwendlela umhlangno osebbenza ngayo, kumbandakanya imithetho yokuhoxiswa kwama-AM nokuhlelwa kwekomidi.
Ama-AM azoba nezwi lokugcina odabeni lokuthi azobizwa ngani uma sekuxoxiswana ngomthetho.

I-Sainsbury izobangisana ne-Bots, Superdrug ne Debenhams ngezitolo zayo ezihlukeniseke ngemikhakha yobuhle nabasizi abaqeqeshekile.

Le supamakethe izophinde ikhiphe kabusha ezokuziphaqula ubuso ukuze iningi nlemikhiqizo yabo ibe nokuyizitshalo nezithelo kuphela njengoba iningi labathengi abancane befuna loko.

Isithombe esisephalamende sa-Cromwell sibe isikhumbuzo samumva.
Lokhu kuye kwabangela iningi labahlali baseNgilandi ukuba lithikamezeke ngenxa yamasiko kanye nezinkolelo.
Nokho u-Cromwell uchaze umbono ka Mr Crick njengowubuwula futhi efuna ukbhala kabusha umlando.
U-John Godsmith omele i-Cromwell Society uthe: “Kumangazile kakhulu ukuzwa mayelana nokususwa kwesithombe ebesingaphandle kwephalamende
Abezempi abatholanga myalezo ovela ku-Cromwell.
Mhlawumbe u-Cromwell ubengaba idlozi elikahle ku-Thomas owayephila ngesikhati sangaphambili.
Umnumuzane William Hmao obemelele u-Cromwelll ngezango-19th century ebambe naye iqembu ukholelwa ukuthi ukumukhumbula kungaba into inhle.
Umnumzane u-Goldsmith watshela ithelegrafu ngesonto “u-Cromwell unconywa iningi, mhlawumbe kunaba into ekahe ukukhnjulwa kwakhe.
Kungakhathaliseki ukthi umlando uvusa kuphi ukungezwani.
Emakhulwini e-17 aye ashintha isizwe futhi u-Cromwell uvele phambili njengomummeleli ongahlukanisa aphinde akhe intuthuko yezwe lakithi.
Imiphumela ayithola njengenkosi yobuvikeli kufanele ikhunjulwe nayo.
Ingulube ilume yaze yabulala umlimi wase China.
Lomlimi wahlaselwa futhi wabulawa yingulube emakethe yase-Southwest China, ngokulandisa kwabezindaba.
Le ndoda,eyesibongo sakwa Yuan itholakale ifile ,igcwelel igazi emzimbeni emakethe yase-Liupanshui esifundaweni sase-Guizhou eningizimu yase-China ngesonto.
Umlimi onezingulube ulungele ukuzijova ngohlaka 30 enyangeni kaMay 2005 e-Xining yase Qinghai ,e-China.
Uye wavakashela umzala wakhe yena ohlala eYunnan esifundazweni sifanayo ngolwesithathu ukuze amdayisele izingulube ezingu 15 emakethe.
Osukwini olulalendelayo ekseni ,umzala wakhe atholakala efile,eduze komnyango kukhona ingulube.
Uthi lengulube yayi eyesilisa ikhuluphele  Inkulu inegazi emlonyeni.
Ngemva kokuhlolwa okuningiliziwe uqinisekise ngokuthi lengulube yesisindo sama pound angu-550 iyona eyadla lomlimi.
”Umlenze womzala wami wawugcwele igazi,” kwasho umzala, wathi isibongo sakhe “ngu-WU,” kwasho izindaba zakusihlwa zase-Guiyang.
Amakhamera abinisa u-Yuan engena emakethe ngo 4:40 ngolwesine ezokondla izingulube.
Umzimba wakhe watholwa ngemva kwehora.
Isilwane esabulala lendoda sasingesona esika Yuan noma umzala wakhe.
Umphathi walemakethe utshele abaezindaba ukuthi lengulube yayivalelwe ukuvimbela ukthi ingalimazi muntu ,kuyilapho amaphoyisa eqeoqa ubufakazi.
Umndeni ka-Yuan neziphahimandla zasemakethe ziyaxoxisana mayelana nokulungiselela umufi umngcwabo.
Nakuba kungavamile, amacala ezingulube ezihlasela abantu aye abikwa ngaphambilini.
Ngo-2016, ingulube yahlaseka owesifazane nomyeni wakhe epulazini labo e-Massachusetts, yashiya indoda ilimele kabi.
Eminyakeni eyishumi edlule, ingulube enesisindo esingamaphawundi angu-650 yahlasela ugandaganda ohamba u-Welsh umlimi kwaze kwaba umkakhe osabisa lesi silwane.
Ngemva kokuba umlimi wase-Oregon edliwe yizingulube zakhe ngo-2012, omunye wabalimi base-Manitoba watshela Abezindaba e-CBC ukuthi izingulube akuvamile ukuthi zibe nolaka kodwa iphunga legazi "kungazibangela."
"Zimane nje ziyathanda ukudlala.
Zibukeka zilungile nezifuna ukwazi ... zisuke zingaphumelanga ukukulimaza.
Uthi, kudingeka nje uzihloniphe.
Izinsalela Zesishingishane uRosa zizoletha izimvula ezingamandla eningizimu-ntshonalanga ye-US
Ngokwesibikezelo sezulu, Isishingishane uRosa sizoya ngokuphelelwa amandla uma sesiya ngasemanzini apholile asogwini lwasenyakathi ye-Mexico.
Nokho, uRosa uzoletha .
uRosa unesivinini somoya esingu 85 mph, isiphepho ngasinye, kusukela ngo 5 a.m. Eastern time Sunday, and was located 385 miles southwest of Punta Eugenia, Mexico.
uRosa ulindelwe ukuba abheke eNyakatho ngeSonto.
Okwamanje,umkhombe uyaqala ushintsha isimo kwi-Pacific Ocean futhi uhamba ngempumalanga ubheke entshonalanga  yase U.S Njengoba uRosa esondela esiqhingini sase Baja California ngoMsombuluko isiphepho sizoqala ukuqinisa ngomswakama ezindaweni zaseNyakatho phakathi neNtshonalanga e-U.S.
uRosa uzoletha imvula enobude obubalelwa kuma-inches ayishumi ezindaweni ezithile eMexico ngoMsombuluko.
Ngakho-ke, ezinsukwini ezilandelayo umswakama uzohlangana nomkhombe bese kwakhekha imvula enamandla futhi eyandile ezindaweni zaseNtshonalanga.
LocalEzindaweni ezisondele, imvula ebalelwa kwi-inch kuya kwamane izodala izikhukhula ezigubezelayo eziyingozi, ukukhukhuleka kwadoti ngisho nokudilika kwenhlabathi ezingwadule.
tropiUmswakama uzokwenza izinga lemvula libe nga-inches amabili kuya kwamathathu ngehora ngokunembile, ikakhulukazi ezindaweni zaseNingizimu yase-Nevada nase Arizona.
Amazinga emvula angaba ngama-inch amabili kuya kwamane ilindelekile e Ningizimu yasentshonalanga,ikakhulukazi eningi yayo e Arizona.
Izikhukhula ezigubezelayo zikindelekile zihambisana nesimo esiwohloza ngokushesha ngenxa yokuhlakazeka kwemvelo ye mvula enomswakama.
Kungaba ubuwula ukuvula ibhizinisi okwagule empeleni ngoba sekuza izimvula ezinoswakama.
Izimvula ezinamandla zingabangela imihosha ukuba ibe imifula ebukeka ngathi iseniminyaka yaba khona ukuduma kona kobangela isivuthela somoya ezindaweni eziseduze ozobe uhamba nothuli.
Izikhombe ezizayo zizoletha imvula enamandla ezindaweni ezisondelene neNingizimu California nasogwini.
Izimvula ezibalelwa kumahhafu we-inch, zingadala umonakalo omncane wodoti nemigwaqo eshelelayo
lena koba imvula yokuqala esifundeni njengoba nje kuyisikhathi sazo izimvula.
Ezinye izimvula ezihlakazekile zizoqala ukusondela i-Arizona ntambama ngesonto nasekuseni ngoMsombuluko, ngaphambi kokuba imvula yande ntambama ngoMsombuluko nangolwesibili.
Imvula izosabalala emagumbini amane ngolwesibili kuze kube ngulwesithathuthu.
Enyangeni ka-October sizobona ukushitsha kwamazinga okushisa e-U.S njengoba i-Arctic izobe iya ngokuphola, kodwa izindawo ezingama-Tropics zizofudumala.
Ngokuvamile lokhu kubangela ukushintsha emazingeni okushisa ngesikhathi esincane.
Kunesibonelo esihle samadkingozi ekushintsheni kwamazinga okushisa ezindaweni eziphakathi e U.S ngesonto.
Kunomahluko ka 20-degrees emazingeni okushisa phajathi kwe- Kansas City, Missouri, and Omaha, Nebraska, naphakathi kwe-St. Louis ne Des Moines, Iowa.
Ezinsukwini ezilandelayo ihlobo elibala ukufudumala lizozama ukwakheka lande futhi.
Phakathi ne U.S nase Mpumalanga kulindeleke ukubonakala koqala kwa-October nokufudumala kuka- 80s kusukela ezinkangala zaseNingizimu kuya enyakatho.
e-New York City kulindeleke ukuba ifinyelele emazingeni ka- 80 degrees ngolwesibili okobe kusho ukuthi ibe ngaphezulu ngo 10 degrees kwavamile .
abahloli bethu bezemvelo bathe lokhu kubinise ukuthi amazinga azokhuphuka ezindaweni zasempumalanga .

uKavanaugh,enikeza ubufakazi  enkantolo,uthe naye uqiniseka ngokuphelele ukuthi akwenzekanga lutho.
Ngokombiko wakwa-Nielsen bangaphezu kwa 20.4 million abantu abababukela .
lombiko uvele enkampanini ebibalala ababukeli ku- CBS, ABC, NBC, CNN, Fox News Channel naku MSNBC.
Figuresa amanye amanani awasheshanga ukutholakala kuziteshi ebizisakaza kubawa i-  PBS, C-SPAN ne  the Fox Business Network.
futhu u-Nielsen ngokuvamile uyaye ubhekanane nenselele ekubaleni inani  lababukele besemahhovisi abo.
ukuze basivezele indlela ababona ngayo, ukuthi inani labantu lithi alilingane nelabazo bukela umdlalo webhola noma abaze kumiklonyeliswo .
i-Fox News Channel,enomqondisi onombono ovuna u- Kavanaugh,okuye kwaholela ekutheni zonke iziteshi zibe nababukeli besilinganiso sika 5.69 million  lonke usuku lwecala ,ngokusho kuka - Nielsen.
i-ABC ibe sendaweni yesibili ngababukeli abangu- 3.26 million .
i-CBS yona ibe nenani la  3.1 million,i- NBC yona ibeno- 2.94 million,i- MSNBC yona ibe no 2.89 million kwathi i-CNN yabano 2.52 million, ngokusho kwe-Nielsen.
Ukulangazelelwa kokufuna ukwazi kusaqhubeka kuphezulu ngemva kwecala.
u-Flake uyena obebhekwe ngabomvu kwidrama ebengolwesihlanu .
Ngemva kokukhishwa isitatimende esimayelana nokuvotelwa uhlangothi lwa-Kavanaugh,uye wabanjwa amakhamera ase-  CNN nawase  CBS ngolwesihlanu ekseni ngenkathi ememezwa isixuku ngesikhathi ezama ukugibela ikheshi elizomyisa phambi kwejaji .
Esakazwa bukhoma yisiteshi sa-CNN,uye wama wabhekisa amehlo phansi okwesikhashana eshaywa amahloni.
"Nimi lapha phambi kwakho," kwaso omunye wesifazane .
"Ucabanga ukuthi ukhuluma iqiniso phambi kwezwe?
Watshelwa, "Unamandla uma iningi labesifazane lingenamandla.""
uFlake wathi ihhovisi lakhe lakhipha isistatimende wabe esethi ,ngaphambi kokuba ikheshi livaleke ,wathi unokuningi kokukusho phambi kwenkantolo .
Zisebenzisa izintambo iziteshi ziye zasakaza icala ,lapho kuye kwafika isikhathi sokuba ijaji livotele ukukululwa kuka Kavanaugh.
Kodwa ke u Flake utheuzokwenza lokho kuphela uma eseqonda ukuthi I- FBI ibheke zonke izinhlangothi zaloludaba ngeviki elizayo,lokho okukade kufunwa intando yeniningi.
u-Flake uye washintsha umqondo umngani wakhe ngenkathi bexoxa nomngane wakhe , Democratic Sen. Chris Coons.

Inqaku lika Menga liwinise iLivingston ngo 1-0 idlala ne Rangers
Inqaku lika Dolly Mega lokuqala linqobise iLivingston
ILivingston esanda kunyuswa imangaze iRanger ka Steven Gerrard ukuthi yamukela ukuhlulwa kwayo kwesibili emva kwemidlalo engu-18 njengo mqeqeshi we qembu Ibrox.
Inqaku lika Menga libe ngumehluko njengo iqembu lika Gary Holt li linyuke la lingana, ihibernian yalala isibili.
Iqembu lika Gerrard alika nqobi ekuhambeni kwi premiership kule sizini futhi bayohlangana ne Hearts esecongweni, ebashiya ngamaphuzu ayisishiyangalombili ngomgqibelo.
Ngaphambi kwalokhu, iRangers yamukela iRapid Vienna kwi Europa League ngo lwesine.
Okwamanje iLivingston ayikahlulwa emidlalweni ewu 6, njengoba umqeqeshi uHolt eqhubeka engahlulwa kusukela avala isikhala sika Kenny Miller ngenyanga edlule.
iLivingston ishwebe ithuba lapho ibambeni nezivakashi ezibuthuntu
Iqembu lika Holt funeka ngabe libephambili kakhulu phambi kokuba bakore, ukuqonda kwabo kubangele inkinga eziningi iRangers.
U Scott Robinson uthole ithuba kodwa wahluleka ukushaya inqaku eseqondene ne pali, kwase Allan Lithgow phasela Craig Halkett wailishaya ngekhanda washweba.
Omkhaya bebekhulekile ukudedela iRanger idlale phambi kwabo, ngoba bazi ukuthi bangahlukuzema ngama-set piece.
Futhi kwaba iyona indlela iqhaku eliseqoka eliqhamuke ngalo.
iRangers yenze ifree-kick kwase Livingston yathola elokuvula iqhaku, u Declan Gallagher no Robinson bahlanganise uMenga, uthinte ibhola wafaka inqaku esephakathi nebhokisi.
Ngalesokhathi, iRangers ibiphethe umdlalo kodwa bekungadluleki kuba dlali base mumva futhi nozinti Liam Kelly ubezimele,
Le phethini iqhubekile kwisiwombe sesibili, noma u Alfredo Moralose ezamile ukuthi uKelly ichithe ibhola.
UScott Pitmtman uvinjelwe inyawo zika nozinti we Rangers u Allan McGregor futhi Lithgow ushiye ibhola kwenye iset play ye Livingston.
Ama-cross eze elandelana ebhokisini le Livingston kodwa ilibe esuswa, kube khona izimangalo zama phenathi – emva kwalokho Halkett udlalise kabi uGlenn Middleton, futhi ibola lishaye esandle- konke kwachithwa.
‘Kuhle’ okwenziwa iLivingston- Mhlaziyi
Alasdair Lamont wakwa BBC Scotland e Tony Macaroni Arena
Umdlalo umuhle nemiphumela kwi Livingston.
Ukumuntu nje, bedlale kahle, bayaqhubeka ukudlula obekulindelekile njengoba beqhubeka benyuka.
Indlela yabo yokudlala noqobo lwabo alukashintshi kusukela bebuyile kwiligi, kodwa kumele sincome u Holt ngendlela alipheke ngalo iqembu kusekela efika.
Ube namaqhawe amaningi.
Kapteni Halkett ubevelele, odonga lwakhe uliqinile, ngenkathi uMenga egcine u Conn or Goldon no Joe Worroll bemincile umdlalo wonke.
iRangers ibishoda ngogqozu, kodwa.
Noma benza kahle ngaphansi kuka Gerrard, bashodile ngokugcina lawo mazinga.
Ambhola abo okugcina abe shoda- Uma sebelivulile iqhembu lase khaya – iRangers kumele ivuke emaqandeni, njengoba bezithola maphakathi ne tafula.
uErdogan uthole ukwamukelwa okuxubile eCologne
Bekumamathekwa futhi sbhakabhaka siluhlaza ngo Mgqibelo(umdulmo 29) njengoba umhholi wase Turkey nase Germany behlangane eBerlin kusidlo sasekuseni.
Usuku lokugcina lo hambo oludabuzekwayo luka mongameli Erdogan eGermay – Ehlose ukulungise ubudlelwano phakathi kwe NATO nabahlobo bayo.
Kube khona ukungabonisani mayelana nezinkinga njengama lungelo abantu, inkululeko yezintatheli kanye nokuphuma kwe Turkey kwi EU.
uErdogan uzosuka aye eCologne eyovula imosque enkulu entsha.
Leli dolobha liyakhaya kubantu abaningi abadabuka eTurkey ngaphandle kwese Turkey.
Amaphoyise ombe izimo zokuphepha njengoba bevimbe abantu abaningi abangu 25,000 ukuthi bame phambi kwe mosque, kodwa baningi abalendeli abathekile eduze kuzobona umongameli wabo.
Inkulungwane zabhikishi abangahambisani Erdogan- baningi babo ama kurdish- futhi bafuna kuthi amazwi abo zwiwe, ecitha emthetho ka Erdogan kanye no hulumeni wase Germany ngoku mamukela kulelazwe.
Le mbikhisho ikhombisa ukwehlukana phakathi kwemibono nge sivakashi esibonakal siyiqhawe kuma German Turks futhi njengo ndlovukayiphikiswa kwabanye.

Isiphepho Rosa ihlasela iPhoenix, Las Vegas, Salt Lake City hambisana nezikhukhula(Izindawo ezinesomiso ziyohlomula)
Akujwayelekile ukuthi isishingishane sihlasele e Arizona, kodwa ilokho ekuzokwenzeka ekuqaleni kwesonto nge sonto elizayo njengoba amandla ka Hurricane Rosa Eqhubeka esondela ogwadule eNingizimu-ntshonalanga, Uletha izingozi zezikhukhula.
Izangoma zezulu sezoikhiphe isexwayiso ukuthi niqaphe izikhukhula ngo Msombuluko nango Lwesibili e Ntshonalanga Arizona ukuya eningizimu kanye empumalanga Nevada, eningizimu-mpumalanga Carlifornia and Utah, kubalwa amadolobha ase Phoenix, Flagstaff, Las Vegas, and Salt Lake City.
Rosa ulindekele ukuthi athathe indlela phezu kwe Phoenix ngo Lwesibili, eza ngo Msobuluko ne mvula.
Izangoma zezulu ePhoenix bathe ku ngomyalezo ka Twitter ukuthi “Izishingishane iziyishumi kuphela ezagcina ziyisi shingishane ngaphakathi kwamakhilomitha awu 200 e Phoenix kusukela ngo 1950!
UKatrina(1967) waye siphepho ngaphakhathi kwamakhilomitha awu 40 nakumzila wase AZ”.
I National Hurricane Center ibikezela 2 kuya 4 amasentimitha emvul, ehambisana namanani awu 6 amasentimitha kwi Mogollan Rim e Arizona.
Kwezinye indawo zogwadule eNingizimu-ntshonalanga kubalwa maphakathine Rockies kanye ne Great Basin zilindekele ukuthi zithole amasentimitha awu 1 to 2, maseziphelele kunga baliselwa ku masentimitha angu 4 umakwenzeka.
Ngalezo zingozi zezi khukhula, u Rosa angahle abe isibusiso njengoba ingxenye ihlaselwe isomiso.
Noma izikhukhula ziyingozi kakhulu, enye yemvula uzoba isimvuzo ngoba eNingizimu-ntshonalanga ihlaselwe isomiso.
Ngokwe U.S Drougth Monitor( babheka izomiso), amaphesenti angu 40 we Arizona ahlaselwe isomiso, ekwiyona eyisibili enkulu ohlwini, weather.com ibikile.
Okukuqala, isiphepho uRosa ezodlula phambi kwe Baja California peninsula of Mexico.
Rosa, Usanawo amandla esiphepho ngeSonto ekuseni njengoba hamba ngesivinini sama khilomitha angu 85 nge hora, 385 wamakhilomitha eningizimu ne Punta Eugenia, eMexico futhi nyukela enyakatho ngesivinini esingu 12 wakhilomitha nge hora.
Isiphepho sisondela ngase manzini apholile kwi Pacific futhi ngalokho lindekele ukuthi yehla amandla.
Ngakho ke, silindelekile ukuthi siwele eMexico sesiyisiphepho esishisayo esinamandla ntambama noma ngo Msombuluko.
Imvula kwidlanzana lezindawo e Mexico ingaba nkulu, ingadala umonakalo ngezikhukhula.
Imvula ihlanga kusukaku 3 kuya 6 wamasentimitha Baja California iyakwi nyakatho-ntshonalanga Sonara, nama sentimitha awu 10 angezeka,”weather.com reported.
Rosa uzobe esanyukela enyakatho phesheya njenge sphepho ngaphambi kokuba afike emzileni wase Arizona ngezikhathi zasekuseni ngilwesibili eshingishane, izonyuka idlule e Arizona futhi ingene nase ningizimu Utah ngezikhathi zasebusuku ngolwesibili.
Ubungozi obukhulu obulindelekile obungadalwa uRosa noma akushiyayo imvula enamandla e Baja California, inyakatho-ntshonalanga Sonara, nase U.S. Ugwadule Southwest, “ kusho abakwa National Hurricane Cente.r
Lezi zimvula kulindeleke ukuthi ziveze izikhukhula ezihamba nomphefumulo kanye nezinhlayiya ezigeleza ezikhungweni, nasezindaweni eziphakeme zezintaba.

Amakhulu abulewe ukuzazama komhlaba, tsunami, inani liyakhuphuka
Kushone okungenani abantu abangu -384, abaningi bagugulwe ngamagagasi amakhulu ngenkathi ehlasele amabhisi, ngenkathi kuzamazama umhlaba ne tsunami ishaya kwi sqingi sase Indonesian sase Sulawesi, kusho izikhulu ngomgqibelo.
Amakhulu abantu ayebuthene emcimbini ogwini edolobheni lasePalu ngoLwesihlanu lapho amagagasi aphakeme ngamamitha angu-18 ehlaselwa osebeni ngehora lesishiyagalolunye, ebulala abaningi ekufeni kwabo futhi ebhubhisa noma yini endleleni.
I-tsunami yalandela ukuzamazama komhlaba okungamamitha angu-7.5.
"Ngesikhathi usongo lwama-tsunami luvela ngoLwesine, abantu babesenza imisebenzi yabo ogwini futhi abazange baphuthume ngokushesha futhi baba yizisulu," kusho uSutopo Purwo Nugroho, okhulumela i-Indonesia, ekuhlaseleni izinhlekelele eBNPB.
"I-tsunami ayizange ifike yodwa, yahudula izimoto, izingodo, izindlu, zishaya yonke into emhlabathini," kusho Nugroho, wanezela ukuthi i-tsunami yayidabula ulwandle oluvulekile ngesivinini esingu-800 kph (497 mph) ngaphambi kokushaya ezihlabathini.
Abanye bantu bagibele ezihlahleni bebalekela I-Tsunami, esho.
Abantu abangaba ngu-17 700 bahanjiswa ezikhungweni angu-24 ePalu.
Izithombe ezithathwe ibhanoyi ezikhishwe isikhungo sezenhlekelele zabonisa izakhiwo eziningi nezitolo zabhubha, amabhuloho abhidlika futhi adiliza kanye nomsikashi owazungezwe ngamanzi.
Ukuzamazama kuqhubekile ukunyakazisa idolobha elisogwini umgqibelo wonke.
Uchungechunge lokuzamazama komhlaba kwakuziwa endaweni enezigidi ezingu-2.4 zabantu.
I-Indonesia's Agency for the Assessment and Application of Technology (BPPT) ithi isitatimende amandla akhishwe ukuzamazama okulukazi ngoLwesihlanu yayingamaphesenti angu-200 amandla ebhomu le-athomu awela eHiroshima eMpini Yezwe II. .
I-geography yedolobha, ehlezi ekupheleni kwesigamu eside, esincane, kungenzeka sikhulise ubukhulu be-tsunami, besho.
U-Nugroho wachaze umonakalo onjengokuthi "inkulu" futhi wathi izinkulungwane zezindlu, izibhedlela, izindawo zokuthenga ezitolo kanye namahhotela awile.
Amalungu ezinye izisulu zitholakale evaleleke ngaphansi kwesigubhu sezakhiwo ezidilikile, uthe, enenezela abantu abangu-540 balimele kwathi abangu-29 bashona.
U-Nugroho uthe labo abalimalayo kanye nomonakalo kungenzeka ube mkhulu ngasogwini olungamakhilomitha angama-300 enyakatho yePalu, indawo ebizwa ngokuthi i-Donggala, esiseduze ne-epicenter ye-quake.
Ukuxhumana “ sikhahlamezekile asinalo ulwazi” ulusuka Donggala, Kusho Nugroho.

Kuthiwa, “Lokhu kakade sekuwusizi kodwa kusengenyuka kunalokhu.”

U.S kumele inyuse uxhaso lwe A.I.
Njengoba i-China isebenza ngokwengeziwe kwi I.A, i-U.S. kufanele iphinde kabili inani elisebenzisayo ucwaningo emkhakheni, kusho umtshali-zimali no-AI, uKai-Fu Lee, osebenzele i-Google, i-Microsoft ne-Apple.
Amazwana avela emva kwezinhlangothi ezehlukene zombuso wase-U.S. wenze smemezelo e-AI, njengoba nje jikelele we-U.S. ingekho isu elihlelekile le-AI.
Phakathi naleso sikhathi, i-China yaqalisa uhlelo layo ngonyaka odlule: ihlose ukuba u numba .1 ku-AI  ngo-2030.
"Isabelomali sokucwaninga nge-AI sizoba yisiqalo esihle, ngoba nje wonke amanye amazwe asekude kakhulu ngemuva kwe-U.S., futhi sifuna ukuphumelela okulandelayo ku-AI," kusho uLee.
Ukuphikisana nokuxhaswa kwemali kungaphindaphinda amathuba okuba kwenziwe ukufezeka okukhulu kwe-AI e-U.S., u-Lee utshele i-CNBC ekuxoxweni kuleli sonto.
Lee, incwadi yakhe ethi "AI Superpowers:   I-China, i-Silicon Valley ne-New World Order "yashicilelwa kule nyanga nguHoughton Mifflin Harcourt, Umphathi we-Sinovation Ventures, eyitshale kwenye yezinkampani ezivelele kakhulu ze-AI eChina, Face ++.
Eminyakeni yama-1980s eCarnegie Mellon University wasebenza ohlelweni lwe-AI olusha umdlali wase-Othello waseMelika obala kakhulu, futhi kamuva waba ngumphathi we-Microsoft Research noMongameli wegatsha lase-Google laseChina
U-Lee wavuma ukuncintisana kobuchwepheshe be-U.S. wangaphambilini njengoMnyango wezokuPhepha oPhezulu wezokuPhepha weRobotics Challenge futhi wabuza ukuthi ngabe olandelayo uzoba nini, ukuze asize ukubona izimboni ezilandelayo.
Abacwaningi base-U.S. ngokuvamile kufanele basebenze kanzima ukuze banqobe izibonelelo zikahulumeni, kusho uLee..
"Akusikho iChina esusa abaholi bezemfundo; yizinkampani," kusho u-Lee.
I-Facebook, i-Google nezinye izinkampani zobuchwepheshe zisebenzise izikhanyiso ezivela emanyuvesi ukuze zisebenze ku-AI eminyakeni kamuva.
U-Lee wathi izinguquko zomgomo wokufuduka zingasiza nase-U.S. ukuqinisa imizamo yawo ye-AI.
"Ngicabanga ukuthi amakhadi aluhlaza kufanele ahlinzekwe ngokuzenzakalelayo kuma-PhD ku-AI," usho kanje.
UMkhandlu Wase-China WaseChina ukhiphe Sokuthuthukisa Intuthuko Yenhlakanipho Yomhlahlandlela olandelayo we-Generation Intelligence Intelligence Plan ngoJulayi 2017.
China National Natural Science Foundation ikhiphe imali kubantu ezikhungweni zokufunda ezifana nalendlela i-Nationla Science Foundation nezinye ezikhipha ngayo imali kubacwaningi, kodwa ikhwalithi yomsebenzi wezifundiswa lincane e-China, kusho Lee.
Ekuqaleniu konyaka. Defense Department eisingule i Joint Artificial Intelligence Center, ekumele ihlanganise ophathini bakulo mkhakha kanye nezifundiswa, futhi ne White House imemezele ukwakhiwa kwekomidi elikhethekile le Artificial Intelligence.
Kulenyanga  i-DARPA imemezele $2 billion kuhlelo olubizwa AI Next.
I NSF, itshale ngaphuze kuka $100 million ngonyaka kucwaningo lwe AI .
Kuse njalo, Umthetho wase Melika wokwakha iNational Security Commision nge Artificial Intelligence iyakakabi nomnyakazo.
Abantu base Macedonia bayavota ukuthi balishintshe yini igama lezwe noma cha.
Abantu base Macedonia bavotile nge- Sonto ukuthi bagiuqule igama lezwe libe “Republic of North Macedonia,” isiqhumo esizoxazulula ingxabano nezwe lase Greece eseli vimbe ubulunga be European Union ne NATO.
I-Greece, elibiza Macedonia negsifundazwe sayo, liyaqhubeka lithi omakhelwane babo abasenyakatho komzila wabo bafuna indawo yabo futhi bafuna ukungena kwio NATO and EU.
Ohulumeni bobabili benza ngesivumelwane nge-gama elibhekiwe, kodwa abanye bathi ukushintsha leli gama kusho ukubukela phansi amasiko iningi labantu base Macedonia aba Slavic
Umengameli Gjorge Ivanov uthe ngeke avote futhi ukubhikisha ukuvota kwenza kube manqikanqika ukuthi 50 percent wabantu bazofika kuze loluketho lube semthethweni.
Umbuzo kwi phepha lokuvota lifundeka kanje: " Uvumelana nobulungu be NATO ne EU ngesivumelwano se Greece."
Abavumelana nokushintshwa gama, kubalwa Ndunankulu Zoran Zaev, uthi iyona into oyikhokha ngoku vuma izinhlaka izifana ne EU ne Nato kwi Macedonia, amanye amazwe avele ngohlakazeka kwe Yugoslavia
"Ngifikile izolo ukuzovotela kusas lezwe lethu, ukuze intsha yaseMacedonia izophila kahle ngaphansi kwe-umbrella ye-European Union ngoba kuchaza izimpilo zethu zonke ezipheile," kusho u-Olivera Georgijevska, 79, eSkopje.
Noma kungabophi ngokomthetho, amalunga anele ephalamende bathe isinqumo sevoti bazosamukela.
Ushintsho uzodinga izinxenye ezimbili kwezintantathu ukudla umhlanganio ephalamende.
Ikhomishane yokuvota yezwe ithi ibingekho imibiko ebikiwe yokungahambisani ngo 1 p.m.
Kodwa, ibisolokhu iku 16 percent, kuno 34 percent wokuvota okwedlule kwasephalamende ngo 2016 ngenkathi  66 percent wabavotiababhalisile befaka amavoti abo.
"Ngiphumile ukuzovota ngenxa yezingane zami, indawo yethu e-Europe," kusho uGjose Tanevski, 62, umvoti kwidolobha, Skopje.
I-PM yaseMacedonia uZoran Zaev, umkakhe uZorica nendodana yakhe uDushko bavotele ireferendum eMacedonia ngokushintsha igama lezwe elizovula indlela ukujoyina iNATO  neEuropean Union eStrumica, eMacedonia Septhemba 30, 2018.
Phambikwephalamende eSkopje, uVladimir Kavardarkov, 54, belungisa isigcawu futhi edonsanezihlalo phambi kwamatendeabekwe yilabo abazomelana nereferendum.
"Singabe NATO ne EU, kodwa sifuna ukujoyina simise amakhanda, hhayi ngomnyango wesevisi" kusho Kavadarkov.
"Siyizwe elimpofu, kodwa sinesidima.
Uma bengafuni ukusamukela njengabase Macedonia, singaguqula abanye njenge China ne Russia futhi baba ingxenye yase Euro-Asia integration."
Prime Minister Zaev uthi ubulungu be-NATO buzoletha ukutshalwa kwemali okudingekayo eMacedonia, enesilinganiso sabantu abangasebenzi abangaphezu kuka 20 percent.
"Ngikholelwa ukuthi iningi elingu 80 percent wezakhamuzi zethu lizochema ne-EU ne NATO,"  kusho uZaev emva kokufaka ivoti.
Uthe "yebo" imiphumela "ukuqinisekiswa kwekusasa lethu."
Ipholi mgomsombuluko washicilelwa eMacedonia's Institute for Policy Research uthe phakathi kuka 30 no 43 percent wabavoti ukuba uhlanganyele – ngaphansi kokulindelwe.
Enye ipholi, ephethwe iMacedonia's Telma TV, ithole 57 percent wabaphendulayo abahlele ukuvota ngeSonto.
Kulabo, 70 percent uthi uvota yebo.
Ukuze ireferendum ibeimpumelelo abezayo mele babe 50 percent nevoti elilodwa.
A Ukwahluleka ireferendum kuzoveza unkinga enkulu yepro-Western government lokhu yathatha isikhathi eside ngoMay nyakenye.

Sibe nenhlanhla ngokuthi akore igoli kuso leso sikhashana.”
Kodwa kube yi-Sterling enike i-Sky Blues ithuba ekuqaleni komzuliswano we-Premiere League.

Iqembu Labasebenzi akuselona ibandla lanoma ubani.
Alisabameli abakhuluma okusemiqondweni yabo.
Lapho izishoshovu zakwa-Momentum eqenjini langakithi zivotela ukungivala umlomo, angimangalanga nakancane.
Kodwa vele, sengingene kamuva ohideni lwama-MP eqembu Labasebenzi abatshelwe ukuthi abamukelekile - ngenxa nje yokukhuluma okusemicabangweni yethu.
Uzakwethu wasePhalamende u-Joan Ryan uthole ukuphathwa okucishe kufane ngenxa yokumelana nabamelene nama-Semitic.
Odabeni lwami ke, abafuna ukuthi ngivalwe umlomo bangigxeka ngenxa yokungavumelani no-Jeremy Corbyn.
Ephuzwini lokubaluleka lohlelo lwezimali olucatshangelwe, ekuphepheni kwesizwe, kwi-Yurophu, nakwezinye izinto okumangazayo u-Jeremy asehilizisane ngazo nabanye abaholi ngaphambilini.
Esazisweni seqembu Labasebenzi base-Nottingham East somhlangano wango-Lwesihlanu sithi “sifuna imihlangano ingabandlululi futhi izuzise.”
Cishe kuyoyonke imnyaka eyisishagalombili ngiyi-MP yeqembu Labasebenzi langakithi, imihlangano ye-GC ya go-Lwesihlanu eb'suku ibilokhu iyiloko nje.
Ngokudabukisayo nam’hlanje, akuhambi njengemihlangano yasemihleni futhi isithembiso sepolitiki “ezwelayo, nemnene” sekwakhohlwa kudala uma, ngempela, sake sabakhona.
Sekuya ngokuya kucaca ukuthi imibono eyahlukene ayisavumelekile eqenjini Labasebenzi nanokuthi imibono yahlulelwa ngokuthi yamukelekile yini kubaholi beqembu.
Loku kuqale ngemva nje kokuthi u-Jeremy abe umholi, nakozakwethu ebengithi sinemibono efanayo yezepolitiki nabo sebebheke ukuthi ngijike ngithathe izinhlangothi ebengingeke ngivumelane nazo - kungakhathaliseki ukuthi ezokuphepha kwesizwe noma esemakethe engayodwana ye-EU.
Noma yinini lapho ngikhuluma emphakathini - akusabalulekile nokuthi ngithini - kuzoza igagasi lokuhlukunyezwa ezingosini zokuxhumana lithi angikhishwe, lichitha ipolitiki engachemile, lithi akumelwe ngibe seqenjini Labasebenzi.
Futhi akusimina kuphela osebhekene nalokhu.
Nakanjani, ngiyazi ukuthi ngibe nenhlanhla kunozakwethu ngoba izinkulumo ezibhekiselwe k’mina zisathanda ukuba ngepolitiki.
Ngisamangele ekutheni labozakwethu basayibambile em’sebenzini nasekuzimiseleni kwabo bangazinyezi yize bebhekene nokucwasa okungokobulili noma okobuhlanga.
Enye yezinto ezidikibalisa kakhulu kulenkathi yezepolitiki indlela amazinga okuhlukumeza asevele abangajwayelekile.
Jeremy Corbyn wathi ngeviki eliphelile i-Labour party kumelwe ibeke isiko lwemingcele.
Iqiniso liwukuthi asisasliona leli sonto elikhulu futhi engazethembi noma ukushintsha kwemithetho yokutomula iqembu liya lincipha.
Benginezeluleko eziningi eminyakeni emibili edlule nginxuswa ukuba ngizehlise, ngingakhulumi kakhulu futhi kuzoba “sengilungile.”
Kodwa akusikhona lokho engikuzele kwezepolitiki.
Selokhu ngazihlangazisa ne-Labour eminyakeni engu-32 edlule njengomfundi, ngacasulwa  uhulumeni Thatcher ngokunganki ngokuthi ashiye amagubi esokole ecekeleke phansi, bengifuna ukuletha izinkonzo zomphakathi ezingcono kakhulu kulabo abazidinga kakhulu – mhlawumbe njengohulumeni wendawo noma njenongqongqoshe kahulumeni.
Angikaze ngizifihle kwezepolitiki, kuhlanganise nasokhethelweni lokugcina.
Akukho muntu e-Nottingham East nganoma iyiphi indlela ongadideka mayelana ngomthetho yokuma kwamia kanye nezindawo zokuphikisana ngobuholi bamanje.
Kulabo abakhutheze uhambo ngoLwesihlanu, konke engingakusho ukuthi lapho izwe liqhubekela phambili kwi- Brexit lokho kuyolimza abaninikhaya, amabhizinisi kanye nenkonzo yethu yomphakathi, angifisi ukuchitha isikhathi kanye namandla ngokuqotho bami kumholi we- Labour party.
Ngempela kodwa munye umyalezo enginawo awuqndile kw-Nottingham Momentum, kwabangikimi, kungaba amalungu e- Labour noma cha: Ngiyaziqenya ngokunikhonza kanti futhi ngiyathembisa ukuthi angeke kube bikho ukusongelwa noma ngokwezepolitiki okuzongivimela ukwenza engikukholelwa ukuthi kuzoba okungcono kini nonke.

Ayr ina-38- 17 Melrose: Ayr engakaze ihlulwe ihlezi phezulu
Ama-tries amibili akamuva ayicezukisile imiphumela yokugcina, kodwa akungatshazwa Ayr iyakufanelekela ukunconywa kulo mdlalo wanamuhla  obe muhle kakhulu  we-Tennent's Premiership.
Manje baphezulu, okuwukupela ohlangothini lwabayishumi abangahlulwa.
Ekugcineni, ukuzivikela kwabo, noma nini amathuba ebavumela, okubeke abasekhaya kanye noqeqeshi Peter Murchie uba nazo zonke izizathu zokujabula.
Uthe,“sivivinywe yonke imidlalo yethu kuze kube manje, futhi asikaze sehlulwe, ngakho kumelwe ngijabule.”
Robyn Christie wase Melrose uthe: “ udumo ku Ayr, basebenzise wonke amathuba ukwedlula thina.”
I-try yemizuzu engu-14 ka Grant Anderson ifakwe ngu- Frazier Climo, ebeka phambili Ayr, kodwa, cap Rory Hughes wesi-soctland uthole ikhadi eliphuzi, yakhululwa emdlalweni Warriors, okubangele Melrose  wazenzela ngamaqaku futhi  Jason Baggot ubambisise wonke ama-try.
Climo ubanagele Ayr yahamba phambili ngepenadi, ngaphambi nje, kwesiwombe sokuqala, ufake i-solo try ukwenza u-17-5 ku Ayr ngekhefu.

‘ulwandle lungolwethu’:abaphathi be-Bolivia bathemba ukuthi inkantolo izovula indlela eya-Pacific
Ababheki babashayeli bezikebhe i- rigging-clad indlunkulu naval e- La Paz.
Izikhiwo zomphakhathi ziphakamisa ifulege ocean-blue.
Naval bases  kusuka Lake Titicaca kuya e-Amazon zinalesi siqubulo: “ulwandle lungwethu ngelungelo
Ukululama kuwumsebenzi wethu.
Kuzo zonke izindawo zase Bolivia, inkumbulo nge-coastline yalahlekela e-Chile ngekhulu lesi-19 umuthombo usacace bha – njengoba kulangazelela ukuya e-Pacific Ocean futhi.
Lawo mathemba mhlawumbe aphezule eminyakeni yakho, Bolivia ilindele ukubuswa yinkantolo yomhlaba wonke yezobulungiswa ngomhlaka-1 Okthoba ngemva kweminyaka emihlanu.
“I-Bolivia inawo Amandla, umoya wobunye kanye nokuzithoba, kanti empeleni iwulindele ngabomvu umuphumela,” kusho Roberto Calzadilla, okhulumela ngokusemthethweni i-Bolivia.
Abaningi e-Bolivia bazobukela ICJ ruling kuma-screens amakhulu kuyo yonke indawo, ngethemba elikhulu lokhuthi inkantolo i- Hague izovuna isikhalo se-Bolivia sokuthi – ngemva kwezinkulumo ezidonse iminyaka –  i-Chile iphoqwe ukuxoxisana ngokunika i-Bolivia ilawule ingxenye yolwandle.
Evo Morales, umongameli ofanelekayo wase- Bolivia – obhekene nomshuduliswano omude ngokhetho-futhi ngonyaka ozayo- unokuningi okusamhlalele ngoMsombuluko.
“ siseduze kakhulu ukubuyeila e-Pacific Ocean," efunga ngasekupheleni kuka-Agasti.
Kodwa abanye abahlaziyibakholwa ukuthi inkantolo mancane amathuba okuvuna i-Bolivia - kanti lelo gama liyoshintsha uma ivuma.
I-Netherlands-isekela indikimba i-UN anawo amandla ukuklomelisa izindawo zase-Chile, igomele ngokuthi angake kunqunywe umphumela wokuphumelela kwezinkulumo.
Ukuthi abe-ICJ ruling beza kuphela ezinyangeni eziyithupha ngemva kwezimpikiswano kwezwakala ukuthi udaba ”belungenzima,” kusho inqapheli yomthetho womhlaba wonke yaseChile, Paz Zárate.
Buqama nasekufezekiseni izinjongo ze-Bolivia, iminyaka emine eyedlule kungenzeka ibahlehlisele emuva.
“Udaba lokuvunyelwa ukusebenzisa ulwandle lungenelelwe ngokungemvume iziphathimandla zaseBolivia,” kusho u-Zarate.
Inkulumo ka-Morales egqugquzela udlame ikhubaza ukubambisana kwelase-Chile, wabeka kanjalo.
I-Bolivia ne-Chile esikhathini esithile bazoqhubeka nezingxoxo, kepha kuyoba nzima kakhulu ukuqhubeka nokubonisana emva kwalokhu.
Amazwe amabili awakashintshisani ngamanxusa kusuka ngonyaka ka 1962.
Owayengumongameli u-Eduardo Rodriguez Veltze, omele elase-Bolivia e-Hague uzichithile izinsolo zokuthi inkantolo isheshe kakhulu ukuthatha isinqumo.
U-Msombuluko uzolethela I-Bolivia “ithuba eliyingqayizivele lokuqala isikhathi esisha sobudlelwane ne-Chile” kanye nethuba “ lokumisa iminyaka engama 139 yokungavumelani ngezinto ezizozuzisa lamazwe omabili”, ubeke kanjalo.
u-Calzidilla futhi uyakuphika ukuthi uMorales – osengomunye womongameli abadumile e-Melika yama-Latin – wasebenzisa udaba lwezasolwandle njengesisekelo kwezombusazwe.
“I-Bolivia ayisoze yalahla ilungulelo layo lokusebenzisa ulwandle i-Pacific Ocean.” Usho kanjalo
“Isinqumo siyithuba lokuthi kubonakale ukuthi sidinga ukunqoba osekwadlula.”
i-North Korea ithi ukuyekiswa ukuhloma ngezikhali zenuzi ngeke kwenzeke ngaphandle uma izokwazi ukuthemba elase-Melika.
Ungqongqoshe wezangaphandle e-North Korea u-Ri Yong Ho uthi izwe lakhe angeke liyeke ukuhloma ngezikhali zenuzi kuqala ngaphandle kokuthi bathembe i-Washington.
u-Ri ubekhuluma ngoMgqibelo kwingungquthela yamazwe abumbene.
Unxuse i-Melika ukuthi ilandele izithembiso zayo eyazenza kwingqungquthela ese-Singapore eyayiphakathi kwabaholi abayizimbangi.
Ukuphawula kwakhe kuze ngesikhathi i-Melika. Unobhala wezwe u-Mike Pompeo ubukeka esengcupheni yokuqala udaba olungaxazululeki lwenuzi emva kwezinyanga ezintathu iSingapore no-Kim Jon Un wase-North Korea.
u-Ri uthi kuyiphupho elingefezeke ukuthi unswinyo oluqhubekayo nokunqaba kwe-U.S. kwisivumelwano esiqeda impi kwelase-Korea ukuthi koke kwenze iNorth Korea iguqe.
i-Washington iwayaqaphelisisa ukuthi ingavumi ukwenza izimemezelo i-Pyongyang ingakaqali ukushabalalisa izikhali zayo.
Bobabili Kim ne U.S. /Melika  Umongameli uDonald Trump udinga ingqungquthela yesibili.
Kodwa ke kunokusabalala kongabazane lokuthi i-Pyongyang izimisele ngokuyeka izikhali izwe okungenzeka lizibuka njengayona ndlela kuphela yokuphepha.
u-Pompeo uhlela ukuvakashela e-Pyongyang ngenyanga ezayo ukulungiselela ingqungquthela yesibili ka Kim no Trump.
Imfashini yase-Paris ikhombisa okuningi okugqokwa ekhanda okuza ezitolo zezingubo eziseduze nawe
Uma ufuna ukwandisa uhlu lwezigqoko zakho noma uvele uvimbe ilanga ngokuphelele ungabe usabheka kude.
Abathungi u-Valentino no-Thom Browne baveze uhlu lwezigqoko ezinkulu zasekhanda kumgodla wabo i-SS19 kumbukiso obukwi-Paris Fashion Week.
Izigqoko ezingakholeki zigcwale kwi-Instagram kulelihlobo, futhi labathungi balethe imibukiso edonsa amehlo.
Okugqamile kokuka-Valentino bekuyigqoko eside emacaleni esiluthuthu esihlebe ngezimpaphe nomhelane owengamele ikhanda lombukisi wengqephu.
Ezinye zezinto ezongosayizi abakhulu zibandakanya amakhabe anamatshe ayigugu, isigqoko sabathakathi.
u-Thom Browne uveze izifihli zobuso ezingavamile esikhathini se Halloween.
Izinto eziningi zokufihla ubuso zivalekile emlonyeni zibukeka njengo-Hannibal Lecter kunokubukeka njengento eyakhiwe abathungi bengqephu abaphambili.
Enye into eyakhiwe ifana nezingubo zokutshuza ngaphansi kwamanzi inento yokuphefumula kanye nezibuko.
Uma uqhubeka nemfashini engadumile ungazibeka enhlanhleni.
Ababuki besitayela baqagula ukuthi izigqoko ezinkulu kungenzeka ukube zisendleleni eya emigaqeni emikhulu enezitolo zezimpahla.
Isigqoko esikhulukazi silandele maduze I ‘La Bomba’, isigqoko esiwumhelane esingalingana izinyawo ezimbili ukuvuleka kulokhu okusitha ilanga, esibonakale kwi “everyone” ka Rihanna kuya ku Emily Ratajkowski.
Uphawu lwenkolo oluyisisekelo sesigqoko esingakholakali esidume emakhasini ezokuxhumana sithumele ezinye izimpahla kumbukiso- isikhwama sasolwandle esicishe silingane nesudi yokubhukuda besikhonjiswa umbukisi omodelayo.
Isikhwama esisaorintshi elishile esakhiwe ngesihlahla rafiya, saphethwa ngerafiya, sagqokiswa isikhumba esimhlophe esibambweni, besizihambela sodwa kumbukiso we-Jacquemus’ La Riviera SS19 kumbukiso wemfashini e-Paris.
Umgqokisi wosaziwayo uLuke Armitage utshele i-FEMAIL  ‘Ngilindele ukubona izigqoko ezinkulu nezikhwama zasolwandle zifika ezitolo ezisemigaqweni emikhulu kulelihlobo elizayo-njengoba abathungi bebe nomthelela omkhulu kuzobanzima ukuziba isidingo sokwenza izinto ezithe xaxa ngokwesikali.’
u-John Edward: Ikhono kwezolimu libalulekile kwizakhamuzi ezwenikazi.
Izikole ezizimele eScotland zigcina imininingwane yemiphumela emihle, futhi lokhu kuqhubekile ngonyaka ka-2018 ngeminye imiphumela yokuhlolwa emihle, eqinisekiswa kuphela ukuphumelela komuntu eyedwa kanye nozakwabo kwezemidlalo, ezobuciko, ezomculo, neminye imizamo yomphakathi.
Ngesibalo esinykayo sabafundi esingamashumi amathathu ezinkulungwane e-Scotland, lezizikolezimelwe iScottish Council of Independent Schools (SCIS), ziphokophelela ekuletheni usizo oluseqophelweni eliphezulu.
Izikole ezizimele zihlose ukulungiselela abafundi ekungeneni ezingeni eliphezulu lemfundo, nasemkhakheni abayikhethayo nasendaweni njengezakhamuzi ezweni.
Njengemnyango wezemfundo ongahlela futhi uqalise uhlelo lwemfundo olukhethekile, sibona izilimu zesimanje ziqhubeka ziba ulimu oludumile futhi oluthandwayo njengesifundo esikhethile ezikoleni.
uNelson Mandela wathi: “uma ukhuluma nendoda ngolimu eluzwayo, lokho okushoyo kuya ngqo ekhanda lakhe”
Uma ukhuluma naye ngolimu lwakhe lokhu okushoyo kuya enhliziyweni.”
Lesi isikhumbuzo esinamandla sokuthi ngeke sathembela kwiSingisi njalo uma sifuna ukwakha ubudlelwano nokuthembana nabanttu bakwamanye amazwe.
Kusuka kwimiphumela yokukuhlolwa yezivivinyo zalonyaka, singabona ukuthi ezolimu izona eziphambili eqhulwini kuphunyelelwa kuzona kakhulu ezikoleni ezizimele.
Bangamashumi ayisthupha nesishiyagalombili sebebebonke abafundi abafunde izilimu zangaphandle bathola Isigaba Esiphezulu kuka-A.
Izinkomba, eziqoqwe ezikoleni ezingamashumi ayisikhombisa nane ezingamalungu ka-SCIS, zikhombisa ukuthi amaphesenti angamashumi ayisikhombisa nambili abafundi bathole Isigaba Esiphezulu A kwi-Mandarin, ekubeni abanye abangamaphesenti angamashumi ayisikhombisa nambili abafunda isiJalimane, abamaphesenti amashumi ayisithupha nesishiyagalolunye  bethole  balabo bafunda isiFrench aabanye abangamaphesenti angamashumi ayisithupha nantathu bafunda i-Spanish nabo bathole o-A.
Lokhu kukhombisa ukuthi izikole ezizimele e-Scotland zigqugquzela izilimi zamazwe angaphandle njengamakhono abalulekile ezinganeni, abantu abasha ekungangabazeki bazozidinga esikhathini esizayo.
Ulimu manje njengesifundo ongakhetha kuso, luthathwa njengokufanayo nezifundo eziwungqaphambili (isayensi, ubuchwepheshe, ezonjiniyela, nezibalo) ezikoleni ezimele ohlelweni lwezifundo nakwenye indawo.
Ucwaningo olwenziwe i-UK Commission for Employmeny and Skills ngonyaka ka 2014 ithole ukuthi izizathu abaqashi  bengakwazi ukuvala izikhala eziyishumi nesikhombisa lamaphesenti (17 per cent) kwenziwe ukushoda kwamakhono okusebenzisa izilimi.
Ngakhoke ikakhulu, ikhono lwezilimi luya ngokubaluleka ekulungiseleni intsha kwezamathuba omsebenzi.
Ngemisebenzi eminingi elindelekile endinga izilimi, lamakhono abalulekile ezweni elibumbene.
Nomangabe umuntu uthatha muphi umkhakha, uma befunda ulimu lwesibili, bazibeka ethubeni elingcono ekusaseni labo ekubeni nekhono elinjenganaleli.
Ukukwazi ukukhuluma ngqo nabantu abasuka emazweni angaphandle kubeka umuntu okwazi ukukhuluma izilimu eziningi phambili kulabo aqhudelana nabo.
Ngokocwaningo lwase-YouGov lwabantu abadala abangaphezu kwezinkulungwane ezine (4000) base-UK ngonyaka ka 2013, abangama shumi ayisikhombisa nanhlanu (75) wamaphesenti babengakwazi ukukhuluma kahle ulimu lwakwamanye amazwe angaphandle nokuba nengxoxo kahle futhi isiFrench siwulona limu kuphela olukhulwa abantu anagamaphesenti enziwa izinombolo ezimbili, ishumi nanhlanu (15) lamaphesenti.
Ingakho ukutshala kwezokufundiswa kwezilimu kubalulekile ezinganeni zanamuhla.
Ukuba nezilimu eziningi ozaziyo, ikakhulu lezo zamazwe asathuthuka, kuyosiza ekucijiseni izingane ngamathuba angconono okuthola umsebenzi ongcono.
E-Scotland, isikole nesikole siyahluka olimini olusifundisayo.
Iningi lezikole zigxila ekufundiseni ikakhulu izilimu ezindala nezamanje, kanti ezinye zifundisa izilimu ezithathwa njengezibaluleke kakhulu e-UK uma kubhekwa ngale konyaka ka 2020, njenge-Mandarin ne-Japanese.
Noma ngabe yini ingane yakho ekuthandayo, kunezinhlobo eziningi zezilimu ongakhetha kuzo ezikoleni ezizimele, nothisa abangongoti kulendawo.
Izikole ezizimele zase-Scotland zizibophezele ekunikeni isimo sezemfundo esizolungisela izingane futhi zicije izingane ngamakhono adingeka ukuthi ziphumelele, kulokhu ikusasa elikuphethe.
Kungephikwe esikhathini samanje, kwezamabhizinisi emhlabeni wonke jikelele ukuthi izilimu zizoqhubeka nokubaluleka kwikusasa lezwe, ngakho lokhu mele kuvezwe kwezemfundo.
Empeleni, izilimu zesimanje kumele zibandakanywe “kumakhono ezokuxhumana kwemhlaba wonke jikelele.”
Izikole ezizimele zizoqhubeka nokunikezela ngalelithuba, ukuhluka, nobungoti kubantu baseScotland abasebancane.
Kumele ukwenze kahle.
u-John Edward ungumqondisi we-Scottish Council of Independent Schools.
u-Lebron uzodlala umdlalo wakhe wokuqala kwi-Lakers nge-Sonto e-San Diego
Sekuseduze kuphele ukulinda kubalandeli abalindele ukubona u-Lebron James edlala umdlalo wakhe wokuqala we-Los Angeles Lakers.
U-Luke Walkon ongumqeqeshi umemezele ukuthi u-James uzodlala ngesonto emdlalweni wokuzilungeselela ukuqala kwemidlalo yesizini, bazodlala ne-Denver Nuggets e-San Diego.
Kodwa ke, ekutheni mingaki imizuzu azoyidlala kusazonqunya.
“Kuzoba ngaphezulu kowodwa ibe ngaphansi kwengamashumi amabili nesishiyagalombili,” kusho u Walton ekhasini leLakers.
Intatheli ye-Lakers u-Mike Trudell ubike ku-Twitter ukuthi u-James maningi amathuba okuthi adlale imizuzu efinyeziwe.
Emva kokuzilolonga kulelisonto, u-James ube esebuzwa mayelana nohlelo lwakhe ne-Lakers ngemidlalo eyisithupha ayidlale ingakaqali isizini.
“Angidingi imidlalo yokuzicijisela ukuqala kwesizini okwamanje ezingeni lamikulomkhakha wami ukuze ngilungele ukuqala ukudlala” ngokusho kwakhe.
Umdlalo yomjaho wezimoto i-Trump’s West Virginia Rally Time uvezwa kuhlelo lwe-YouTube
Umongameli u-Donald Trump uqala isivunguvungu somkhankaso ngomjaho wezimoto e ubusuku ohlelweni iWheeling, e-West Virgina.
Umjaho ka-Trump wokuqala kweyisihlanu ayihlelile ngesonto elizayo, kubandakanya ukuma ezindaweni zobungani kubalwa ne Tennessee ne-Mississippi.
Ngesiqinisekiso sevoti elizokhetha ozovala isikhala sasenkantolo enkulu, uTrump uhlose ukwakha abalandeli kulolukhetho lwamaphakathi njengoba ama Republicans esengozini yokulahlekelwa ukubusa isigungu ngoLwezi.
Umjaho wokhetho ka-Trump’s e-West Virgina , uzoqala ngasikhathi sini?
Umjaho wokhetho ka-Trump e-Wheeling, West Virginia izoqala ngehora lesikhombisa kusihlwa. ET ebusuku, ngomgqibelo, 29 Mandulo 2018.
Ungabuka umjaho wokhetho luka-Trump e-West Virginia ngokungena ku-YouTube ubuke okwenzeka manje.
U-Trump kungenzeka ahole ukalalelwa kwalelisonto koqokwe inkantoloinkantolo enkulu, u-Brett Kavanaugh, eshubiswe izinsolo zamacala ezocansi nesikhulu esilindelwe sevoti le-Senate njengoba I-FBI isaphenya.
Kodwa ke inhlosongqangi yalesivunguvungu somkhankaso ukusiza ama-Republicans athole umdlandla wokubhekana nokhetho lukaLwezi.
Ngakhoke, umongameli uTrump kumkhankaso wakhe uthe lemijaho yeimoto emihlanu ngesonto elizayo uhlose “ukunika umdlandla amavolontiya nabalandeli njengoba amaRepublicans ezama ukuvikela nokwandisa isibalo sabalandeli abanaso ephalamende,” ngokuka Reuters.
“ukulawula isigungu kubalulekile kuloluhlelo lwamongameli lokuhambela amazwe amaningi angakwazi ukuwahambela njengoba siphokophelele kwisikhathi esimatasa somkhakhankaso” kuphika usomlomo womkhankaso ka-Trump onqabele I-Reuters ukuthi idalule igama lakhe.
Ihlelelwe i-Wesbanco Arena ese Wheeling, imijaho yanamuhla yezimoto ingaletha abalandeli abasuka e “Ohio nasePennsylvania isakazwe kwezokuxhumana zasePittsburgh,” ngokusho kwe-West Virginia Metro News.
Ngomgqibelo kuzobe kungokwesibili ezinyangeni ezimbili uTrump evakashela e-West Virginia, izwe aliwina ngamaphesenti angaphezu kwamashumi amabili ngonyaka ka-2016.
u-Trump uzama ukusiza omele ukungena i-West Virgina Republican Senate.
“Akusilo uphawu oluhle ku-Morrisey ukuthi umongameli eze azame ukuzomulekelela awine ukhetho,” kusho u-Simon Haeder, ungoti kwezombusazwe eNyuvesi yaseWest Virgina , ngokubika kuka-Reuters.
Indebe ye-Ryder 2018 Iqembu lase-Melika liyazethemba ukulwa ligcine amathemba ekhona emidlalweni yosuku olulodwa ngeSonto.
Emva kwemhlangano emithathu yohlangothi olulodwa, ngoMgqibelo ntambama, kungenzeka lemidlalo ye-Ryder Cup bekumele iphindwe izikhawu ezine.
Isikhali somdlandla ngokuphelele siwuhlelo lomdlalo oluqaliwe kodwa ke abadlali abakholelwa kuwo, ongefaniswe.
Pho kukuphi lapho bezothi  manje ngamandla?
“Bahola ngamaphuzu ayisithupha kanti manje asemane, ngakho siyaqhubeka njengokungathi ngamandla amancane Ngiyacabanga” kusho Jordan Spieth njengoba ezishayela kancane osukwini.
Europe inamathuba , ngempela, amaphuzu amane ngaphambili kwangamashumi nambili.
Americans, njengoba eshilo Spieth, banokujabula okuncane kanti banokuningi abangakhuthazwa ngakho, hhayi ngendlela ka Spieth kanye no Justin Thomas abadlale ndawonye usuku lonke kanti ngamunye uthole amaphuzu amathathu kwamane.
Spieth ubelokhu eyingozi futhi ubehola ngesibonelo.
Labo ababukele bebejabula kakhulu uma sekunguye, ukushaya ngesineke igalofu kubaluleke ukuze umdlalo ulingane  lapho yena kanye Thomas beshiyana ngamabili.
Igalofu lakhe alifaka banqoba umdlalo ngo-15 injabulo efanayo, loluhlobo likuthsela ukuthi uyakholwa ukuthi iqembu American alikaphumi.
“ngempela kuzomele umbe ujule futhi ukhathazeke ngowakho umdlalo,” kusho u-Spieth.
Sekungamunye walabadlali  abasele manje.
Imigodi engu-18 ukuzibeka uphawu.
Okuwukuphela komdlali onamapuzu amaningi ukudlula Spieth kanye Thomas ezinsukwini ezimbili ezidlule yilaba Francesco Molinari kanye Tommy Fleetwood, akubuzwa kule Ryder Cup.
Europe's odd kodwa umbhanqwano owenza kahe kakhulu futhi ozimisele.
"Moliwood" bawukuphela komata abangeke baqale i-bogey ngoMgqibelo ntambama, kodwa bagwema i-bogeys  uMgqibelo ekuseni, uLwesihlanu ntambama kanye noLwesihlanu ekuseni.
Loku kugijima, ngangendlela  koubili abanomfutho ngayo kusuka kulolu quqaba olunomsindo abaphetha ngokuthi bangabadlali abazonqoba ngeSonto, kanti akuphinde kube khona abadlali abaziwayo abazoba nomdlandla ukunqoba European njengoba ilanga liyishonela Le Golf National kune-Fleetwood noma Molinari.
Yomibili kanye kanye imigodi ayifani
Inkulumo ngodumo European alukashintshi, yize kunjalo.
Bubba Watson kanye Webb Simpson benza omncane umsebenzi Sergio Garcia, amaqhawe e-fourballs  asekuseni, lapho eboshelwa Alex Noren.
Bogey  kanye two doubles baphambili bashiye igebe elide Spaniard kanye Swede abangeke balifice.
NgeSonto, akukho muntu ozokusiza uphume emgodi wakho.
Fourballs kanye foursomes bajabulela ukubukela eduze ngenxa yokubambisana phakathi komata,  iseluleko abasinikayo, siseluleko abangasiki kanye nendlela iqhinga elingashintsha masinyane.
Europe idlale kahle kakhule njengeqembu futhi yahola kwaba sekugcineni kodwa i foursomes ibonisile ukuthi iQembu USA belisasenamandla okuqhubeka, ngokukhethile Stateside, belingabaza.
Europe ithathe 10-6 ihola ngosuku lokugcina Ryder Cup.
Europe izoba sebamathebeni amaingi amahle ngosuku lokugcina Ryder Cup ngemva kokuphuma fourballs kanye foursomes ngoMgqibelo ngo10-6  ihola United States.
duo Tommy Fleetwood kanye Francesco Molinari banqoba kabili ngaphezu kokudonsa kanzima Tiger Woods ngamaphuzu amane Le-Golf National.
Osohlangothini  lwe-Europe Thomas Bjorn, ukuzimisele ukugicna indebe eyabalahlekela e-Hazeltine eminyakeni emibili edlule, ukwehluleka America kwi- fourballs yasekusseni, ibeke uchungechunge luka-3-1.
U.S. iyimise kanzima nakakahulu i-foursomes, ukunqoba imidlalo emibili, kodwa angeke imane izigwazele ibhece.
Ngasohlangothini Jim Furyk udinga amaphuzu ayisishiyagalolunye emidlalweni engu-12 yangeSonto ukuze agcine indebe.
Fleetwood ungowokuqala e-Europe ukuzizuzela amaphuzuamane  kulandelana ngenkathi yena kanye Molinari, yambiza "Molliwood" ngemva kwempelasonto enhle bangabesili abazuze amaphuzu amane  emidlalweni yabo emine yokuvula emlandweni we-Ryder Cup.
Ngokwehlula Woods no Patrick Reed kwi fourballs emva kwalokho bazigwazela ibhece Woods kanye Bryson Dechambeau waseAmerica ngo-5&4.
U-Woods, ungenile emidlalweni emibili yangoMngqibelo, wabonisa ukuzimisela okukhulu kodwa yena manje ulahlekelwe imidlalo engu-19 kwengu-29 fourballs kanye foursomes kulandelana.
U-Justin Rose, uzihlalele kwi-fourballs yasekuseni, waphindela kumata Henrik Stenson kwi-foursomes ngo-2&1 ukwehlula Dustin Johnson kanye Brooks Koepka – isigaba sokuqala nesesithathu emhlabeni wonke.
Futhi bazimisele ukubuyela emandleni nganoma iyiphi indlela abngayithola, buka nje unya, nokungcola.
U-Jordan Spieth kanye Justini bahlomuhle izikhathi ezintathu behlula ama-America ngamaphuzu amathathu ngoMgqibelo.
Bazizuzele u-2&1 ngokwehlula Jon Rahm kanye Ian Poulter baseSpain kwi- fourballs kwathi kamuva bahlula Poulter kanye Rory McIlroy ngo- 4&3 kwi- foursomes ngenkathi begeja imigodi emibili evuleikle.
Emlandweni Ryder Cup kukabili kuphela ukuba neqembu lisuka emaphuzwini amane liya emidlalweni engayodwa, ngakolunye uhlangothini Furyk udinga ukulinganisa kuphela ukuze avikele indebe.
Ngemva kokwenza kangcono izinsuku ezimbili,  noma unjalo, ukuhlasela kwangeSonto ibonakala izobahlula.
I-North Korea ithi ‘angeke’  ingahlomi ngaphandle ayithembi.
Ungqongqoshe wezangaphandle  waseNorth Korea watshela i- United Nations ngoMgqibelo iqhubeka ijulisa ukungathembeki United States kanti akunakwenzeka ngezwe ukuba lingadedela izikhali zenuzi ngaphansi kwanoma iziphi izimo.
U-Ri Yong Ho watshela indikimba yomhlaba i-General Assembly ukuthi North Korea yenze “ukubuyisana” onyakeni odlule, njengokuvimba inuzi kanye nokuvivinya izikhali eziyigozi,  ukuqeda izindawo zenuzi, kanye nokuthembisa ukungazandisi izikhali zenuzi kanye nobuchwephe benuzi.
Uthe,“Noma kunjalo, asiboni ukuziphendulela okuvela e U.S.”
“Ngokungayethembi  U.S. angeke libe khona ithemba ukuvikeleka ezweni kanti ngaphansi kwalesi simo ayikho indlela yokuthi singazihlomisi thina kuqala.”
Ngesikhathi Ri engavumelani ngokukhonda kwe North Korean mayelana nokwenqaba kwe Washington “ngesigaba” ukuqeda kwenuzi kuyilapho North Korea ingase iklonyeliswe ngokuthatha izinyathelo, istatimende sibonufakazi ekutheni asikuvimbi ukuqedwa kwenuzi ngokuphelele njengoba Pyongyang enza ngokwedlule.
U-Ri ubhekisele esitatimendeni emiswa ngu Kim Jong Un kanye Donald Trump okokuqala bedibana phakathi kukamongameli U.S kanye nomholi we North Korea eSingapore ngoJuni 12,  lapho Kim ecela ukusebenza kwi ” denuclearization of the Korean peninsula” ngesikhathi Trump ethembisa ngokuvikeleka kwe North Korea.
I-North Korea beyilokhu ifuna ukuqeda kahle Impi ye Korea ka1950-53, kodwa United States yathi Pyongyang makadedele izikhali zenuzi kuqala.
Washington ibilokhu inqaba ukukhulula North Korea.
“U.S. iphikelela nge ” ukuqedwa kwenuzi-kuqala” kanti iphamakamisa amazinga okucindezela  umthetho ukufeza inhloso yayo ngempoqo, nokuthi futhi  inqabe “isimemezelo sokuqeda impi”” kusho Ri.
“Ukuqonda ukuthi umthetho ungasithobisa okuyiphupho labantu abangendaba nathi.
Kodwa inkinga ukuthi ukuqhubeka phambili kujulisa ukungazethembi kwathina.
U-Ri akazidalulanga izinhlelo zokuthi kuphinde  kube nokudibana phakathi kuka Kim kanye no-Trump ukuthi umholi we U.S. ekuvezile eZizweni Ezihlangene  zisuka evikini.
Ungqongqoshe okungenani ukuveze imihlangano emithathu phakathi ku  Kim kanye nomholi we South Korea Moon Jae-in ezinyangeni ezinhlanu ezedlule futhi wanezela: “ uma ingxenye kule ndaba yokuqedwa kwenuz bekwiyi South Korea kanti hhayi U.S., ukuqedwa kwenuzi Korean peninsula angeke kubangele kulokhu kuzibophezela.”
Noma kuthiwa kunjalo, ukuzwakala kwenkulumo kaRi bekuhluke ngokuphelele kweya ngonyaka odlule, lapho etshela i- U.N. General Assembly lena ebheke U.S. indawo ephambili ne North Korea's rockets eyenzeke ngemva “Mnu. Mongameli Omubi” Trump ebize Kim “rocket man” kulokhu.
Kulo nyaka i-United Nations, Trump, lo owasongela “ngokuqeda ngokuphelele” North Korea, ukuziphakamisa Kim ngesibindi sakhe sokungathathi sinyathelo ngokuhloma, kodwa kuningi okusamelwe kwenziwe kanti umthetho uhlale ukhona kuze kube yilapho  North Korea iqeda inuzi.
NgoLwethathu, Trump uthe akanaso isikhathi sayo yonke lento, uthi ”uma kuthatha iminyaka emibili, emithathu, noma emihlanu – akunankinga.”
China kanye Russia baphikasana ngokuthi I-U.N.  Security Council kuafenele baklomelise i- Pyongyang ngezinyathelo ezithathiwe.
Noma kunjalo, U.S. UNobhala woMbuso Mike Pompeo watshela i-U.N. Security Council ngoLwesine ukuthi: Security Council ngoLwesine ukuthi: “Ukuphoqelela kwe-Security Council kumelwe kuqhube ngamandla futhi ingahluleki kuze kube yilapho sibona isiphetho, ngokugcwele, nobufakazi bokuqedwa kwenuzi.”
Security Council ivumile ukusekela North Korea ekuphuleni umthetho kusukelango-2006 ekumiseni ukukhokheleni inuzi kanye nesimiso ballistic missile kaPyongyang.
U-Pompeo wahlangana Ri bama ne- U.N. General Assembly futhi bathi emva kwako konke sisazo vakashela  futhi Pyongyang ngenyanga ezayo ukulungiselela okwesibili.
Pompeo ube kade evakashele North Korea izikhathi ezintathu kulo nyaka, kodwa uhambo lwakhe lokugcina alubanga luhle.
Washiya Pyongyang ngoJulayi  ethe inqubekela phambili yenziwa,  yeNorth Korea kuphela  ngokumveza obala ”ngokuphoqa nje-sigebengu.”
North Korea ihlela umhlangano no Moon kule nyanga ukuqeda indawo ye missile kanye nenhlanganisela yenuzi uma i- United States ithatha ”izinyathelo ezifanayo.”
Wathi Kim wangitshela  “ngezinyathelo ezifanayo”  wayefuna ukuqinisa ezokuphepha lapho Trump ethembisa eseSingapore futhi ebangela isimo esivamile sobudlelwano ne Washington.
Abafundi be Harvard icourse iyabasiza ekulaleni ngokwanele
Course entsha e Harvard University kulo nyaka bonke abangakaphothuli balala kakhulu ukuze ukunqoba ukumkhuba yokutadisa besebenzisa icaffeine ‘ubusuku bonke.’
Imikhakha yemfundo ithole abafundi abaningi emanyuvesi aphambili ukuthi abazalutho uma kuziwa ezintweni eziyisisekelo zokuthi bangazinakekela kanjai.
Charles Czeisler, uprofesa womuthi wokulala  eHarvard Medical School futhi nongoti eBrigham kanye Women's Hospital, usungule i-icourse, ingoyokuqala ngqa yalolu hlobo US.
Wakhuthazwe ukuqala i-course ngemva kokunika inkulumo mayelana nendlela ukulala okundinma ngayo ekufundeni.
‘Ekupheleni kwayo kweza intombazane kimi yathi: ‘Kungani  ngitshelwa lokhu manje, onyakeni wami wamabanga aphakathi?’
Yathi akekho owake wamtshela yena mayelana nokulala – okungimangalisile,’ utshele iTelegramu.
Course ikhishwe okokuqala kulo nyaka, ichazela abafundi ukubaluleka kwemikhuba yokulala ngokwanele kusiza ikhademu kanye nokuzivocavoca, kanti ithuthukisa inhlalakahle yansuku zonke.
U-Paul Barreira, profesa wengqondo eHarvard Medical School kanti futhi ongumqondisi we university's health services, uthe unyuvesi inqume ukufa i-course ngemva kokuthola ukuthi abafundi abaningi abalali nhlobo phakathi neviki.
Ubude besifundo buhlanganisa uchungechunge lokhuthile okwenziwayo.
Ingxenye yokuqala kunesithombe  segumbi lesikole, lapho abafundi bekhetha izikhomishi ye-coffee, amakhethenisi, abaqeqeshi kanye nezincwadi ezikhuluma ngemiphumela ye-caffeine kanye nokukhanya ukuzivocavoca kusiza kanjani ekulaleni , kanye nendlela yokulala.
Kwenye ingxenye, abanengxenye bayatshelwa ukuthi ukugwema ukulala isikhathi eside kukhulisa amathuba esifo senhliziyo, isitilokhi, ukuncindeleka kanye nomdlavuza.
Ibalazwe lekhempasi, linezimphawu eziwusizo, khona lizokhuthaza abanengxenye ekubakhuthazeni bacabange ngenqubo yabo yansuku zonke.
‘Siyazi ukuthi angeke ishintshe ukuziphatha kwabafundi’ ngokushesha.
Sikholelwa ukuthi banelungelo lokwazi – njengoba nje nawe ilungelo lokwazi ngempilo yakho ngokukhetha ukubhema ugwayi,’ enezela uProfesa u-Czeisler.
Isiko lokuzigqaja 'ekuhlaleni kuze kuse' yinto esenziwa, esho, engeza ukuthi ubuchwepheshe bethekhinoloji besimanje nengcindezi eyeqile kubafundi inciphisa amazinga okulala okuyinkinga eya ngokudlondlobala.
Ukuqinisekisa ukuthi ulala ngkwanele, ngokwanele, kumele kube ‘isikhali esiyimfihlo’ somfundi ukunqoba ingcindezi, ukukhathala nokukhathazeka, esho –ngisho kugwema ukukhuluphala, njengoba ukungalali kufaka ingqondo kwisimo sendlala, okwenza balambe.
Raymond Shuthi, umfundi oneminyaka engu 19 ubudala eCalifornia ofunda i-chemical ne-physical biology, wasiza uPhrofesa Czeisler ukuklama isifundo, eke wafunda kwelinye lamakilasi akhe nyakenye ngenkathi efunda unyaka wakhe wokuqala eHarvard.
Uthe isifundo simvule amehlo futhi samgqugquzela ukuba aphushe lesifundo kube esesikhungo sonke.
Isinyathelo esilandelayo, wethemba, esokucela abafundi beziqu eziphakeme ukuba bafunde ngendlela efanayo naloluhlelo lokufunda phambi kokuba bajoyine lesikhungo esinokuncintisana okucokeme.
UProf Czeisler utuse ukuthi abafundi kumele bacabange ukusetha ama-alarm ngenkathi beya kolala, nakanjalo ukuthi bazovuka nin, nokuqonda imthelela emibi ‘yokukhanya okuluhlaza sasibhakabhaka’ ekhishwa izikrini zagesi kanye nokukhanya kwe-LED, okungakukhipha kwisigqi sokuzungeza, okuholela kwizinga mekumele.
Livingston 1 - 0 Rangers: Inqaku lika Menga lehlisa amadoda ka Gerrard
I-Rangers yehlelwe umshophi futhi behambile ngenkathi bezunywa uDolly Menga ohlasele icala lika Steven Gerrard elingabumbene waliqumba phansi bahluleka 1-0 eLivingston.
I-Ibrox side ibihlose ukuqopha ukunqopha kwabo kokuqala behambile kusukela benqoba ngoFebhruwari 4-1 eSt Johnstone, kodwa iqembu lika Gary Holt ongumthelela wokuhlulwa kwesibili kuka Gerrard kwimidlalo engu 18 njengo mphathi oshiye icala lakhe esemuva ngamaphuzu ayisishiyagalombili kubaholi be-Ladbrokes Premiership Hearts.
Menga uhlasele emzuzwini eyisikhombisa phambi kwe-half-time kanti abadlali beRangers bekhuthazela bengagobi phondo.
Ngenkathi manje iRangers yehlela endaweni yesithupha, iLivingston iqhwakela endaweni yesithathu futhi ngemuva kweHibernian abashiyana ngenqaku vo.
Futhi kungahle kube khona inkinga ezayo kwi-Rangers ngemva kokuba usomugqa uCalum Spence enywangwe ngosizo lokuqala emva kwengozi ekhada ebangelwe okuthile okujikijelwe kude.
UGerrard wenze ushintsho kasishiyagalombili kwicala olwedlule i-Ayr ukuya kwi-Betfred Cup semi-finals.
UHolt, kwelinye icala, uhambe naleyo Livi 11 efanayo ephuce iphuzu kwiHearts ngesonto eledlule futhi ubenga thokoza ngendlela izambatho zakho ebezigqokwe kahle ebezincisha izi mbangi zakhe umoya kumacala onke.
IRangers kungenzeka ukuthi ilibambe kakhulu ibhola kodwa iLivingston yenze okuningi ngebhola elitholile.
Ngabe bakorile ngemizuzu emibili bengenile ngenkathi ukulaliswa kukaMenga kuthumela uScott Pittman kwinqaku lika Allan McGregor kodwa umdlali odlala esiswini elahle ithuba elikhulu egeja ipali.
I-free kick  ka-Keaghan Jacobs ethole uCraig Halkettoyi- skipper kodwa umvimbi ongumlingani wakhe u-Alan Lithgow ulihlabe kude le emuva.
IRangers ikwazile ukulawula kodwa bekungukwethemba kakhulu kunokukholwa kumdlalo wabo kwisigaba sesithathu sokugcina somdlalo.
U-Alfredo Morelos ubezizwa ngathi bekumele athole i-penalty ngokwarathu ngesikhathi eshayisana noSteve Lawless kodwa unompempe uSteven Thomson usichithile isicelo sowase Colombian.
IRangers ikwazileukufaka amanqaku amabili ngesigamu sokuqala ebhekene ngqo nepali kodwa unozinti omdala we-Ibrox uLiam Kelly bengakhathazekile ngenqabu elifakwe ngekhanda lika Lassana Coulibaly nokuhlasela okuthotshiwe kuka Ovie Ejaria.
Ngenkathi uLivi evulela ngenaku ngomzumzu ka34 kungenzeka bekungekho ngokomdlalo, akekho obengaphika ukuthi bebelifanele ngokokusebenza kwabo.
IRangers iphinde yahluleka ukumelana nencwenga yebhola lika Jacobs.
UScott Arfield akenzanga lutho ngenkathi uDeclan Gallagher ekhahlela uScott Robinson, obesipholele waphosela uMenga ukuba aqedele kalula.
UGerrardube nomnyakazo emva kwekhefu ngesikhathi eshintsha uCoulibaly ngo Ryan Kent futhi lolushintsho lucishe laba nothelela ngokushesha ngesikhathi umgadli ekhahlelela eMorelos kodwa uKelly ohlaba umxhwele ujime esuka kulayini wakhe ukuzovimba.
Kodwa uLivingston uqhubekile nokuchaza ababukeli ngokudlala umdlalo abawuthakaselayo, noLithgow neHalkett beshanela amabhola amade emva kwamanye amade.
Icala lika Holt belingavula igebe kubuholi kwizigaba zokugcina kodwa uMcGregor usukumile wanqabela uJacobs phambi kokuba uLithgow eshaye ibhola ngekhanda ekhoneni.
Ongenele uRangers uGlenn Middleton uthola sekukudala iphenathi ngesikhathi ebambana noJacobs kodwa futhi uThomson ubheke eceleni.
Almanac: Umsungli we-Geiger Counter
And Futhi manje ikhasi lethu “leSonto Ekuseni” Almanac: Septhemba 30, 1882, eminyakeni ewu 136 eyedlule, futhi UBALA ... usuku lapho i-physicist yakusasa uJohannes Wilhelm "Hans" Geiger wazalwa eGermany.
UGeiger usungule indlela yokuthola nokulinganisa radioactivity, okusunguliwe eyaholela kwidavayisi eyagcina yakhiwe nje leGeiger Counter.
Umgogodla wesayensi kusukela lapho, iGeiger Counter eyaphenduka umgogodla wesika lepop, njengakumamuvi ango 1950 "Bells of Coronado," okudlla kuwo amakhawa ososayensi uRoy Rogers noDale Evans:
Indoda: "Engabe yini leyo?"
Rogers: "IGeiger Counter, isetshenziselwa ukuthola ama-radioactive minerals, njenge uranium.
Ngenkathi ufaka ama-earphones avuliwe, ungakwazi ukuzwa ama-atoms akhishwe i-radioactivity ngamamineral."
Evans: "Ithi, ziyakhipha manje!"
"Hans" Geiger washona ngo 1945, kusele izinsukwana agubhe iminyaka ewu 63.
Kodwa lokhu okusunguliwe kuthwele igama lakhe kuze kube phakade.
Umgomo omusha womdlavuza ungafundisa isistimu yokuzivikela ‘ukubona’ ama-cell angalungile
Umgomo omusha womdlavuza ungafundisa isistimu yokuzivikela ‘ukubona’ ama-cell angalungile bese iwabulala
Umgomo ufundisa isistimu yokuzivikela ‘ukubona’ ama-cell angalungile njengohlelo lokwelashwa
Indlela ibandakanya ukuthatha ama-cell esistimu yokuzivikela kwisiguli, ashintshwe elebhu
’Ayayibona’ i-protein evamile kwimdlavuza eminingi bese ujovwa kabusha
Umgomo wokunhlovo ukhombisa imiphumela ethembisayo kwiziguli ezinezinhlobo zemidlavuza.
Owesifazane olashwe ngomgomo, ofundisa isistimu yokuzivikela ukuba ibone ama-cell angalungile, wabona umdlavuza wesibeletho unyamalala ngaphezi kwezinyanga eziwu 18.
Le ndlela ibandakanya ukuthatha ama-cell avikelayo kwisiguli, aguqulwe elabhorethri ukuze “abone” i-protein evamile kumdlavuza emningi ebizwa HER2, bese ujovwa kabusha ama-cell.
UPhrofesa uJay Berzofsky, we-US National Cancer Institute in Bethesda, Maryland, uthe: "Imiphumela yethu ivezaukuthi sinomgomo othembisayo."
HER2 "ikhuthaza ukuhluma kwezinhlobo zomdlavuza," kubandakanya eyowebele, owesibeletho, owephaphu kanye neminye imidlavuza, kuchaza uProf Berzofsky.
Enye indlela efanayo yokuthatha ama-cell avikelayo kwiziguli”nokuwafundisa” ukuthi uqonda kanjani kuma-cell omdlavuza okusebenz kahle ekulapheni uhlobo oluthile lwe- leukaemia.

HIV/Aids: I-China ibika u-14% ukuqhubekela phambili ezimweni ezintsha
I-China isimemezela ukunyuka ngo 14% kwanani lwezakhamizi eziphila nengculazi ne sandulela ngculazi.
Abantu abangaphezu kuka-820,000 bathinteka kuleli zwe, izikhulu zezempilo zithi.
Amacala amasha angaba ngu-40,000 abikwa kwikota yesibili ka-2018 uwodwa.
Iningi lamacala amasha eze.
Iningi lamacala amasha adluliselwa ngezocansi, amaka ushintsho kusuka esikhathini esidlule.
Kodwa isibalo sabantu abathola ngculazi ngale ndlela siye sanciphisa cishe safika ku zero , izikhulu zempilo zase China zasho njalo emhlanganweni wesifundazwe saseYunnan.
Unyaka-no-nyaka, kodwa ke inani labantu abaphila negculazi nesandulela ngculazi sesinyuke ngaba abangu 100,000.
Ukuthelelana kwengculazi ngoku cansi inkinga encane kwi LGBT community.
Ukubayicala ukuthandana nobuliliobufanayp e-China kwasulwa ngo 1997, kodwa kucwaswa kubantu abathandana nobulili obufanayo kudlangile.
Ngenxa yendlela zokuphila, ucwaningo luke lwaveza ukuthi 70-90% wabantu besilisa abalala nabanye besilisa bagcine beshade nabantu besifazane.
Okuningi ukutheleleka kwezifo kuqhamuka kukuzivikela akungalungile kucansi kulobu budlelwano.
Kusukela ngo 2003, uhulumeni wase China wathembisa ukufinyelela komhlaba kwimishwanguzo njengemizamoyokubhekana nenkinga.

Lezinsolo ezingeasisekelo zamanga impela futhi azilona iqiniso."

"Lokuphika kunokudinwa," kubhala uFleischer.
"Lokhu kuchaza ukuthi akanabo ubumnene bokua iLungu likaKhongolose.
Uma umuntu esolwa ngokuthile abangakwenzanga, akumele badinwe.

Umbono ngoJohnny English Strikes Again – yehlise amandla spy poof yaRowan Atkinson
Kuyisiko manje ukubheka ukubaluleka kuka Brexit kunoma iyiphi i-engela ifilimu yase Britain futhi ayibukeki ihambisa nokuvuswa kwalomdlalo wamahlaya i-Johnny English – eyaqala kudala ngo 2003 noJohnny English nokubuyiswa kwayo ngo 2011 i-Johnny English Reborn.
Ukudla amazambane ashisayo njenge sisho kwisihloko sokuthi singaba nethuba elisha lokudayisa ngaphandle?
Kunoma isiphi isilinganiso, ihlo elivuliwe, ubuso berabha baJohnny English obenegunya lokukhuthaza izinto ezintsha okwesibili – lelo gama liyihlaya elikhulu eliklanyelwe izinkundla zamabhayisikobho zabantu abangasikhulumi Isingisi.
Impela uyi-ejenti yenhloli engakhaliphile okudlula ngisho nokuzenzisa kwakhe okungajwayelekile kuya kubukhazikhazi kuveza  i-Clouseau, uchatha ka Mr Bean nomfutho wakhe ovela kushuni weChariots of Fire theme kumkhosi wokuvulwa weeLondon 2012 Olympics.
Futhi kususelwa kumhambi nendoda yemfihlakalo uAtkinson odlula kwizikhangiso omanje sewakhohlakala eBarclaycard TV, oshiye isiphithiphithi ekuvukeni kwakhe.
Kunezikhathi ezinye nezimbili kulokuvakasha kwamanje e-JE.
Ngiyamthanda uJohnny English eyogibela ihelicopter ebe egqke isudi yakudala yamasosha nezinkemba ezincane zilenga esigqokweni sakhe.
Isipho sika Atkinson samahlaya siwumbukiso, kodwa ukuhlekisa kubukeka ngathi kuphansi futhi kuyihaba kakhulu, ikakhulukazi kumkhiqizo wamafilimu “ajulile” njengo 007 neMission Impossible uqobo manje anikeza amahlaya njengesithako.
Amahlaya ngathi aphezuukwizingane kunabantu abadala, kanti kimi uhambo luka Johnny English awanahlonze futhi awamasha futhi awagxilile kwifilimu ka Atkinson engenamsindo eyengezwe ngemisindo nobuntu buka Bean.
Indaba esegudwini manje ileyo yokuthi iGreat Britain isenkigeni enkulu.
Icyber-hacker ingene kwinethiwekho eymfihlo yezinhloli yase Britain, iveza imniningwane yama-ejenti aseBritain kumkhakha, okukhathaze i-ejenti ebibekiwe emsebenzini – okuwumsebenzi omncane kuKevin Eldon.
Umzuzu wokugcina kwi-prime minister ozithwele  nosemnkantsha ubovu, obhekene nokwahluleka kumphakathi wezepolitiki: U-Emma Thompson uzama ngokusemandleni ukulingisa uTeresa-May kodwa akukho okutheni kumbhalo angasebeza ngakho.
Abayali bakhe bobunhloli bamazisa ukuthi yonke inhloli impintshiwe, kuzomele alande umuntu osesempeshenini.
Lokhu kusho ukuthi uJohnny English uqobo, manje njengo schoolmaster endaweni ebizayo, kodwa enika izifundo ezingaqoshiwe zokuthi ubakanjani inhloli: amahlaya lawa, njengoba u-English unikeza imfundiso zobunhloli eRock-type academy.
U-Englishugijinyiswe eWhitehall ukuba anikwe imiyalo ephuthumayo futhi ahlanganiswe nomlingani uBough, pedlalwa futhi uBen Miller.
UBough useyindoda eshadile, ohlanganiswa ne-submarine commander, indawo emnandi edlalwa ngu Vicki Pepperdine okudlalwe ngaye.
Ngakho ke uBatman noRobin wokwenza izinto zibhede impela kuSevisi eyimfihlo yeNdlovukazi ibuyile, ihlangabezana no-Olga Kurylenko's beautiful femme fatale Ophelia Bulletova.
Lapho ke, uprime minister uyadobeka ngokushesha kwimpucuzeko zasozigidi othi yena angaxazulula izinkinga zamakhompuyutha: the sinister Jason Volta, edlalwa ngu Jake Lacy.
U-English no Bough baqala uhambo lwabooluyindida: becashe njengo weta, baqala umlilo kwindawo yokudlela eFrance; baqala inkinga bezishushumbisa ngesikebhe sikanokusho iVolta; noEnglish okususe indida ngenkathi efunda  ukusebenzisa iVirtual Reality headset ukuzijwyeza indlu kaVolt.
Yonke imizamo yenziwe ukwenza ngcono isiqephu sokugcina noma sinobungane nomfutho, kune TV yezingane mayelana nayo yonke into.
Okuvamisile impela.
Futhi njengamanye amafilimu kaJohnny English angikwazanga ukuzibamba: umkhakha wezamafilimu eBritain  awukwazanga ukunika uRowan Atkinson indawo ekhombisa khle ithalente lakhe?

Iqembu lika Jeremy Corbyn le- Labour ukucabanga icebo elimangalisayo elizobona uBritons esebenza izinsulu ezine – kodwa akhokhelwe ezinhlanu.

Yini i-Global Citizen Festival futhi Isike Yazama Ukunciphisa Ububha?
Kulo Mgqibelo iNew York izosingatha iGlobal Citizen Festival, umcimbi wanyaka yonke olunohlu lwabadlali abanohlonzeabazodlala nabanenhloso efanayo; yokuqeda ububha emhlabeni.
Manje kunyaka wesikhombisa, iGlobal Citizen Festival izoba nezinkumbi zabantu betheleka egcekeni elikhulu eCentral Park ukungathokoziswa kuphela uJanet Jackson, Cardi B no Shawn Mendes, kodwa ukuqwashisa ngenhloso yangempela yokuqeda ububha ngo 2030.
I-Global Citizen Festival, echazwe ngo 2012, okuyisixhantela seGlobal Poverty Project, iqembu lomhlaba olulwela ukuqeda ububha ngokwandisa abantu abakulwelayo.
Ukuze uthole ithikithi lomcimbi (ngaphandle kokuthi ufuna ukukhokhela amathikithi e- VIP ticket), abahambi khionsathi bekumele benze kuthile “okuyizenzo” njengokuvolontiya, ukuthumela i-imeyili kumholi womhlaba, ukufona noma ukwenza okunye okujulile ukusiza uqwashise ngokuqeda ububha.
Ingabe ibe yimpumelelo kangakanani i-Global Citizen eminyakeni engu 12 esele ukufinyelela lumgomo wayo?
Ingabe umqondo wokuzuzisa abantu ngekhonsathi yamahhala kuyindlela efanele ukuzama abantu ukuba benze okuthile, noma okunye nje okubizwa "i-clicktivism" – abantu abazizwa ngathi benza umehluko ngokusayina uhlu kwikhompiyutha noma ukuthumela kutwitter?
Kusukela ngo 2011, i-Global Citizen isiqophe “izenzo” zabalandeli babo ezingaphezu kwa 19 million, kuphushwa ukusingathwa kwezinhloso ezahlukene.
Ithi lezenzo sisizile ukucijisa abahli bomhlaba ekwathuleni ukuzinekela kanye nezinqubomgomo ezinga phezu kwa $37 billion ezothinta izimpilo zabantu abangu 2.25 billion ngo 2030.
Ngo 2018 uqala, iqembu licoshe imibono engu 390 kanye nezaziso kusukela kwizenzo zabo, cishe $10 billion osukhishiwe noma wazanywa ukuqoqwa.
Iqembu lilinganisela ukuthi imali etholiwe ibenomthelela ngqo kubantu cishe abawu 649 million emhlabeni jikelele.
Okunye ukuzinikela kubandakanya The Power of Nutrition, abalingani base U.K. babatshali zimali nobaqalisi abazinikele "ukusiza abantwana ngendlela efanele," kuthenjiswa ukunikeza Rwanda $35 million ukusiza kupheliswe indlala ezweni emvakokuthola 4,700 tweets kwiGlobal Citizens.
"Ngokokusekwa uhulumeni wase UK, abanikelayo, ohulumeni bamazwe, ne Global Citizens efana nawe, singazama ukwenza kube umlando ukungondleki kwabantu ngenxa yokungabikho kobulungiswa kumphakathi," I- Power of Nutrition ambassador Tracey Ullman utshene uquqaba bukhoma kwikhonsathi eLondon ngo April 2018.
Iqembu liphinde lathi kube neminyakazo engaphezu kwe 5,000 ukubiza U.K. yenze ngcono ukudla okunomsoco komama nabantwana, uhulumeni umemezele uxhaso lwephrojekthi, i-Power of Nutrition, ezofinyelela kwabesifazane nezingane ezingu 5 million ngokungenelel ngokokudla okunomsoco.
Ekuphenduleni eminye ye-FAQs kwiwebhusayithi yabo ebuza "yini ocabanga ukuthi singayenza ukuqeda ububha obukhulu?"
Global citizen iphendulile: "Kuzoba indlela ende nenzima – ngezinye isikhathi sizowa futhi sehluleke.
Kodwa, njengamalungelo omphakathi nemibhikisho ye-anti-apartheid phambi kwethu, sizonqoba, ngoba sinamandla kakhulu ndawonye.

Washington "uma kudingeka" ingasebenzisa Amantilosi ukuvimba izimakethe zase Russian ze-energy,kubandakanya  i-Middle East, US Internal Secretary Ryan Zinke wambule, ngokucoshwe iWashington Examiner.
Zinke uthe izingxoxo zeRussia neSyria - ngokucacile, lapho isebenza ngokumenya kukahulumeni osemthethweni – kuyindlela yokuzama ezinye izimakethe ezintsha ze-energy.
"Ngiyakholelwa kwisizathu sokuba se-Middle East bafuna ukuthola i-energy njengase eastern Europe, nasenkabeni yase nigizimu ne-Europe," ebika.
Futhi, ngokuvumelana nesisebenzi, kunezindlela zokuyilungisa.
"I-United States iyakwazi, Ngebutho lethu, ukuqinisekisa ukuthi izindlela zasolwandle ziyavulwa, futhi, uma kudingeka, zivalwe, ukuze kuqikelelwe ukuthi amandla abo awayi ezimakethe," kusho yena.
U-Zinke ubekhuluma nababekhona emcimbini ebisingathwa yi-Consumer Energy Alliance, iqembu elingenzi nzuzo elizibiza ngokuthi "iphimbo lomsebenzisi wamandla" e-US.
Wabuye waqhathanisa nemizamo yase-Washington wokusebenzelana ne-Russia ne-Iran, ethi imiphumela iyafana.
"Ukukhetha ukuhwebelana ne-Iran ne-Russia, ngokwezinga elithile, kuyindlela yokuzuza nokuthola uwoyela," kusho yena, ngesikhathi ekhuluma nge-Russia ethi "liyihhashi elinamaqhinga" futhi linomnotho othembele ezinsaleleni zikawoyela.
Lezi zitatimende zivele njengoba abehhovisi lika-Trump benza imizamo yokukhuthaza ukuthunyelwa kwegesi yabo yemvelo ewuketshezi eYurophu, ingene esikhundleni se-Russia, indlela eshibhe kakhulu kubathengi baseYurophu.
Ngenxa yalokho, izikhulu zehhovisi lika-Trump, kuhlanganise nomongameli wase-US u-Donald Trump ngokwakhe, zizama ukukhuthaza iJalimane ukuba liphume kuprojekthi yamapayiphi ye-Nord Stream 2 "engafaneleki", ngokuka-Trump, eyenze i-Berlin yaba "ngaphansi" kwe-Moscow.
I-Moscow iye yagcizelela ngokuphindaphindiwe ukuthi amapayipi e-Nord Stream 2 angu-$11 billion, okuhlelwe ukuba iwuphinde kabili umthamo wamapayipi akhona manje ube ngamamitha angu-110 billion cubic, ngempela ayiphrojekthi yezomnotho.
I-Kremlin ithi ukuphikisana nephrojekthi kwe-Washington ngokungayeki kubangelwa izizathu ezingokomnotho futhi kuyisibonelo somncintiswano ongenabulungisa.
"Ngikholelwa ukuthi sinombono ofanayo wokuthi amandla awanakuba ithuluzi lokufaka ingcindezi nokuthi abathengi kufanele bakwazi ukukhetha ukuthi bathenga kubani," kusho uNgqongqoshe Wamandla Wase-Russia u-Aleksandr Novak ngemva komhlangano noNobhala Wamandla wase-US u-Rick Perry e-Moscow ngo-September.
Ukuma kwe-US kwenze iJalimane lahlehla nyovane, okuqinisekise kabusha ukuzibophezela kwayo kule phrojekthi.

"Nginenkinga enkulu lapho izwe lesithathu liphazamisa ukuthumela kwethu amandla," kusho u-Dieter Kempf, umphathi we-Federation of German Industries (BDI) ngemva komhlangano wamuva phakathi kwe-Chancellor yaseJalimane u-Angela Merkel noMongameli wase-Russia u-Vladimir Putin.
U-Elizabeth Warren "Uzobhekisisa" Ukungenela Ukhetho Lokuba Umongameli Ngo-2020, Kusho I-Senator Yase-Massachusetts
I-Senator Yase-Massachusetts u-Elizabeth Warren ithe ngoMgqibelo "izobhekisisa" ukungenela ukhetho lokuba umongameli ngemva kokhetho olumaphakathi nenkathi.
Phakathi nomhlangano obusehholo ledolobha e-Holyoke, e-Massachusetts, u-Warren uye waqinisekisa ukuthi uzokucabangela ukungenela ukhetho.
"Sekuyisikhathi sokuba abesifazane baye e-Washington futhi balungise uhulumeni wethu owonakele okuhlanganisa owesifazane ozoba umholi," kusho yena, ngokuvumelana ne-The Hill.
"Ngemva kuka-November 6, ngizobhekisisa ukungenela ukhetho lokuba umongameli."
U-Warren ukhulume ngoMongameli u-Donald Trump phakathi nomhlangano wasehholo lasedolobheni, ethi "ubekhuluma nabantu ebadukisa.
"Kungikhathaza kakhulu lokho okwenziwa u-Donald Trump kubantu bakithi," kusho yena.
U-Warren ubekhuluma ngokukhululekile egxeka u-Trump nalowo amkhethele iNkantolo Ephakeme u-Brett Kavanaugh.
Kulokho akubhalile ku-Tweeter ngoLwesihlanu, u-Warren uthe "kuyiqiniso ukuthi sidinga uphenyo lwe-FBI ngaphambi kokuvota."
Umbiko okhishwe ngoLwesine, nokho, ubonise ukuthi iningi labalandeli baka-Warren alicabangi ukuthi kufanele angenele ukhetho ngo-2020.
Amaphesenti angu-50 "okungenzeka" angabantu base-Massachusetts bathi i-senator akufanele ingenele ukhetho, ngokuvumelana nezibalo ezitholwe yi-Suffolk University Political Research Center/Boston Globe.
Amaphesenti angu-32 aye akusekela ukuthi alungenele.
