Izindawo ezingu-18 states, i-D.C. isekela umsebenzi wenqubomgomo entsha yokuvikeleka
Izifundazwe ezingu-18 kanye ne-District of Columbia zisekela umzamo omusha ongokomthetho wokuba nenqubomgomo entsha yase-U.S. enqabela ukuvikeleka kubantu ababalekela udlame lwezigilamkhuba noma lwasekhaya.
Abameleli bezifundazwe ezingu-18 nesifunda bathumele idokhumenti kufakazi ngoLwesihlanu e-Washington ukuze basekele umuntu odinga ukuvikelwa omelene nale nguqomgomo, kubika i-NBC News.
Igama eliphelele lommangali ku-Grace v. Sessions leyo i-American Civil Liberties Union eyifake ngo-August ngokumelene nenqubomgomo yombuso alikambulwa.
Uthe abambisene naye "namadodana akhe angamalungu ezigilamkhuba ezinodlame," bamhlukumeza kodwa izikhulu zase-U.S. zangasamukela isicelo sakhe sokuvikelwa ngo-July 20.
Uye wahlaliswa e-Texas.
Abameli bombuso abasekela u-Grace bachaze i-El Salvador, i-Honduras ne-Guatemala, ekhiqiza abantu abaningi abanezicelo zokuvikelwa yi-U.S., njengezizwe ezibhekene nezinkinga ezinkulu ngezigilamkhuba nodlame lwasekhaya.
Inqubomgomo entsha yase-U.S. yokuvikeleka ijike isinqumo sango-2014 se-Board of Immigrant Appeals esavumela izifiki ezingenamaphepha ezibalekela udlame lwasekhaya ukuba zithole ukuvikeleka.
I-Attorney General yesiFunda sase-Columbia u-Karl Racine ithe emazwini ayo ngoLwesihlanu inqubomgomo entsha "ayiwanaki amashumi eminyaka omthetho wombuso, nowomhlaba wonke."
"Umthetho uthi zonke izicelo zokuvikelwa kumelwe zahlulelwe ngamaqiniso endaba nesimo ngasinye sesicelo, futhi ukwenza isinqumo esinjengalesi kuwukwephula lowo mthetho," kusho ufakazi obizwe yinkantolo.
Abameli baphinde baveza nokuthi inqubomgomo enqabela izifiki ukuba zingene ibulala umnotho wase-U.S., bethi zingase zibe osomabhizinisi futhi "zisungule amathuba emisebenzi."
I-Attorney General u-Jeff Sessions weluleke amajaji ezifiki ukuba angasaphinde avikele abantu ababalekela udlame lwasekhaya nodlame lwezigilamkhuba ngo-June.
"Abantu bangavikelwa uma beshiya izwe labo ngenxa yokushushiswa noma ukwesatshiswa ngenxa yohlanga, inkolo, ubuzwe, noma ukuba ilungu leqembu elithile noma umbono wezepolitiki," kusho u-Sessions esimemezelweni sakhe ngo-June 11 ngenqubomgomo.
Ukuvikelwa kwakungahlosiwe ukuba kuqede zonke izinkinga -- ngisho nazo zonke izinkinga ezinkulu -- abantu ababhekana nazo nsuku zonke emhlabeni wonke.
Kwenziwa imizamo emikhulu e-Palu njengoba inani labafayo liphindaphindeka emizamweni yokuthola abasindile
Kulabo abasindile, isimo besimanzonzo.
"Kubucayi ngempela," kusho umama oneminyaka engu-35 u-Risa Kusuma, eduduza indodana yakhe esikhungweni salabo abaye basinda edolobheni lase-Palu.
"Umzuzu ngamunye i-ambulensi iletha izidumbu.
Asinawo amanzi ahlanzekile."
Izakhamuzi zibonakale ziphindela emizini yazo ecekelwe phansi, ziyobheka impahla yazo emanzini amaningi, zizama ukuthola noma yini ezingayithola.
Amakhulu abantu alimele futhi izibhedlela, ezicekelwe phansi ukuzamazama okuyisilinganiso esingu-7.5, bezigcwele mfi.
Abanye balabo abalimele, kuhlanganise no-Dwi Haris, oye waphuka umgogodla nehlombe, bebehlezi ngaphandle kwase-Palu's Army Hospital, lapho iziguli bezelashelwa khona ngaphandle ngenxa yokuzamazama obekusekhona okuqhubekayo.
Wagcwala izinyembezi emehlweni ngesikhathi ekhumbula indlela okuzamazame ngayo egunjini lasehhotela esitezi sesihlanu abehlala kulo nomkakhe nendodakazi yabo.
"Besingekho isikhathi sokufuna indlela yokusinda.
Bengicindezeleke ezindongeni ezibhodlokile, ngiyacabanga," u-Haris utshele i-Associated Press, enezela nokuthi umndeni wakhe ubusedolobheni emshadweni.
"Ngizwe umkami ekhalela usizo, kwaphinde kwathuleka.
Angazi ukuthi kwenzekeni kuye nasenganeni yami.
Ngethemba ukuthi bayaphila."
Inxusa lase-U.S. limangalela i-China 'ngokwesabisa' 'ngezikhangiso ezingamanga'
Ngemva kweviki iphephandaba elingokomthetho lase-China libe nesikhangiso esingamakhasi amane esibonisa impahla yase-U.S. yezohwebo oluzuzisa kokubili i-U.S. ne-China, inxusa lase-U.S. e-China limangalele i-Beijing ngokusebenzisa iphephandaba laseMelika ukuze isakaze amanga.
UMongameli wase-U.S. u-Donald Trump ngoLwesithathu odlule ukhulume ngempahla ekhokhelwe ye-China Daily e-Des Moines Register - iphephandaba lase-Iowa elithengwa ubuthaphuthaphu - ngemva kokumangalela i-China ngokufuna ukungenela odabeni lokhetho lwango-Nov. 6 e-U.S., okuyinto i-China eyenqabayo.
Isimangalo sika-Trump sokuthi i-Beijing ibizama ukungenela okhethweni lwase-U.S. sidale lokho izikhulu zase-U.S. ezithe ku-Reuters kuyisigaba esisha emkhankasweni we-Washington wokucindezela i-China.
Nakuba kuvamile ukuba ohulumeni bakwamanye amazwe ukuba bakhangise ukuze bahwebe, i-Beijing ne-Washington njengamanje zibambeke empini yohwebo ekhulayo edale ukuba kube nomshuduliswano wezinkokhelo ezingapheli lapho zithumelelana izimpahla.
Izimali ebezifunwa yi-China ngasekuqaleni kwempi yezohwebo zazihloselwe ukuhlukumeeza abathumeli ezindaweni ezinjenge-Iowa ezisekela i-Republican Party ka-Trump, kusho abahlaziyi base-China nase-U.S.
U-Terry Branstad, inxusa lase-U.S. e-China nalowo owayengumbusi wesikhathi eside e-Iowa, okuyiyona ethumela izimpahla eziningi zezolimo e-China, uthe i-Beijing ilimaze izisebenzi zaseMelika, abalimi namabhizinisi.
I-China, kubhala u-Branstad odabeni lwangeSonto i-Des Moines Register, "isikuphinda kabili lokhu kuhlukumeza ngokwenza izikhangiso ezingamanga ephephandabeni lethu lamahhala."
"Emgangeni aye asakazwa, uhulumeni wase-China uzenze watholakala esikweni elithandwayo laseMelika lenkululeko yokukhuluma nephephandaba lamahhala ngokubeka isikhangiso esikhokhelwayo ku-Des Moines Register," kubhala u-Branstad.
"Ngokuphambene nalokho, endaweni edayisa amaphephandaba emgwaqweni lapha e-Beijing, ayiminingi imibono ehlukile ozoyithola futhi ngeke ubone ukusabela kwangempela kwemibono ehlukahlukayo abantu base-China okungenzeka banayo ngemiphumela eyinkinga yomnotho wase-China, uma kucatshangwa ukuthi abezindaba bayibheke ngelokhozi i-Communist Party yase-China," uyabhala.
Uye wanezela ukuthi "elinye lamaphephandaba ahamba phambili e-China libalekele ithuba lokushicilela" indaba yakhe, nakuba engazange asho ukuthi yiliphi lelo phephandaba.
Ama-Republican Achitha Abesifazane Abavotayo Ngaphambi Kokhetho Lwaphakathi Nenkathi Ngenxa Yokwehluleka Kuka-Kavanaugh, Kuxwayisa Abahlaziyi
Njengoba ama-Republicans amaningi aphezulu elindile futhi evikela osethubeni lokufakwa eNkantolo Ephakeme u-Brett Kavanaugh ekumangalelweni okuningana ngokunukubeza, abahlaziyi baxwayise ngokuthi isikhuni sizobuya nomkhwezeli, ikakhulukazi kwabesimame, phakathi nokhetho lwaphakathi nenkathi oluzayo.
Amaphaphu aphezulu ngokuqondene nalokhu, futhi ama-Republican amaningi kakade aseyaziveza ukuthi abefuna ukuqhubekela phambili nokhetho.
Lezo zinto ngeke zisahlehliswa," u-Grant Reeher, uprofesa wesayensi yezepolitiki e-Syracuse University's Maxwell School etshela i-The Hill esihlokweni esishicilelwe ngoMgqibelo.
U-Reeher uthe uyangabaza ukuthi imizamo yokugcina ka-Senator Jeff Flake (R-Arizona) yokuba i-FBI yenze uphenyo izokwanela ukuba yenze abantu abazovota abathukuthele behlise amaphaphu.
"Abesifazane ngeke bakhohlwe lokho okwenzeke izolo - ngeke bakhohlwe kusasa nango-November," kusho u-Karine Jean-Pierre, umeluleki osemnkantsh’ ubomvu nomkhulumeli kazwelonke weqembu elithuthukayo i-MoveOn ngoLwesihlanu, ngokwephephandaba lase-Washington, D.C.
NgoLwesihlanu ekuseni, ababhikishi bamemeze bethi "Uyeza U-November!" njengoba bebebhikisha ehholo le-Senate njengoba ama-Republicans alawula i-Judiciary Committee ekhetha ukuqhubekela phambili nokukhetha u-Kavanaugh naphezu kobufakazi obethulwe nguDkt. Christine Blasey Ford, kubika u-Mic.
"Intshisekelo yama-Democrats nogqozi kuzophela nya," kusho u-Stu Rothenberg, umhlaziyi ongathathi hlangothi wezepolitiki, etshela abezindaba.
"Abantu bathi kakade kuyashisa; iqiniso lelo.
Kodwa kusengaba phezulu kunalokho, ikakhulu phakathi kwabantu abavotayo besifazane emadolobheni nentsha evotayo, eneminyaka engu-18- kuya ku-29, okuthi nakuba bengamthandi umongameli, bengavamile ukuvota."
Ngisho nangaphambi kobufakazi baka-Ford basobala obunemininingwane yezinsolo zakhe zokunukubezwa ezimelene nosethubeni lokufakwa eNkantolo Ephakeme, abahlaziyi bathi isikhuni singabuya nomkhwezeli uma ama-Republican eqhubekela phambili nokuqinisekisa.
"Lokhu sekube umonakalo we-GOP," kusho uMichael Steele, owayengusihlalo we-Republican National Committee, ekuqaleni kweviki elidlule, ngokwe-NBC News.
"Akuqondene nje nevoti yekomiti noma ivoti yokugcina noma ukuthi u-Kavanaugh ubekwa ebhentshini, kumayelana nanendlela ama-Republican akusingathe ngayo lokhu nendlela amphathe ngayo," kusho uGuy Cecil, umqondisi we-Priorities USA, iqembu elisiza abantu ukuba bakhethe ama-Democrats, etshela isiteshi sabezindaba.
Nokho, abaseMelika babonakala behlukene phakathi ngokuthi bakholelwe bani ebufakazini buka-Ford nobuka-Kavanaugh, futhi bathambekele kobuka-Kavanaugh.
Amanani amasha avela kwa-YouGov abonisa ukuthi amaphesenti angu-41 abantu ngokuqinisekile noma ngezinga elithile abekholelwa ubufakazi buka-Ford, kuyilapho amaphesenti angu-35 ethi ngokuqinisekile noma ngezinga elithile akholelwa obuka-Kavanaugh.
Ngaphezu kwalokho, amaphesenti angu-38 athi abecabanga ukuthi u-Kavanaugh ngokuqinisekile noma ngezinga elithile ubeqamba amanga ebufakazini abunikezile, kuyilapho amaphesenti angu-30 asho okufanayo ngo-Ford.
Ngemva kokucindezelwa yi-Flake, i-FBI njengamanje iphenya izimangalo ezilethwe ngu-Ford kanye nommangali okungenani oyedwa, u-Deborah Ramirez, kubika i-The Guardian.
U-Ford wakhuluma phambi kwe-Senate Judiciary Committee efungile ngeviki elidlule ukuthi u-Kavanaugh wamnukubeza edakiwe ngesikhathi eneminyaka engu-17.
U-Ramirez uthi ummangalelwa eNkantolo Ephakeme waveza izitho zakhe zangasese wambonisa ngesikhathi besephathini phakathi nenkathi yokutadisha kwakho e-Yale ngawo-1980.
Umsunguli we-World Wide Web Uhlela Ukuqala I-inthanethi Entsha Ezoqophisana No-Google no-Facebook
U-Tim Berners-Lee, umsunguli we-World Wide Web, uqalisa uhlelo oluzoqophisana nembangi i-Facebook, i-Amazon no-Google.
Iphrojekthi yezobuchwepheshe entsha, i-Inrupt, iyinkampane eyakhelwe emthonjeni ovulekile wepulatifomu yakwa-Berners-Lee i-Solid.
I-Solid ivumela abasebenzisi ukuba bakhethe lapho idatha yabo izogcinwa khona nolwazi abantu abavunyelwa ukuba balufinyelele.
Engxoxweni eyingqayizivele ne-Fast Company, u-Berners-Lee wenze ihlaya wathi inhloso ye-Inrupt "iwukukhonya umhlaba."
"Kumelwe sikwenze manje," usho njalo ngalo msebenzi.
"Kuyingqophamlando."
Le app isebenzisa ubuchwepheshe be-Solid ukuze ivumele abantu bazenzele "indawo yokugcina i-personal online data" noma i-POD.
Ingaba nezinhlu zezinombolo zabantu, okufanele ukwenze, ikhalenda, umtapo womculo namanye amathuluzi obuchwepheshe nawomuntu.
Injenge-Google Drive, i-Microsoft Outlook, i-Slack ne-Spotify zonke zitholakala kubhrawuza eyodwa futhi ngesikhathi esifanayo.
Okuphawulekayo ngesitolo se-POD ukuthi kuxhomeke kumsebenzisi ukuthi ubani ongathola luphi uhlobo lwemininingwane.
Inkampane ikubiza ngokuthi "idatha ekwenza ube namandla."
Umqondo we-Inrupt, ngokuvumelana ne-CEO yenkampane u-John Bruce, uwukuba inkampane ilethe amarisosi, iphrosesi namakhono afanele ekwenzeni i-Solid itholakale kuwo wonke umuntu.
Le nkampane okwamanje ino-Berners-Lee, u-Bruce, ipulatifomu yokuvikeleka ethengwe yi-IBM, izisebenzi ezingabasunguli ezinamankontileka okusebenza kuphrojekthi, kanye nabasunguli bamakhodi abaningi abangamavolontiya.
Kusukela kuleli viki, abasunguli bezobuchwepheshe emhlabeni wonke bangase basungule ama-app abo besebenzisa amathuluzi atholakalayo kuwebusayithi ye-Inrupt.
U-Berners-Lee uthe yena neqembu lakhe abakhulumi no-"Facebook no-Google ngokuthi kufanele yini noma akufanele kulethwe ushintsho oluphelele lapho lonke ibhizinisi labo lizoshintsha khona ngokuphelele.
"Asiceli imvume yabo."
Kwenye iphosti ku-Medium eshicilelwe ngoMgqibelo, u-Berners-Lee ubhale ukuthi i-Inrupt "ifuna ukunikeza amandla ezohwebo nesimiso sokusebenza esizosiza ekuvikeleni ubuqotho nekhwalithi yewebhu entsha eyakhelwe ku-Solid."
Ngo-1994, u-Berners-Lee waguqula i-Inthanethi lapho esungula i-World Wide Web Consortium e-Massachusetts Institute of Technology.
Ezinyangeni zamuva, u-Berners-Lee uye wahola enkulumweni mpikiswano ekungathathini uhlangothi.
Ngisho nalapho kukhishwa i-Inrupt, u-Berners-Lee uzolokhu enguMsunguli noMqondisi we-World Wide Web Consortium, i-Web Foundation ne-Open Data Institute.
"Ngibheke ngabomvu ukuqala kwale nkathi ezayo yewebhu," kunezela u-Berners-Lee.
U-Bernard Vann: Kuhalaliselwa umfundisi othole i-Victoria Cross ye-WW1
Okuwukuphela komfundisi we-Church of England ukuba awine i-Victoria Cross phakathi neMpi Yezwe Yokuqala eyisosha uye wahalaliselwa edolobheni lakubo ngemva kweminyaka engu-100.
ULt Col uMfundisi u-Bernard Vann wathola umklomelo ngo-29 September 1918 ekuhlaseleni e-Bellenglise nase-Lehaucourt.
Nokho, wabulawa ngemva kwezinsuku ezine futhi akazange athole ukuthi wayewine umklomelo omkhulu kunayo yonke ebusosheni eBrithani .
Kuye kwavulwa itshe lesikhumbuzo livulwa abazukulu bakhe ababili ngesikhathi kunemashi e-Rushden, e-Northamptonshire, ngoMgqibelo.
Omunye wabazukulu bakhe, u-Michael Vann, uthe kube "uphawu oluhle" ukuthi itshe livulwe ngonyaka wekhulu ngqo kusukela umkhulu wakhe athola umklomelo.
Ngokwe-London Gazette, ngo-29 September 1918 u-Lt Col Vann wahola ibutho lakhe lawela i-Canal de Saint-Quentin "enkungwini eyayikhasa phansi kuqhuma nezibhamu nombayimbayi."
Kamuva waphuthuma waya lapho kudutshulwa khona futhi "ngesibindi esikhulu" wahola phambili ngaphambi kokugijima ephethe isibhamu wabulala amasosha amathathu.
U-Lt Col Vann wabulawa umdubuli waseJalimane ngo-4 October 1918 - ngemva nje kwenyanga ngaphambi kokuba iphele impi.
U-Michael Vann, oneminyaka engu-72, uthi izenzo zomkhulu wakhe "zingokuthile engaziyo ukuthi ngangingeke ngikwazi ukuzenza kodwa okuthile okungenza ngimhloniphe."
Yena nomfowabo u-Dr James Vann babeka izimbali ngemva kwemashi, ebiholwa yi-Brentwood Imperial Youth Band.
U-Michael Vann wathi "uzizwe enelungelo elikhulu ngokuba nengxenye kumashi" futhi wathi "ubuqhawe bengqalabutho yangempela buboniswa ngokusekela okuzonikezwa ngabantu abaningi."
Abalandeli be-MMA bahlale ubusuku bonke ukuze babukele i-Bellator 206, kodwa bathola i-Peppa Pig
Cabanga nje, uhlale ubusuku bonke ukuze ubukele i-Bellator 206 bese wenqatshelwa ukubukela umcimbi.
Lo mcimbi wase-San Jose wawunemidlalo engu-13, ehlanganisa eyisithupha esekhadini eliyinhloko futhi yayiboniswa bukhomba ubusuku bonke e-UK ku-Channel 5.
Ngo-6am, njengoba u-Gegard Mousasi no-Rory MacDonald bebelungela ukulwa, ababukeli e-UK bashiywe bemangele lapho isiteshi sishintshela ku-Peppa Pig.
Abanye bebengajabule ngemva kokuba belinde ubusuku bonke kwaze kwaba sentathakusa ikakhulu belinde lo mqhudelwano.
Omunye umlandeli ku-Twitter uchaze lokhu kushintshela kopopayi bezingane "njengehlaya ebelingalindelekile."
"Kungumthetho kahulumeni ukuthi ngo-6 a.m. lo mqhudelwano ubungafaneleki ngakho kuye kwadingeka kushintshelwe ohlelweni lwezingane, " kusho u-Dave Schwartz, iphini likamongameli we-Bellator wezokudayisa nokuxhumana, lapho ebuzwa ngalokhu kushintshwa kohlelo.
""UPeppa the pig," yebo."
Umongameli wenkampane i-Bellator u-Scott Coker uthe bazowabhekisisa amashejuli abo ukuze ahlanganise ababukeli base-UK esikhathini esizayo.
"Ngicabanga ukuthi uma ngicabanga ngokuyidlala futhi, ngicabanga ukuthi singazama ukuyidlala," kusho u-Coker.
"Kodwa yihora lesithupha ngeSonto lapho futhi ngeke sikwazi ukuyilungisa le nto kuze kube yiSonto ngesikhathi sethu, uMsombuluko ngesikhathi sabo.
Kodwa siphezu kwayo.
Ngikutshela ukuthi, ngesikhathi kushintsha kube nemilayezo eminingi okuthunyelelwene yona futhi yonke ibingemnandi.
Besizama ukuyilungisa, besicabanga ukuthi yinkinga yezobuchwepheshe.
Kodwa bekungeyona, bekuyindaba ethinta uhulumeni.
Ngiyathembisa ukuthi ngeke kuphinde kwenzeke.
Sizogcina imiqhudelwano imihlanu ingabi yisithupha - njengoba sivame ukwenza - futhi besizama ukujabulisa abalandeli bethu futhi siye seqisa.
Kube isimo ebesingafiseleki."
I-Desert Island Discs: U-Tom Daley uzizwe 'ekhishwe inyumbazane' ngenxa yobulili bakhe
Umtshuzi wama-Olympics u-Tom Daley uthi ukhule ekhishwa inyumbazane ngenxa yobulili bakhe - kodwa lokho kumnike ugqozi lokuphumelela.
Lo mtshuzi oneminyaka engu-24 uthe ubengaqapheli waze waya esikoleni samabanga aphakeme ukuthi "akuyena wonke umuntu ongithandayo."
Ekhuluma nge-Radio 4 Desert Island Discs yokuqala esakazwa ngu-Lauren Laverne, uthe ukhulume ngamalungelo ongqingili ukuze anikeze abanye "ithemba."
Uphinde wathi ukuba umzali kumenze wangaba nandaba yokuwina ama-Olympics.
Umsakazi ovamile wohlelo olunesikhathi lukhona, u-Kirsty Young, useqede izinyanga engasebenzi ngoba egula.
Evela njengomuntu olahliwe ohlelweni lokuqala luka-Laverne, u-Daley uthe uzizwe "ekhishwa inyumbazane" yiwo wonke umuntu ngesikhathi ekhula ngoba "kwakungamukelwa ukuthanda abafana namantombazane."
Uthe: "Kuze kube namuhla, leyo mizwa yokuzizwa ungelutho, ukuzizwa uhlukile, ibe imizwa engokoqobo eye yanginika amandla namandla okukwazi ukuphumelela."
Wayefuna ukubonisa ukuthi naye "ungumuntu," kusho yena, ukuze angadumazi wonke umuntu lapho kugcina kutholakele ukuthi ungungqingili.
Lo mnqobi owathola umklomelo wethusi wama-Olympic kabili usebe umuntu wephrofayili ephakeme okhankasela i-LGBT futhi wasebenzisa isimo sakhe Emidlalweni ye-Commonwealth e-Australia kulo nyaka ukuze anxuse amanye amazwe ukuba angakubheki njengokwenza ububi ubungqingili.
Uthe uye wakhuluma ngoba uzizwe enenhlanhla ukuba akwazi ukuphila engafihli lutho ngaphandle kokubhekana nezinkinga futhi ufuna ukunikeza nabanye "ithemba."
Leli qhawe elanqoba kathathu emqhudelwaneni womhlaba wonke lithe ukuthandana nomuntu wesilisa - umenzi wamafilimu wase-US u-Dustin Lance Black, ahlangana naye ngo-2013 - "kumfikele engalindele."
U-Daley washada nowanikezwa umklomelo we-Oscar, omshiya ngeminyaka engu-20, ngonyaka odlule kodwa uthe ukushiyana ngeminyaka akukaze kube inkinga.
"Lapho ubhekana nokuningi ekuphileni usemncane kangaka" - uye kuma-Olympics akhe okuqala eneminyaka engu-14 futhi ubaba wakhe wabulawa umdlavuza eminyakeni emithathu ngemva kwalokho - uthe kube nzima ukuthola umuntu alingana naye oke wabhekana nezimo ezifanayo.
Laba ababili bathola umntwana ngo-June, indodana abayiqamba ngokuthi u-Robert Ray Black-Daley, futhi u-Daley uthe "umbono wakhe" uye washintsha.
"Uma ubungangibuza ngonyaka odlule, bekuqondene nokuthi 'Ngidinga ukuwina indondo yegolide'," esho.
"Uyazi ukuthini, kunezinto ezibaluleke kakhulu kunezindondo zegolide zama-Olympic.
Indondo yami yegolide yama-Olympic ngu-Robbie."
Indodana yakhe inegama elifanayo nelikayise u-Robert, owashona ngo-2011 eneminyaka engu-40 ngemva kokutholakala enomdlavuza wobuchopho.
U-Daley uthi ubaba wakhe akazange akwamukele ukuthi uzofa futhi enye yezinto zokugcina ayezibuzile ukuthi sebenawo yini amathikithi okuya ku-London 2012 - njengoba ebefuna ukuba khona.
"Angikwazanga ukusho ukuthi 'ngeke ukwazi ukuba khona kuleyo midlalo baba'," esho.
"Ngangimbambe ngesandla lapho ephefumula okokugcina futhi kwaze kwaba yilapho ephefumula okokugcina futhi efa lapho ngabona khona ukuthi kanti naye ungumuntu njengathi," esho.
Ngonyaka olandelayo u-Daley wangenela umqhudelwano wama-2012 Olympics futhi wathola indondo yethusi.
"Ngavele ngabona ukuthi nansi into ebengilokhu ngiyifuna ukuphila kwami konke - ukutshuza phambi kwabantu bakithi Emidlalweni Yama-Olympic, ayikho into edlula leyo," kusho yena.
Kwabuye kwamenza wakhetha nengoma ayithanda kunazo zonke - i-Proud ka-Heather Small - ebilokhu inkeneneza engqondweni phakathi nesikhathi sokulungela ama-Olympics futhi isamfaka ugqozi.
I-Desert Island Discs iku-BBC Radio 4 ngeSonto ngo-11:15 BST.
U-Mickelson ongadlali kahle uhlaliswe ebhentshini ku-Ryder Cup ngoMgqibelo
U-Phil Mickelson waseMelika uzoqopha umlando ngeSonto lapho edlala umdlalo wakhe ka-47 we-Ryder Cup, kodwa kuzodingeka akhuphule amasokisi ukuze kungabi ingqophamlando edumazayo.
U-Mickelson, oyobe edlala kulesi senzakalo esiba khona kanye eminyakeni emibili okwe-12, uhlaliswe ebhentshini ngukaputeni u-Jim Furyk kuma-fourball nama-foursome angoMgqibelo.
Kunokuba kube nguye ohola phambili, njengoba evame ukuhola lapho edlalela i-United States, lo mnqobi owine kahlanu uhlukanise usuku kabili waba umgqugquzeli futhi wasebenza emdlalweni wakhe enethemba lokuthola ukuthi yini emkhinyabezayo.
Njengoba engeyena umuntu okahle olishaya liqonde ibhola ngisho noma esenesikhathi kulo mdlalo, lo mdlali oneminyaka engu-48 akafaneleki kulo mdlalo onguWafa Wafa we-Le Golf National, lapho khona indawo okudlalelwa kuyo enkulukazi ivame ukuba yinkinga uma ushaya ibhola eliya kude.
Futhi uma kuwukuthi indawo okuzodlalelwa kuyo ayiyona inkinga kangako, u-Mickelson, oyobe edlala umdlalo wesishiyagalolunye ngeSonto, uzobhekana no-Francesco Molinari ongumpetha we-British Open nokwaziyo ukushaya anembe, obedlala no-Tommy Fleetwood osemnkantsh’ ubomvu ukuze bawine yomine imidlalo yabo kuleli viki.
Uma laba baseMelika, abalahlekelwe amaphuzu amane emidlalweni engu-12 yomdlali oyedwa, beqala kahle umdlalo, umdlalo ka-Mickelson ungaba umnqamulajuqu.
U-Furyk uveze ithemba analo ngozakwabo, akukho nokho okunye akushilo.
"Uyiqonde ngokugcwele indima abenayo namuhla, wangimbambatha emhlane wangigaxa ngengalo futhi wathi uzobe ekulungele kusasa," kusho u-Furyk.
"Uyazethemba kakhulu.
Ungumdlali odumile futhi kuningi akufezile kula maqembu esikhathini esidlule, nakuleli viki.
Cishe angizange ngimcabange edlala imidlalo emibili.
Bengilindele okwengeziwe, kodwa yilokho okwenzekile futhi yilokho esicabange ukuthi kufanele sikwenze.
Ufuna ukudlala, njengawo wonke umuntu."
U-Mickelson uzoqopha umlando kabusha edlule u-Nick Faldo enanini lemidlalo ayidlalile eminingi kunayo yonke ku-Ryder Cup ngeSonto.
Kungase kube umdlalo wakhe wokugcina ku-Ryder Cup ongakaze ufane nalokho akufezile njengomdlali.
U-Mickelson usenqobe izikhathi ezingu-18, wadliwa ezingu-20 wadlala ngokulingana eziyisikhomisa, nakuba u-Furyk ethi ukuba khona kwakhe kulithuthukisile iqembu.
"Kumnandi ukuba naye, uyathanda ukubhuqa, uyahlekisa, uthanda ukwenza amahlaya ngabantu, futhi ungumuntu okumnandi ukuba naye egumbini leqembu," uye wachaza.
"Ngicabanga ukuthi abadlali abasebancane baye bakujabulela ukuba naye, futhi, kuleli viki, okube kuhle ukukubona.
Kuningi akufezayo ngaphandle kokudlala nje."
Ukaputeni waseYurophu u-Thomas Bjorn uyazi ukuthi ukuhola ngamaphuzu amaningi akusho lutho
U-Thomas Bjorn, ukaputeni waseYurophu, uyazi ukuthi ukuhola ngamaphuzu amaningi uma kuyiwa osukwini lokugcina lwamasingili ku-Ryder Cup kungashintsha kalula kube umdlalo onzima.
U-Dane wadlala okokuqala emdlalweni wango-1997 e-Valderrama, lapho iqembu elalinokaputeni ongu-Seve Ballesteros lahola ngamaphuzu amahlanu phezu kwamaMelika kodwa ekugcineni babe sebephambili ngephuzu elilodwa, bewina ngo-14½-13½.
"Uhlale uzikhumbuza ukuthi besihola ngamaphuzu amaningi e-Valderrama; sasihola ngamaphuzu amaningi e-Brookline, lapho sadliwa khona, kanti e-Valderrama, lapho sawina khona, kodwa ngamaphuzu ambalwa," kusho u-Bjorn, osesithombeni, ngemva kokubukela iKilasi lika-2018 liwina ngo-5-3 kokubili ngoLwesihlanu nayizolo ukuze lihole ngo-10-6 e-Le Golf National.
Ngakho umlando uzongibonisa mina nawo wonke umuntu kulelo qembu ukuthi akukapheli.
Yenza konke okusemandleni akho kusasa.
Shona khona futhi wenze konke ngendlela efanele.
Akukapheli kuze kube yilapho usuwatholile amaphuzu.
Sinomgomo, futhi uwukuzama ukuthatha le ndebe, futhi yilokho esigxile kukho.
Sekukade ngikusho lokhu, ngigxila kubadlali abangu-12 abaseqenjini lethu, kodwa sazi kahle ukuthi kunani ngale kuleliya qembu - abadlali abakhulu kunabo bonke emhlabeni."
Ejabule ngendlela abadlali bakhe abadlale ngayo endaweni okunzima ukudlala kuyo, u-Bjorn uye wanezela: "Ngeke ngilokothe ngifinyelele iziphetho ngalokhu.
Umdlalo wakusasa uhlukile.
Kusasa kuzonquma ukuthi umdlali ngamunye uzodlala kanjani, futhi lokho kuyinto ehlukile.
Kuhle ukuphuma uyodlala nomuntu lapho izinto zihamba kahle, kodwa uma udlala wedwa, yilapho lapho uvivinyeka khona ngokugcwele njengomdlali wegalofu.
Yilowo umlayezo okudingeka uwudlulisele kubadlali, ukuthi yenza konke ongakwenza kusasa.
Manje, ushiya umdlali okanye naye ngemuva futhi kumelwe ahambe enze konke angakwenza."
Ngokungafani no-Bjorn, aqhudelana naye u-Jim Furyk uyobe ebheke ukuthi abadlali bakhe badlale kangcono bebodwa kunalokho okwenzeke bebhangqiwe, ngaphandle kuka-Jordan Spieth no-Justin Thomas, abathole amaphuzu amathathu kwamane.
U-Furyk ngokwakhe ukwazi kokubili ukudliwa nokunqoba ngosuku lokugcina ngomzuzu wokugcina, njengoba eke waba ingxenye yeqembu eliwinayo e-Brookline ngaphambi kokuba adliwe lapho iYurophu “yagila izimanga e-Medinah.”
"Ngikhumbula kahle," usho njalo ephendula lapho ebuzwa ngendlela u-Ben Crenshaw, ukaputeni wango-1999, agqugquzela ngayo abadlali bakhe lapho kuyodlalwa ngosuku lokugcina.
"Sinemidlalo ebalulekile engu-12 kusasa, kodwa kungaba kuhle ukuqala ngegiya eliphezulu njengoba wabona e-Brookline, njengoba wabona e-Medinah.
Lapho lolo gqozi nomdlandla uqhubeka ungapheli, ufaka ingcindezi enkulu kuleyo midlalo ephakathi nendawo.
Sihlele abadlali bethu ngokuvumelana nalokho futhi sabeka abadlali bethu ngendlela esicabanga ukuthi, izosenza sikwazi ukwenza umlingo kusasa."
U-Thomas unikezwe umsebenzi wokuzama ukuhola ekulweni nokubuya emdlalweni futhi ubhekene no-Rory McIlroy emdlalweni ophambili, no-Paul Casey, u-Justin Rose, u-Jon Rahm, u-Tommy Fleetwood no-Ian Poulter nabanye baseYurophu esigabeni esiphezulu.
"Ngihambe naleli qembu limi ngale ndlela ngoba ngicabanga ukuthi lizowulungela wonke umdlalo," kusho u-Bjorn ngabadlali abakhethile.
Umkhumbi wokulwa waseJalimane usuphinde wahlehliswa
Uhlobo olusha lomkhubi lweJalimane Navy olubizwa ngokuthi i-frigate kwakumelwe luqale ukusebenza ngo-2014 lithathele indawo imikhumbi yakudala ye-Cold War-era, kodwa ngeke lube khona kuze kube okungenani ngonyaka ozayo ngenxa yama-system nezindleko ze-snowball, kubika abezindaba bandawo.
Ikhomishini ka-"Rheinland-Pfalz," umholi wemkhumbi emisha i-Baden-Wuerttemberg-class frigate, manje isihlehliselwe engxenyeni yokuqala ka-2019, kusho i-Die Zeit iphephandaba icaphuna okhulumela ezempi.
Umkhumbi kwakufanele ujoyine i-Navy ngo-2014, kodwa izinkinga ezavela ngemva kwedilivari zakhungatha ikusasa lephrojekthi ezimisele.
Imikhumbi emine ye-Baden-Wuerttemberg-class eya odwa yi-Navy kudala ngo-2007 iyona ezothahta isikhundla semikhumbi ye-Bremen-class.
Kuyaqondakala ukuthi imikhumbi izoba nombayimbayi abanamandla, izinhlobo zezibhamu eziqhumisa amabhomu okucekela phansi izindiza nemikhumbi nobuchwepheshe obufihlekile, njengokungatholakali kwendawo enikuyo, amasiginesha e-infrared and nomsindo.
Ezinye izinto ezibalulekile ezifakiwe zihlanganisa izinkathi ezinde zokunakekela - akunakwenzeka ukusebenzisa imikhumbi emisha kuze kudlule iminyaka embili endaweni izimikhumbi esuka kuyo.
Nokho, ukudileya okuqhubekayo kusho ukuthi intuthuko ebalulekile yemikhumbi yempi - izonika iJalimane sokuba namandla phesheya - izobe isiphelelwe isikhathi lapho iqala ukusebenza, kusho u-Die Zeit.
Umkhumbi onekusasa elifile i-F125 ivele emaphepheni ngonyaka odlule, lapho iJalimane Navy inqaba ukuthi kusetshenziswe umkhumbi futhi yawubuyisela e-Blohmbnase-Voss indawo yemikhumbi e-Hamburg.
kwakungokokuqala ukuthi i-Navy iphindisele umkhumbi lapho owenziwa khona ngemva kokulethwa.
Kuncane okwaziwayo mayelana nezizathu zokubuyiselwa emuva komkhumbi, kodwa abezindaba baseJalimane bathe kuningi okubalulekile obekunenkinga mayelana ne-"software ne-hardware" okwenza umkhumbi wempi ungabi usizo uma uthunyelwa empini.
Izinkinga ze-Software bezibalulekile ikakhulukazi njengoba imikhumbi i-Baden-Wuerttemberg-class izobe isetshenziswa iqembu lamatilosi angu-120 - okuyingxenye yabantu abasebenza emikhumbi emidala ye-Bremen class.
Kuphinde kwavela ukuthi umkhumbi unesisindo esiphezu kakhulu kwalokho okudingekile okunciphisa ukusebenza kwayo kunciphise namathuba okuthi i-Navy ikwazi ukufaka izinto ezizoyithuthukisa esikhathini esizayo.
Ithoni ka-7,000 u-"Rheinland-Pfalz" ukholelwa ukuthi ibinesisindo esiphinda kabili esemikhumbi efanayo eyasetshenziswa amaJalimane ngeMpi Yezwe Yesibili.
Ngaphandle kwezinkinga ze-hardware, imali yayo yonke lephrojekthi - kuhlanganisa eyokuqeqesha iqembu lamatilosi - nayo ibisiba yinkinga.
Kuthiwa ifinyelele emalini ebabazekayo izigidi ezingu-€3.1 ($3.6bn) - ukusuka ezigidini ezingu-€2.2 .
Izinkinga zemikhumbi emisha zibaluleke kakhulu njengoba kube nezixwayiso zamuva zokuthi amandla e-naval yaseJalimane ayehla.
Ekuqaleni kwalo nyaka, u-Hans-Peter Bartels, isikhulu saseJalimane sekomiti yasephalamende, savuma kuyi-Navy ukuthi kahle kahle "inakekela ukuphuma nokungena kwemikhumbi engasetshenziswa."
Isikhulu sithe izinkinga ziye zana ngokuhamba kwesikhathi, ngoba imikhumbi emidala ibingasasebenzi kodwa ayikho imikhumbi esebenza esikhundleni sayo.
Udumale ngokuthi ayikho imikhumbi ye-Baden-Wuerttemberg-class ekwazile ukujoyina i-Navy.
I-National Trust ilalela ukuphila okufihlekile kwamalulwane
Ucwaningo olusha olwenziwa endaweni yase-Scottish Highlands ihlose ukwambula indlela amalulwane asebenzisa ngayo ukwakheka kwendawo lapho ezingela ukudla.
Kuthenjwa ukuthi okuzotholakala kuzosenza siqonde kahle indlela eziphila ngayo lezi zilwane ezingavamile ezindizayo futhi kusize ekuqondiseni imisebenzi yokulonda esikhathini esizayo.
Ucwaningo lososayensi e-National Trust for Scotland luzolandela ama-pipistrelles avamile aculayo kanye namalulwane ase-Daubenton anezindlebe ezinde ezinsundu e-Inverewe Gardens e-Wester Ross.
Kuzobekwa amarekhoda akhethekile ezindaweni ezithile endaweni ukuze ahlole imisebenzi yamalulwane kuyo yonke le nkathi yonyaka.
Izisebenzi ze-NHS namavolontiya zizokwenza izinhlolovo ezincane zisebenzisa iziqapheli eziphathwa ngesandla.
Ukuhlaziya okunengqondo kosolwazi kwawo wonke amarekhodi kuzobonisa ukuvama kokukhala kwamalulwane nokuthi izilwane ezithile zenzani.
Ibalazwe lezindawo ahlala kuzo nombiko uzokhishwa ukuze kwakhiwe isithombe esinemininingwane yendawo sendlela aphila ngayo.
U-Rob Dewar, umeluleki wendawo yokugcina izilwane we-NTS, unethemba lokuthi imiphumela izoveza ukuthi iziphi izindawo ezibaluleke kakhulu kumalulwane nokuthi lezi zilwane zizisebenzisa kanjani.
Lolu lwazi luzosiza ekuboneni izinzuzo zomsebenzi wokulawulwa kwendawo njenge-meadow creation nendlela engcono kakhulu yokulondoloza izindawo ezinezihlahla yamalulwane nezinye izilwane ezihlobene nalezi.
Amalulwane e-Scotland nakuyo yonke i-UK enqabile kulo lonke leli khulu leminyaka elidlule.
Ayasongelwa ngomsebenzi wokwakha nokusungulwa kwezinto okuthinta indawo ahlala kuyo nokulahlekelwa yiyo.
Imishini ephehla ugesi nezibani kungadala ubungozi, futhi kungaba njalo nangamaphepha abulala izimpukane nemithi yokunakekela izakhiwo, kanye nokuhlaselwa amakati afuywayo.
Amalulwane akukona ngempela ukuthi awaboni.
Nokho, njengoba ezingela ebusuku amadlebe awo asebenza kakhulu kunamehlo awo uma ezingela isilwane.
Asebenzisa ikhono elithile eliyinkimbinkimbi lokuzwa ukuthi umsindo uvela ngakuphi ukuze athole izilwanyana nezinto ezisendaweni andizela kuyo.
I-NTS, enakekela izakhiwo ezingokomlando ezingaphezu kuka-270, izingadi ezibalulekile ezingu-38 namahekthare angu-76,000 endawo kulo lonke izwe, iwabheka njengabalulekile amalulwane.
Inochwepheshe abayishumi abaqeqeshiwe, abenza izinhlolovo zikhathi zonke, bahlole indawo ahlala kuyo nendlela yokuwavikela.
Le nhlangano ize yahlela nesiqiwi sase-Scotland sokuqala ngqa nokuwukuphela kwaso samalulwane e-Threave e-Dumfries nase-Galloway, okuhlala kuyo izinhlobo eziyisishiyagalombili kweziyishumi zamalulwane ase-Scotland.
Umphathi wale ndawo u-David Thompson uthi lena yindawo ekahle yokuba ahlale kuyo.
"Lapha e-Threave sindawo ekahle kakhulu yamalulwane," kusho yena.
"Sinezakhiwo ezindala, izihlahla eziningi ezinkulu nezinye izindawo ezikahle.
Kodwa kuningi ngokuqondene namalulwane esingakwazi, ngakho umsebenzi esiwenzayo lapha nakwezinye izakhiwo uzosisiza siqonde okwengeziwe ngalokho akudingayo ukuze aphile."
Ugcizelela ukubaluleka kokuhlola ukuthi akhona yini amalulwane ngaphambi kokusebenza ezakhiweni ngoba kungenzeka ukuthi ukucekela phansi indawo yawo yokuhlala eyodwa kungabulala amalulwane ensikazi angaba ngu-400 nasemancane, cishe kuwabulale wonke ahlala kuleyo ndawo.
Amalulwane ayavikelwa futhi umthetho awukuvumeli ukuwabulala, ukuwahlukumeza noma ukuwaphazamisa noma ukucekela phansi izindawo ahlala kuzo.
U-Elisabeth Ferrell, isikhulu saseScotland se-Bat Conservation Trust, ukhuthaze umphakathi ukuba uze uzosiza.
Uthe: "Kuningi okusafanele sikufunde ngamalulwane ethu futhi eziningi zezinhlobo zethu asikazi ukuthi yini ewenza aqhubeke ephila."
U-Ronaldo uyazenqaba izimangalo zokunukubeza njengoba abameli behlela ukuhlawulisa umagazini waseJalimane
U-Cristiano Ronaldo ukhulume ngezimangalo zokuthi uye wanukubeza wathi "izindaba ezingamanga," ethi abantu "bafuna ukuzithuthukisa bona" ngokusebenzisa igama lakhe.
Abameli bakhe bahlela ukuhlawulisa umagazini wezindaba waseJalimane i-Der Spiegel, oye washicilela lezi zinsolo.
Lo mdlali wase-Portugal nodlalela i-Juventus umangalelwe ngokunukubeza owesifazane waseMelika, ogama lakhe ngu-Kathryn Mayorga, egumbini lasehhotela e-Las Vegas ngo-2009.
Kubikwa ukuthi uye wamkhokhela u-$375,000 ukuze amvale umlomo ngalesi sigameko, kubika i-Der Spiegel ngoLwesihlanu.
Ekhuluma kuvidiyo yaku-Instagram Live nabalandeli bakhe abayizigidi ezingu-142 ngemva kwamahora kubikwe lezi zinsolo, u-Ronaldo, oneminyaka engu-33, uchithe le mibiko wathi "iyizindaba ezingamanga."
"Cha, cha, cha, cha , cha.
Lokho abakushilo namhlanje, kuyizindaba ezingamanga," kusho umpetha oseklonyeliswe nge-Ballon d'Or kahlanu kukhamera.
"Bazama ukuzakhela igama ngokusebenzisa elami igama.
Kuyinto evamile.
Bafuna ukuba izilomo ngokubiza igama lami, kodwa kuyingxenye yomsebenzi.
Ngijabulile futhi konke kungihambela kahle," kunezela lo mdlali, emomotheka.
Abameli baka-Ronaldo balungela ukuhlawulisa i-Der Spiegel ngalezi zinsolo, abazibize ngokuthi "umbiko ongamukeleki wezinsolo ezithinta ukuphila komuntu siqu," kusho i-Reuters.
Ummeli u-Christian Schertz uthe lo mdlali uzofuna ukubuyiselwa imali "yokulinyazwa kwesithunzi sakhe ngenani elilingana nobukhulu becala amangalelwa ngalo, cishe okuyinto ebucayi kakhulu ewukwephulwa kwamalungelo omuntu eyenzekayo muva nje."
Lesi sigameko esibikwayo kuthiwa senzeke ngo-June 2009 egunjini elise-Palms Hotel and Casino e-Las Vegas.
Ngemva kokuhlangana ku-nightclub, u-Ronaldo no-Mayorga kuthiwa baphindela egunjini lalo mdlali, lapho okuthiwa wafike wamnukubeza khona, ngokuvumelana namaphepha afakwe e-Clark County District Court e-Nevada.
U-Mayorga uthi u-Ronaldo wawa ngamadolo ngemva kwalesi senzakalo futhi wamtshela ukuthi "ungumuntu ozilungele" "ngamaphesenti angu-99" onamaphutha "ayiphesenti elilodwa."
Amadokhumenti athi u-Ronaldo uvumile ukuthi bayile ocansini bobabili, kodwa bebevumelene.
U-Mayorga naye uvumile ukuthi uyile emaphoyiseni futhi wathatha izithombe zalabo elinyazwe khona esibhedlela, kodwa kamuva uye wavuma ukuthi le ndaba isingathwe ngaphandle kwenkantolo ngoba uzizwa "esaba ukuziphindiselela" futhi ekhathazeke "ngokuhlazeka emphakathini."
Le ntokazi eneminyaka engu-34 ithi manje ifuna ukusijika isivumelwano njengoba iqhubeka ilinyazwa yilokho okuthiwa kwenzekile.
U-Ronaldo wayesezojoyina i-Real Madrid esuka ku-Manchester United ngesikhathi kubikwa lezi zinsolo, futhi kulo nyaka ushintshele eqenjini elikhulu lase-Italy i-Juve esivumelwaneni esiyizigidi ezingu-€100.
I-Brexit: I-UK 'izohlale izisola njalo' ngokulahlekelwa abenzi bezimoto
I-UK "izohlale izisola njalo" uma ingalahlekelwa isikhundla sayo njengeholayo emhlabeni wonke ekusunguleni izimoto ngemva kwe-Brexit, kusho uNobhala Wezamabhizinisi u-Greg Clark.
Uye wanezela nokuthi "kuyakhathaza" ukuthi i-Toyota UK itshele i-BBC ukuthi uma iBrithani ishiya i-EU ngaphandle kwesivumelwano izomisa okwesikhashana umkhiqizo embonini yayo e-Burnaston, eduze nase-Derby.
"Sidinga isivumelwano," kusho u-Mnu Clark.
Lo mklami wase-Japan uthe umphumela wokwephuza emngceleni lapho kwenzeka singaphumeleli isivumelwano ne-Brexit ungadala ukulahleka kwemisebenzi.
Imboni yase-Burnaston - eyenza i-Auris ne-Avensis yakwa-Toyota - ikhiqize izimoto ezingaba ngu-150,000 ngonyaka odlule futhi ezingu-90% zithunyelwe kwamanye amazwe e-European Union.
"Engikucabangayo ukuthi uma i-Britain iphuma ku-EU ekupheleni kuka-March umkhiqizo uzokuma embonini yethu," kusho u-Marvin Cooke, umphathi oqondisayo kwa-Toyota e-Burnaston.
Abanye abakhiqizi bezimoto base-UK besabise ngokuphuma ku-EU ngaphandle kwesivumelwano endleleni ukuhwebelana namanye amazwe okuzosebenza ngayo, kuhlanganise ne-Honda, i-BMW ne-Jaguar Land Rover.
I-BMW, ngokwesibonelo, ithi izoyivala imboni yayo ye-Mini e-Oxford ngemva kwenyanga kudlule i-Brexit.
Okukhathazayo ngokuyinhloko kuhlobene nalokho abaklami bezimoto abakubiza ngokuthi ubungozi uma kwenzeka singafezeki izivumelwano se-Brexit.
Umkhiqizo we-Toyota uqhutshwa "ngokwesidingo sangaleso sikhathi", izingxenye zezimoto zifika njalo ngemva kwemizuzu engu-37 zivela kubahlinzeki kokubili e-UK nase-EU ngokwezimoto ezi-odiwe.
Uma i-UK ishiya i-EU ngaphandle kwesivumelwano ngo-29 March, kungase kube neziphazamiso emngceleni lezo imboni ethi zingaholela  ekwephuzeni nasekupheleni kwezingxenye zokwakha izimoto.
Kuyinto engenakwenzeka ngo-Toyota ukubamba izimoto ezingaphezu kwezakhiwa ngosuku embonini yabo e-Derbyshire, kusho le nkampane, ngakho umkhiqizo kungadingeka umiswe.
UMnu Clark uthi uhlelo lwe-Chequers ka-Theresa May lokusebenzelana esikhathini esizayo ne-EU "lulungiswa ngokucophelela ukuze kugwemeke lokho kuhlola emngceleni."
"Kudingeka sithole isivumelwano. Sifuna ukuthola isivumelwano esingcono kunazo zonke esizosivumela njengoba ngisho hhayi nje ukuphumelela manje esizokujabulela kodwa ukuba sibambe leli thuba," etshela uhlelo lwe-Today i-BBC Radio 4.
"Ubufakazi obuvela hhayi nje kwa-Toyota kodwa nakwezinye izimboni buwukuthi kudingeka sikwazi ngokuphelele ukuqhubeka nalokho okuyiketanga labahlinzeki osekuyisikhathi kuphumelela."
I-Toyota ayikwazanga ukusho ukuthi umkhiqizo uzomiswa isikhathi eside kangakanani, kodwa ngokuhamba kwesikhathi, ixwayisa ngokuthi ukunezelwa kwezindleko kuzonciphisa ukuphumelela kwemboni futhi ekugcineni kuzolahleka imisebenzi.
U-Peter Tsouvallaris, osesebenze kwa-Burnaston iminyaka engu-24 futhi ongumxhumanisi kule mboni wenyunyana ye-Unite, uthi amalungu akhe akhathazekile: "Kulokho engikubonile uma le misebenzi iphela ayiphinde ibuye.
Umkhulumeli kahulumeni uthi: "Siye sabeka uhlelo olucacile nolunokwethenjelwa lobuhlobo bethu esikhathini esizayo ne-EU."
Umhlangano ka-Trump no-Rosenstein ungase wephuze futhi, kusho i-White House
Umhlangano olindelwe ngabomvu ka-Donald Trump nephini likammeli jikelele u-Rod Rosenstein ungase "uhlehliswe ngelinye iviki" njengoba impi yenkantolo ephakeme nokubekwa kuka-Brett Kavanaugh iqhubeka, kusho i-White House ngeSonto.
U-Rosenstein uqondisa umsebenzi wekhansela elikhethekile u-Robert Mueller, ophenya ukuphazamiseka kokhetho kwase-Russia, ukuxhumana phakathi kuka-Trump ne-Russia neziphazamiso ezingaba khona zobulungisa ezivela kumongameli.
Kungakhathaliseki ukuthi u-Trump uzolixosha yini iphini likammeli jikelele, ngokwenza kanjalo ebeke engozini inkululeko ka-Mueller, kuye kwanikeza i-Washington izindaba okungaxoxwa ngazo izinyanga.
Ngasekuqaleni kwale nyanga, i-New York Times ibike ukuthi u-Rosenstein uxoxe ngokufaka umbobho ukuze aqophe izingxoxo no-Trump nethuba lokuxoshwa kukamongameli ngesichibiyelo sama-25.
URosenstein uwenqabile lo mbiko.
Kodwa ngoMsombuluko odlule uye waya e-White House, nakuba kunemibiko yokuthi usezoshiya umsebenzi.
Esikhundleni salokho, ukuhlangana no-Trump, ngaleso sikhathi obeku-United Nations e-New York, kumenyezelwe ukuthi kuzoba ngoLwesine.
U-Trump uthe "uncamela" ukungamhlaseli u-Rosenstein kodwa umhlangano wephuzile ukuqala ukuze kugwenywe ukuba ungqubuzane necala lekomiti yokwahlulela ye-Senate lapho khona u-Kavanaugh nomunye wabesifazane ommangalele ngokunukubeza, uDkt Christine Blasey Ford, bobabili bebe ofakazi.
NgoLwesihlanu, u-Trump uyale ukuba kube nophenyo lweviki elilodwa lwe-FBI lwezimangalo ezimelene no-Kavanaugh, okuhlehlisa nakakhulu ivoti eligcwele le-Senate.
Unobhala wezindaba ka-Trump, u-Sarah Sanders, uye wavela ku-Fox News ngeSonto.
Lapho ebuzwa ngomhlangano no-Rosenstein, uthe: "Usuku lwalokho alukabekwa, kungaba kuleli viki, ngicabanga ukuthi lokho kuzohlehliswa ngelinye iviki njengoba zikhona nezinye izinto eziqhubekayo nenkantolo ephakeme.
Kodwa sizobona futhi ngiyathanda ukugcina abezindaba bazi ukuthi kwenzekani."
Abanye ababiki bezindaba bangase bangavumelani nalokho: U-Sanders akakaze abe nomhlangano wabezindaba e-White House kusukela ngo-10 September.
Umphathi-hlelo u-Chris Wallace ubuzile ukuthi kungani.
U-Sanders uthe ukuncipha kwale mihlangano akubangelwa ukuthi abezindaba "bathanda ukukhuluma," nakuba eye wathi: "Ngeke ngilenqabe iqiniso lokuthi bayakhuluma."
Ube eseveza ukuthi ukuxhumana phakathi kuka-Trump nabezindaba kuzoba kuningana.
"Umongameli wenza amaseshini emibuzo nezimpendulo ukwedlula noma imuphi omunye umongameli ongaphambi kwakhe," kusho yena, enezela ngaphandle kokuveza ubufakazi: "Siwabhekile lawo manani."
Isazoba khona imihlangano, kusho u-Sanders, kodwa "uma abezindaba bethola ithuba lokubuza umongameli wase-United States imibuzo ngokuqondile, lokho kungcono kakhulu kunokukhuluma nami.
Sizama ukwenza lokho kaningi futhi nisibonile sikwenza kakhulu emavikini ambalwa adlule futhi kuzothatha isikhundla somhlangano wabezindaba uma nizokwazi ukukhuluma nomongameli wase-United States."
U-Trump uvamile ukulalela imibuzo lapho ephuma e-White House noma lapho ehlanganyela kumaseshini esidlangalaleni noma izinkomfa zabezindaba nezivakashi ezihlonishwayo.
Akuvamile ukuba athathe imibuzo lapho eyedwa.
U-New York kuleli viki umongameli cishe ubonisile ukuthi kungani, ngokungabi nandaba futhi ngezinye izikhathi ngokukhuluma ngokunganaki phambi kwabezindaba.
Unobhala Wabezempilo ubhalela izisebenzi ze-EU e-NHS e-Scotland mayelana nalokho i-Brexit ekwesabayo
Unobhala Wabazempilo uye wabhalela izisebenzi ze-EU ezisebenza e-NHS yase-Scotland ukuze abonise ukwazisa nezifiso zezwe zokuba bahlale kuyi-post-Brexit.
U-Jeane Freeman MSP wathumela incwadi eyayisele nezinyanga ezingu-6 ngaphambi kokuba i-UK ihoxe kuyi-EU.
UHulumeni wase-Scotland kakade usezibophezele ukukhokhela izindleko ezidingekayo zezicelo zezakhamuzi ze-EU ezisebenza ngokusiza umphakathi.
Encwadini yakhe, uNksz Freeman wabhala: "Ngehlobo, izingxoxo phakathi kwe-UK ne-EU ngokuhoxa ziye zaqhubeka, zibheke ezinqumweni ezilindelekile kule kwindla.
Kodwa uHulumeni wase-UK nawo ubulokhu ulungiselela izinhlelo zayo zokuba kungabi nasivumelwano.
Ngiyazi ukuthi lokhu kungase kungabi isikhathi esikahle kini nonke.
Yingakho ngifuna ukugcizelela manje indlela engiwazisa ngayo umsebenzi owenziwa yiwo wonke amalungu ezisebenzi, kungakhathaliseki ukuthi angawaliphi izwe.
Ozakwethu abavela e-EU, nakwezinye izindawo, baletha isipiliyoni esiyigugu namakhono aqinisa futhi athuthukise umsebenzi wesevisi yezempilo, kuzuze iziguli nemiphakathi esiyisebenzelayo.
I-Scotland iyikhaya lenu futhi siyafuna ngempela ukuba nihlale lapha."
U-Christion Abercrombie Uhlinzwa Ngokuphuthumayo Ngemva Kokulimala Ekhanda
Umdlali we-Tennessee State Tigers u-Christion Abercrombie uye wahlinzwa ngokuphuthumayo ngemva kokulimala ekhanda ngoMgqibelo lapho behlulwa ngo-31-27 yi-Vanderbilt Commodores, kubika u-Mike Organ wase-Tennessee.
Umqeqeshi we-Tennessee State u-Rod Reed utshele abezindaba ukuthi ukulimala kwenzeke ngaphambi nje kwekhefu.
"Ufike ngasebhentshini wavele wawela phansi," kusho u-Reed.
Abaqeqeshi nezisebenzi ezingodokotela zinikeze u-Abercrombie umoyampilo ngasebhentshini ngaphambi kokumbeka ku-stretcher zamyisa ngemuva ukuze zimhlolisise.
Isikhulu sase-Tennessee State sitshele u-Chris Harris we-WSMV e-Nashville, e-Tennessee, ukuthi u-Abercrombie useqedile ukuhlinzwa e-Vanderbilt Medical Center.
U-Harris unezele ngokuthi "ayikho imininingwane ngohlobo/ubukhulu bokulimala okwamanje" futhi i-Tennessee State izama ukuthola ukuthi ukulimala kwenzeke nini.
U-Abercrombie, umfundi wezibomvu, ukusizini yakhe yokuqala ne-Tennessee State ngemva kokusuka e-Illinois.
Ukwaze ukumaka izikhathi ezinhlanu ngoMgqibelo ngaphambi kokuphuma emdlalweni, okwenze ingqikithi yesizini yokumaka izikhathi ezingu-18.
Abathengi bakwamanye amazwe bazokhokhiswa imali ethe xaxa yesitembu lapho bethenga indlu e-UK
Abathengi bakwamanye amazwe bazokhokhiswa imali ethe xaxa yesitembu lapho bethenga indlu e-UK ukuze le mali isetshenziselwe ukusiza abangenazindawo zokuhlala ngaphansi kwezinhlelo ezintsha zika-Tory
Lokhu kuzokwenza kube nzima ukuphumelela kuka-Corbyn ekutholeni abantu abasebasha ukuba bavote
Ukwenyuka kwemali yesitembu izofunwa kulabo abangayikhokhi intela e-UK
Abezimali balindele ukuthola imali engaba izigidi ezingu-£120 ngonyaka- ukuze basize abantu abangenamakhaya
Abathengi bakwamanye amazwe bazokhokhiswa imali yesitembu ephezudlwana uma bethenga indlu e-UK - le mali izosetshenziselwa ukusiza abangenamakhaya, u-Theresa May uzomemezela namuhla.
Lokhu kuzobhekwa njengomzamo wokukwenza kube nzima ngo-Jeremy Corbyn ukuba aphumelele emzamweni wokudonsa abantu abasha ukuba bavotele ukuthola izindlu ezengeziwe ezingabizi futhi kubhekwe abantu abahola imali eningi.
Ukukhushulwa kwemali yesitembu kuzosebenza kubantu namabhizinisi angayikhokhi intela e-UK, futhi le mali enezelwayo izosiza emzamweni kaHulumeni wokuqeda abantu abangenamakhaya.
Le mali enezelwayo - enezela emalini yamanje yesitembu, kuhlanganise namaleveli aphakeme afakwe eminyakeni emibili edlule ezindlini zesibili nezidayiswayo - ingaba amaphesenti amathathu.
Abezimali balindele ukuba lokhu kubanikeze imali engaba izigidi ezingu-£120 ngonyaka.
Amaphesenti angaba ngu-13 ezindlu ezakhiwe kabusha e-London athengwa izakhamuzi ezingezona ezase-UK, okukhuphula amanani futhi kwenze kube nzima ngabathengi abaqalayo ukuba bakwazi ukuthola izindlu.
Izindawo eziningi zabacebile kuleli - ikakhulu enhloko-dolobha - sezibe "amadolobha akhala ibhungane" ngenxa yenani eliphakeme labathengi bakwamanye amazwe abachitha isikhathi sabo esiningi bengekho kuleli zwe.
Inqubomgomo entsha ifike ngemva kwamaviki ambalwa u-Boris Johnson ekhulume ngokuncishiswa kwenkokhelo yesitembu ukuze kusizwe intsha eyengeziwe ithole izindlu zokuqala.
Umangalele amabhizinisi okwakha ngokugcina amanani ezindlu ephakeme ngokuthatha indawo yokwakha bese engayisebenzisi, futhi unxuse uNkkz May ukuba avale ama-quota ezindlini ezithengekayo ukuze kulungiswe "ihlazo lezindlu" lase-Britain.
UMnu Corbyn umemezele uchungechunge oluhlabahlosile loshintsho olucatshangelwayo ezindlini, kuhlanganise nokulawulwa kwemali yokuqasha nokuqedwa kokukhishwa endlini "ungenaphutha".
Ufuna nokunikeza amakhansela amandla amakhudlwana okwakha amakhaya amasha.
UNkkz May uthe: "Ngonyaka odlule ngithe ngizozinikela ekuvuseleleni iphupho laseBrithani - ukuthi ukuphila kufanele kube ngcono esizukulwaneni ngasinye esisha.
Futhi lokho kusho ukulungisa ukudayiswa kwezindlu.
I-Britain izohlale ikulungele ukwamukela abantu abafuna ukuhlala, ukusebenza nokwakha ukuphila lapha.
Nokho, ngeke kufaneleke ukuthi kube lula ngabantu abangebona abase-UK, kanye nezinkampane zakwamanye amazwe, ukuthenga izindlu kunezakhamuzi ezisebenza kanzima zaseBrithani.
Kubantu abaningi kakhulu iphupho lokuba nendlu seliyinto engenakufinyeleleka, nokungabi nasithunzi kokulala emgwaqweni akupheli."
U-Jack Ross: 'Isifiso sami esikhulu siwukuba umqeqeshi we-Scotland'
Umphathi we-Sunderland u-Jack Ross uthi "isifiso esikhulu" anaso ukuba umqeqeshi we-Scotland ngelinye ilanga.
URoss, oneminyaka engu-42, ufisa inselele yokusiza iqembu lase-North-East, manje elingelesithathu ku-League One, lishiywa ngamaphuzu amathathu yiqembu eliphezulu.
Uthuthele e-Stadium of Light kuleli hlobo ngemva kokusiza i-St Mirren iphindele ku-Scottish Premiership kusizini edlule.
"Bengifuna ukudlalela izwe lakithi ngisengumdlali.
Ngathola i-B cap futhi kwaphela kanjalo," uRoss utshela i-BBC Scotland's Sportsound.
"Kodwa ngikhule ngibukela i-Scotland e-Hampden kaningi nobaba ngisemncane, futhi bekulokhu kuyinto engicabanga ngayo.
Lelo thuba ngingalithola kuphela, nokho, uma ngiphumelela njengomqeqeshi weqembu elincane."
Abaqeqeshi bangaphambi kuka-Ross ku-Sunderland bahlanganisa u-Dick Advocaat, i-David Moyes, u-Sam Allardyce, u-Martin O'Neill, u-Roy Keane, u-Gus Poyet no-Paulo Di Canio.
URoss owayengumqeqeshi we-Alloa Athletic uthi akazange esabe ukungena ngemva kwala baqeqeshi abakhulu kuleli qembu elikhulu, njengoba eye enqaba izicelo ezivela ku-Barnsley ne-Ipswich Town.
"Impumelelo kimi njengamanje izokalwa ukuthi 'ngingalibuyisela yini leli qembu ku-Premier League?'
Ngenxa yokwakheka nezinto kuleli qembu, akungabazeki ukuthi kufanele lingene ku-Premier League," kusho yena.
"Akulula ukuba ngiliphindisele khona, kodwa cishe ngizozibheka njengophumelele lapho uma ngingabuyisela leli qembu khona."
U-Ross useneminyaka emithathu kuphela engumqeqeshi, ngemva kwesikhashana engumsizi womqeqeshi e-Dumbarton nezinyanga ezingu-15 eyisisebenzi esiqeqeshayo ku-Hearts.
Wabe esesiza i-Alloa yaphunyuka ezembeni, futhi waguqula i-St Mirren eyacishe yadliwa izembe yaba ompetha be-Championship ngesizini elandelayo.
Futhi u-Ross uthi uzizwa enokuqiniseka manje kunangesikhathi esengumdlali ku-Clyde, ku-Hartlepool, ku-Falkirk, ku-St Mirren naku-Hamilton Academical.
"Izinto zavele zashintsha ngokuphelele," uyakhumbula, ngokuqeqesha i-Alloa.
"Ngangiqiniseka ngokuphelele ukuthi umsebenzi wokuqeqesha ungifanele, ngaphezu kokuba umdlali.
Kuzwakala kungenangqondo ngoba ngangidlala kahle, ngiphila kahle, futhi zikhona izinto engangizijabulela.
Kodwa ukudlala akulula.
Ziningi izinto okufanele uzenze maviki onke.
Namanje ngisazenza lezo zinto uma kuziwa kukucindezeleka nengcindezi yomsebenzi kodwa ukuqeqesha ngiyakuthanda.
Nginesikhathi eside ngifuna ukuqeqesha futhi manje singiyakwenza, ngiyezwa ukuthi manje ngenza into enginesikhathi ngifuna ukuyenza kukho konke ukuphila kwami sengimdala."
Ungalalela ingxoxo ephelele ku-Sportsound ngeSonto, 30 September, ku-Radio Scotland phakathi kuka-12:00 no-13:00 BST
Isikhathi esikahle se-pint ngu-5.30pm ngoMgqibelo, kusho inhlolovo
Ukungena kwehlobo kufukule amaphabhu aseBrithani adonsa kanzima kodwa kwathwalisa kanzima izitolo zokudlela.
Amaqembu amaphabhu namabha akhushukelwe abantu abathengayo ngamaphesenti angu-2.7 ngo-July - kodwa ezitolo zokudlela kwehle ngamaphesenti angu-4.8, kusho izibalo.
U-Peter Martin, we-business consultancy CGA, okuyiyona ethole lezi zibalo, uthi: "Ukuphumelela okuqhubekayo nokuhlanganyela kweNgilandi isikhathi eside kunesilindelekile ku-World Cup kusho ukuthi u-July ulandele indlela efanayo neyangenyanga edlule ka-June, lapho amaphabhu ekhuphuke ngamaphesenti angu-2.8, ngaphandle kokuthi izitolo zokudlela zikhale ngaphansi.
Ukuwa ngamaphesenti angu-1.8 ekudayiseni ezitolo zokudlela ngo-June kuye kwaba kubi kakhulu ngo-July.
Amaphabhu okuphuzela namabha adayise kakhulu kunezitolo zokudlela.
Amaphabhu adayisa ukudla athwale kanzima nawo elangeni, nakuba kungazange kube kubi njengezitolo zokudlela.
Kubonakala sengathi abantu bebefuna nje ukuzikhipha bayothola iziphuzo.
Kumaphabhu namabha ukudayiswa kweziphuzo kukhuphuke ngamaphesenti angu-6.6 kule nyanga, ukudla kwehla ngamaphesenti amathathu."
U-Paul Newman, umhlaziyi wezenjabulo nokwamukela izivakashi RSM uthi: "Le miphumela iqhubezela phambili esikubonile kusukela ekupheleni kuka-April.
Isimo sezulu nomphumela wezenzakalo ezinkulu noma ezemidlalo kuzohlale kuyizizathu ezinamandla uma kuziwa ekudayiseni ezimakethe.
Akumangazi ukuthi izitolo zokudlela ziyaqhubeka zidonsa kanzima, nakuba ukudayisa kwehle ngamaphesenti angu-4.8 unyaka nonyaka kuzoba buhlungu naphezu kwezinkinga zezindleko eziqhubekayo.
Ihlobo elide elishisayo lifike kabi kakhulu ezitolo ezidayisa ukudla futhi ngokuhamba kwesikhathi kuzobonakala ukuthi amazinga okushisa aphansi esibe nawo ngo-August azosinika lokho esikudingayo."
Ukwanda kwamanani okudayisa kumaphabhu nezitolo zokudlela, kuhlanganise nezisanda kuvulwa, kwakungamaphesenti angu-2.7 ngo-July, okubonisa ukwehla kwamanani ebhrendi.
Imonitha ye-Coffer Peach Tracker yokudayisa kwezimboni yesektha yamaphabhu, amabha nezitolo zokudlela zase-UK, iqoqa futhi ihlaziye idatha yokusebenza yamaqembu asebenzayo angu-47, akhiqiza imali engaphezu kwezigidi ezingu-£9, futhi kuyisiqalo semboni ethuthukayo.
Ingane eyodwa kwezinhlanu inama-akhawunti ayimfihlo ezikhungo zokuxhumana awafihlele abazali bayo
Ingane eyodwa kwezinhlanu - ezinye ezineminyaka engu-11 - inama-akhawunti ayimfihlo ezikhungo zokuxhumana ewafihlele abazali bayo nothisha, kuveza inhlolovo
Inhlolovo yezingane zesikole samabanga aphakeme abangu-20,000 ibonise ukwanda emakhasini "angamanga e-Insta"
Izindaba zidala ukukhathazeka kokuthi kuphostwa izinto ezibonisa ucansi
Amaphesenti angu-20 abantu athi ane-akhawunti "okuyiyonayona" ayibonisa izingane
Ingane eyodwa kwezinhlanu - ezinye ezineminyaka engu-11 - zivula ama-akhawunti ezikhungo zokuxhumana eziwafihlela abantu abadala.
Inhlolovo yezingane zesikole samabanga aphakeme ezingu-20,000 ibonise ukukhula okusheshayo kuma-akhawunti "angamanga e-Insta" - okubhekisela kusayithi yokuthumelelana izithombe i-Instagram.
Izindaba zidale ukwesaba kokuthi kuphostwa izinto ezibonisa ucansi.
Amaphesenti angu-20 abo athi asebenzisa i-akhawunti ehlanzekile "okuyiyonayona" abayibonisa abazali, kuyilapho benawo amanye ayimfihlo.
Omunye umama obone ngandlela-thile isayithi eyimfihlo yendodakazi yakhe eneminyaka engu-13 wathola osemusha ecela abanye ukuba "bamdlwengule."
Lolu cwaningo, lwe-Digital Awareness UK ne-Headmasters" and Headmistresses" Conference (HMC) ezikoleni ezizimele, luthole amaphesenti angu-40 ezingane ezineminyaka engu-11 kuya ku-18 enamaphrofayili amabili, isigamu sabo siyavuma ukuthi sinama-akhawunti ayimfihlo.
Umphathi we-HMC u-Mike Buchanan uthi: "Kuyaphazamisa ukuthi intsha eningi kangaka ilingeka ukuba yakhe ama-akhawunti ku-inthanethi lapho abazali nothisha bengeke bayithole khona."
U-Eilidh Doyle uzoba "yizwi labadlali" kubhodi ye-Scottish Athletics
U-Eilidh Doyle ukhethwe yibhodi ye-Scottish Athletics njengomqondisi emhlanganweni waminyaka yonke wendikimba ebusayo.
U-Doyle ungumdlali othandwayo wase-Scotland futhi usihlalo u-Ian Beattie uchaze lesi senzo njengethuba elihle kulabo abaqondisa ezemidlalo ukuba bazuze kusipiliyoni sakhe esibanzi emidlalweni ehlanganisa namanye amazwe eminyakeni eyishumi edlule.
"U-Eilidh uyahlonishwa kakhulu kuyo yonke i-Scotland, i-UK nabo bonke abadlali emhlabeni futhi siyaqiniseka ukuthi ezemidlalo e-Scotland zizozuza kakhulu ngokumletha kubhodi," kusho uBeattie.
U-Doyle uthi: "Ngizimisele ukuba yizwi labadlali futhi nginethemba lokunikela kakhulu futhi ngisize ekuqondiseni ezemidlalo e-Scotland."
Lo mdlali waseMelika, owanqoba i-200 metres ne-400 metres Emidlalweni yango-1996 e-Atlanta phakathi kwezindondo zakhe ezine ze-Olympic futhi manje ongusolwazi ovamile kwa-BBC, uzithole engakwazi ukuhamba ngemva kokufa uhlangothi (TIA).
Wabhala ku-Twitter: "Enyangeni edlule namuhla ngafa uhlangothi.
Ngahluleka ukuhamba.
Odokotela bathi kimi kuzobonakala ngokuhamba kwesikhathi ukuthi ngizolulama yini noma ngezinga elingakanani.
Kube umzukuzuku kodwa ngalulama ngokugcwele, ngafunda ukuhamba futhi namuhla ngiyazivocavoca!
Ngiyabonga ngemilayezo yokungikhuthaza!"
Isikhangiso sokupompa amabele eqhathanisa omama nezinkomo idala uqhekeko ku-inthanethi
Inkampane empompa amabele idale uqhekeko ku-inthanethi ngesikhangiso esiqhathanisa omama abancelisayo nezinkomo ezisengwayo.
Ukuze iphawule ukufakwa kwalokho okuthiwa kuzoba "iphampu yamabele egqokwayo engenamsindo yokuqala emhlabeni," inkampane yamakhasimende i-Elvie ikhiphe isikhangiso esiyividiyo yomculo esiyihlaya elibhuqayo ukuze ibonise inkululeko iphampu entsha eyinikeza omama abancelisayo.
Omama abane badansela ingoma emkhombeni wezinkomo enamagama athi: "Yebo, ngiyazisenga, kodwa awuboni msila" bese ithi "Uma kuwukuthi awubonanga lo akuwona umbele, amabele ami."
Ikhorasi ithi: "Iphampe uyikhiphe, iphambe uyikhiphe, ngincelisa izingane, iphambe uyikhiphe, iphambe uyikhiphe, ngincelisa abangane bami."
Nokho, lesi sikhangiso, esishicilelwe ekhasini le-Facebook lale khampani, sidale impikiswano ku-inthanethi.
Levidiyo enabangu-77,000 asebeyibukile namakhomenti angamakhulu, ithole imibono engafani kubabukeli, lapho abaningi bethi ikubukela phansi "ubunzima" bemboni yobisi.
"Isinqumo esibi kakhulu ukusebenzisa izinkomo ukuze ukhangise ngalo mkhiqizo.
Njengathi zidinga ukukhulelwa futhi zizale ukuze zikhiphe ubisi, ngaphandle kokuthi izingane zazo ziyathathwa ngemva kwezinsukwana zizelwe," kubhala omunye.
Iphampu yakwa-Elvie yamabele ingena ifihleke ngaphakathi kwe-bra yokuncelisa (Elvie/Mother)
Omunye uthe: "Kuyisimo esinzima kubo bobabili umama nosana.
Kodwa-ke kungani ningayisebenziseli ukukhangisa ngephampu yamabele omama abakwazi ukubagcina abantwana babo?"
Omunye uthe: "Lesi sikhangiso asifaneleki."
Abanye basivikele lesi sikhangiso, omunye owesifazane wavuma ukuthi uthole ingoma "ihlekisa."
"Ngicabanga ukuthi umqondo omuhle lo.
Bengizoyithenga ukube bengisancelisa.
Ukumpompa kwakungenza ngizizwe ngifana ncamashi nenkomo.
Isikhangiso sona sinehaba kodwa ngizwile ukuthi siqonde ukuthini.
Lo mkhiqizo uzoba usizo ngempela," kubhala omunye.
Omunye uye wakhomenta: "Lesi sikhangiso siyahlekisa futhi sibhekise komama abampompayo (ngokuvamile emsebenzini noma ezindlini zangasese) futhi bazizwe "njengezinkomo."
Lesi akusona isikhangiso esidumisa noma esahlulela imboni yobisi."
Ekupheleni kwevidiyo iqembu labesimame libonisa ukuthi belikade lidansa ngamaphampu afihlekile ngaphansi kwama-bra abo.
Inhloso yalo mkhankaso usekelwe emqondweni wokuthi abesifazane abaningi abasebenzisa amaphampu amabele bathi bazizwa sengathi bayizinkomo.
Kodwa i-Elvie Pump, ayinamsindo, ayinazintambo noma amashubhu futhi uyigqoka ifihleke ngaphansi kwe-bra yokuncelisa, inikeze abesifazane inkululeko yokunyakaza, baphathe abantwana babo, futhi bazikhiphe bephampa.
U-Ana Balarin, ongumlingane ne-ECD kwa-Mother uye waphawula: "I-Elvie Pump iwumkhiqizo ozoba negalelo kakhulu ngakho ubuyifanelekela indlela yokuyikhangisa ngendlela ecacile.
Ngokufanisa abantu besifazane abancelisayo nezinkomo besifuna ukubeka ukumpompa amabele nazo zonke izinselele zako esidlangalaleni, kuyilapho sibonisa ngendlela ejabulisayo neqondakalayo umuzwa wokukhululeka iphampu entsha ezowuletha.
Lokhu akukhona okokuqala iphampu yakwa-Elvie ibe ngundabuzekwayo.

Amakhulu Ezingane Eziyizifiki Zithuthela Ngokuthula Ekamu Eliyitende Emngceleni Wase-Texas
Inani lezingane ezithathiwe eziyizifiki linyukile ngisho noma lingazange lishintshe inani lanyanga zonke labadlula emngceleni, ngokuyingxenye ngenxa yokuthi amapholisi alukhuni afakwe ihhovisi lika-Trump akwenze kwaba nzima ukunikeza izingane abasekeli.
Ngokuvamile, abasekeli abaningi kube izifiki ezingenamaphepha, futhi ziye zesaba ukubeka engcupheni ithuba lazo lokuhlala kuleli ngokuziveza njengomzali.
Le ngozi ibe yimbi ngo-June, lapho iziphathimandla zimemezela ukuthi abasekeli namanye amalungu angabantu abadala emakhaya kuzodingeka athumele imigqa yeminwe, nokuthi idatha izonikezwa iziphathimandla zezifiki.
Ngeviki elidlule, u-Matthew Albence, isikhulu se-Immigration and Customs Enforcement, sivume phambi kwe-Congress ukuthi le ejensi ibophe abantu abaningi ababhalisele ukusekela izingane ezingenabazali.
Kamuva le ejensi yavuma ukuthi amaphesenti angu-70 alabo ababoshwayo bebengenawo amacala obugebengu.
"Cishe amaphesenti angu-80 abantu abangabasekeli noma amalungu omndeni abasekeli alapha kuleli ngokungemthetho, futhi inani elikhulu labo liyizigebengu.
Ngakho siyaqhubeka sifuna labo bantu," kusho uMnu. Albence.
Zifuna ukuphrosesa izingane ngokushesha, izikhulu zisungule imithetho emisha ezodinga ukuba ezinye zazo zivele enkantolo phakathi nenyanga ziboshiwe, kungabi ngemva kwezinsuku ezingu-60, obekungumthetho wangaphambilini, ngokuvumelana nezisebenzi ze-shelter.
Eziningi zizovela ocingweni lwenkomfa lwevidiyo, ngeke ziye ngokoqobo, ukuze zizicelele amalungelo angokomthetho kujaji lezifiki.
Lezo ezibhekwa njengezingafaneleki zizodingiswa ngokushesha.
Uma izingane zihlala isikhathi eside ziboshiwe, maningi amathuba okuba zikhathazeke noma zicindezeleke, okungaholela odlameni noma ekutheni zizame ukubaleka, ngokuvumelana nezisebenzi ze-shelter nemibiko ekhishiwe evela kusistimu ezinyangeni ezidlule.
Abameli bathi lokhu kukhathazeka kuyakhula esikhungweni esikhudlwana njengase-Tornillo, lapho izimpawu zokuthi ingane idonsa kanzima kungenzeka anganakwa, ngenxa yobukhulu bendawo.
Banezele nokuthi ukuthutha izingane ziyiswe edolobheni letende ngaphandle kokuzinika isikhathi sokuzilungiselela ngokomzwelo noma ukuvalelisa kubangane kungadala ukuphazamiseka eziningi esezinakho kakade.
I-Syria itshela amabutho ase-US, ase-France nawase-Turkey 'ahlaselayo' ukuba ahoxe ngokushesha
Ekhuluma ne-UN General Assembly, uNgqongqoshe Wezangaphandle u-Walid al-Moualem ukhulume nababaleki base-Syria ukuba baphindele ekhaya, ngisho noma impi ezweni lakubo manje isisonyakeni wayo wesishiyagalombili.
U-Moualem, ophinde abe iphini likangqongqoshe omkhulu, uthe amabutho akwamanye amazwe abese-Syria ngokungemthetho, ethi azoqeda ubuphekula, futhi "azosingathwa ngendlela efanele."
"Kumelwe ahambe masinyane ngaphandle kwemibandela," utshele izilaleli.
U-Moualem ugomele ngokuthi "ukulwa nobuphekula cishe sekuyaphela" eSyria, lapho abantu abangaphezu kuka-360,000 beye bafa kusukela ngo-2011, nabantu abayizigidi bekhishiwe emizini yabo.
Uthe i-Damascus izoqhubeka "ilwa le mpi engcwele size siyihlanze yonke indawo yase-Syria" emaqenjini obuphekula kanye "nanoma ubani ovela kwelinye izwe."
I-United States inamasosha angaba ngu-2,000 e-Syria, agxile kakhulu ekuqeqesheni nasekuqondiseni amabutho e-Kurdish ne-Syrian Arabs aphikisana noMongameli u-Bashar al-Assad.
I-France inamasosha angaphezu kuka-1,000 ayimigundatshani ezweni eloniwe yimpi.
Mayelana nababaleki, u-Moualem uthe izimo ziyabavumela ukuba babuyele, futhi usola "amazwe athile asentshonalanga" “ngokubasabisa" okwenze ababaleki bangabe besabuya.
Uthe, "Sesikhulume nenhlangano yomphakathi womhlaba wonke kanye neyezenhlalakahle yabantu ukuba ziqikelele ukuthi ababaleki bayabuyela."
"Baqhuba ipolitiki ngendaba okufanele isingathwe kuphela abezenhlalakahle zabantu."
I-United States ne-European Union baxwayise ngokuthi ngeke bayisize iSyria yakhe kabusha kuze kube yilapho sekwenziwe isivumelwano sezepolitiki phakathi ne-Assad kanye abamelene nokuqedwa kwempi.
Amanxusa e-UN athi isivumelwano esisanda kwenziwa phakathi kwe-Russia ne-Turkey sokwakha umngcele enqabeni yamambuka enkulu yokugcina yase-Idlib yakhe ithuba yokuqhubekela phambili nezingxoxo zepolitiki.
Isivumelwano se-Russia ne-Turkey sivimbele ukuhlasela okukhulu kwamasosha ase-Syria asekelwa yi-Russia esifundazweni, lapho okuhlala khona izigidi ezintathu zabantu.
Nokho uMoualem ugcizelele ukuthi isivumelwano “besibekelwe isikhathi esicacile" futhi unethemba lokuthi amasosha azohlasela ama-jihadist kanye nabalwayo be-Nustra Front abaxhumene ne-Al-Qaeda, "abazoqothulwa."
Inxusa ye-UN uStaffan de Mistura uthemba ukuthi maduze uzohlela imihlangano yokuqala yekomiti entsha ehlanganisa uhulumeni namalungu aphikisayo ukuze kubhalwe umthethosisekelo ngemva kwempi wase-Syria futhi uhlelembe indlela yokhetho.
UMoualem ubeke imingcele yokuhlanganyela kukahulumeni wase-Syria ekomitini, ethi umsebenzi wephaneli kufanele ugcine "ngokubhekisisa izihloko zomthethosisekelo omusha," futhi waxwayisa ngokugxambukela.

Izindodla zezimali zifakwa okhethweni lwenkathi ephakathi yomqhudelwano ye-House
Akumangazi ukuthi okwesi-17 kwase-17 kuthola izindodla zezimali, ngenxa yokumiswa kabusha kwezifunda ze-congress okuphume nabaphathi ababili ekuncintisaneni ngesihlalo esifanayo.
Lesi sifunda sase-Pittsburg esisanda kudwetshwa kabusha simbeka emqhudelwaneni u-Democrat Rep. Conor Lamb - owanqoba isihlalo sakhe kwesinye isifunda okhethweni olukhethekile entwasahlobo ngonyaka odlule.
U-Lamb useqhudelana nenye ingqungqulu, u-Republican Keith Rothfus, njengamanje omelela isifunda esidala sase-Pennsylvania sika-12, esiwelela ngokugcwele kwesisha esingu-17.
Amabalazwe adwetshwa kabusha ngemva kokuba iNkantolo Ephakeme yase-Pennsylvania yanquma ngo-January ukuthi izifunda ezindala zephula umthethosisekelo ngokweba amavoti aye kuma-Republican.
Umqhudelwano kulesi esisha esingu-17 ususe umqhudelwano womkhankaso wezimali phakathi kwamalunga ezimali eqembu elikhulu, i-Democratic Campaign Congressional Committee (DCCC) ne-National Republican Campaign Committee (NRCC).
Igama elithi Lamb laduma e-Pennsylvania ngemva kokuwina ukhetho olukhethekile ngo-March olwalubukelwe abantu abaningi lwe-Pennsylvania's 18th Congressional District.
Leso sikhundla besiphethwe yi-Republican isikhathi esingaphezu kweminyaka eyishumi, uMongameli u-Donald Trump wawina isigodi ngamaphoyinti awu-20.

I-U.S. Yacabangela ukujezisa i-El Salvador Ngokusekela I-China, Yabe Isihoxa
Ama-diplomat aphawule ukuthi i-Dominican Republic ne-Panama isikade isiyiphawulile i-Beijing, ngokuncenga okuncane okuvela e-Washington.
UMnu. Trump waba nomhlangano okhululekile noMongameli u-Juan Carlos Varela wase-Panama ngo-June 2017 futhi baba sehhotela e-Panama kwaze kwaba yilapho besusa iqembu lokuqondisa le-Trump Organization.
Izikhulu ze-State Department zinqume ukuphinde zibize izikhulu zase-America ze-diplomatic missions zase-El Salvador, i-Dominican Republic kanye ne-Panama mayelana "nesinqumo samuva sokungasebenzelani ne-Taiwan," uHeather Nauert, okhulumela umnyango, usho njalo ekuqaleni kwale nyanga.
Kodwa kuhlawuliswe kuphela i-El Salvador, ngezigidi ezingu-$140 ngokusiza iMelika ngo-2017, nangokulawula ama-narcotics, ukuthuthukisa nokusekela ezomnotho.
Inhlawulo esikiselwe, ehlanganisa ukunqanyulwa kosizo ngokwezimali futhi yabela imingcele mayelana namavisa, okwakungase kulizwise ubuhlungu izwe i-Central America ngenxa yokwanda kokungabibikho komsebenzi nokubulala.
Njengoba imihlangano yabo ithuthuka, izikhulu zase-North America nezase-Central America zahlehlisa inkomfa ephakeme egxile ekuvikeleni nasekuthuthukiseni umnotho ukuze ilandele umbuthano ofanayo ngonyaka odlule owabhekwa njengesinyathelo sokuya phambili semizamo yokuvimbela izifiki ukuba ziye e-United States.
Kodwa phakathi kuka-September, izikhulu eziphakeme zokuqondisa zenza kwacaca ukuthi zazifuna inkomfa iqhubekele phambili, iqeda ngokuphumelelayo noma yimuphi umbono wokuhlawulisa i-El Salvador.
Iphini likaMongameli uMike Pence manje sekufanele ahlele ukukhuluma nenkomfa, manje ehlelwe ukuba maphakathi no-October, njengophawu olulethwa abalawuli kulo mhlangano, kusho izikhulu.
Futhi abameleli abathathu baseMelika baphindela ngokuthula e-El Salvador, e-Panama nase-Dominican Republic ngaphandle kwemilayezo emisha enamandla noma izijeziso ezivela e-Washington.
Usomlomo we-White House ka-Mnu. Bolton wenqabile ukuphawula ngemininingwane yenkulumo-mpikiswano eyachazwa izikhulu zaseMelika ezintathu, kuhlanganise nezithunywa ezimbili, ezavuma ukuxoxa ngezinhloso zangaphakathi ngesimo sobumfihlo.
Ama-akhawunti azo aqinisekiswe umhlaziyi wangaphandle osondelene nabalawuli futhi wakhuluma ngesimo sobumfihlo.

Abesifazane abakwazi ukulala ngoba besaba indaba yezimali zomhlalaphansi
Naphezu kokuba ababambiqhaza benhlolovo bebenombono ocacile wendlela abafuna ukunakekelwa ngayo, bambalwa abantu abebekhuluma nemindeni yabo ngakho.
Cishe isigamu sabantu kucwaningo lukaZwelonke bathi bakhuluma nabantu abashade nabo ngezindleko zokunakekelwa isikhathi eside.
Bangamaphesenti angu-10 kuphela abathi bakhuluma nezingane zabo ngakho.
"Abantu bafuna ukunakekelwa ilungu lomndeni, kodwa abathathi izinyathelo zokuxoxa ngakho," kusho uHolly Snyder, iphini likamongameli webhizinisi lomshwalense wokuphila i-Nationwide.
Ake kuqalwe la.
Xoxa nomuntu oshade naye nezingane zakho: Awukwazi ukulungiselela umndeni wakho ukuba ukunakekele uma ungawutsheli izifiso zakho kusenesikhathi.
Sebenza nomeluleki wakho nomndeni wakho ukuze nixoxe ngokuthi uzokuthola kanjani futhi kuphi ukunakekelwa, ngoba lezo zinqumo zingaba nomthelela omkhulu ekuboneni izindleko.
Letha umeluleki wakho wezimali: Umeluleki wakho angakusiza nangokuthi uze nendlela yokukhokhela lezo zindleko.
Izinqumo zakho zezimali zokunakekelwa isikhathi eside zingahlanganisa inqubomgomo yomshwalense yokunakekelwa isikhathi eside evamile, inqubomgomo yomshwalense wokuphila okunika imali uma ukhansela ukuze ukwazi ukukhokhela lezi zindleko noma ibe umshwalense wempilo yakho - uma nje usenayo imali.
Lungisa amadokhumenti akho ezomthetho: Vimbela izimpi zezomthetho.
Thola iphrokzi yokunakekelwa kwempilo ukuze umise umuntu omethembayo ukuba anakekele ezokwelashwa kwakho futhi aqikelele ukuthi odokotela bahambisana nezifiso zakho uma kwenzeka awukwazi ukukhuluma.
Futhi, cabangela ne-power of attorney ezimalini zakho.
Uzokhetha umuntu omethembayo ukuba akwenzele izinqumo ngezimali zakho futhi aqikelele ukuthi izindleko zakho ziyakhokhwa uma ungasakwazi kwenza lutho.
Ungayikhohlwa imininingwane emincane: Cabanga umzali wakho osekhulile uvelelwa isimo esiphuthumayo sezempilo futhi uphuthunyiswa esibhedlela.
Ungakwazi yini ukuphendula imibuzo mayelana nemithi nezinto ezimgulisayo?
Bhala phansi leyo mininingwane ngokuhlelekile ukuze ulungele leso simo.
"Akuzona nje izimali kuphela okufanele zibhekwe, kodwa bangobani odokotela?" kubuza uMartin.
"Iyiphi imithi?
Ubani ozonakekela inja?
Yiba nohlelo olukhona."
Umlisa udutshulwe kaningana nge-air rifle e-Ilfracombe
Kudutshulwe umlisa kaningana nge-air rifle njengoba ehamba eya ekhaya ngemva kokuzikhipha ebusuku.
Lona odutshuliwe, oneminyaka engaba ngu-40, wayese-Oxford Grove e-Ilfracombe, e-Devon, ngesikhathi edutshulwa esifubeni, esiswini nasesandleni.
Amaphoyisa achaze ukudutshulwa lokhu, okwenzeke cishe ngawo-02:30 BST, "njengesigameko ebesingalindelekile."
Isisulu asimbonanga umhlaseli.
Akalimalanga kakhulu kanti amaphoyisa asekhulumile nofakazi.
Ukuzamazama komhlaba nama-tsunami e-Indonesia
Okungenani abantu abangu-384 babulawe ukuzamazama komhlaba ne-tsunami edolobheni lase-Indonesian okuthiwa yi-Palu ngoLwesihlanu, kusho izikhulu, isibalo sabafile kulindeleke ukuba sande.
Njengoba ezokuxhumana zingasebenzi, izisebenzi eziletha usizo azikwazanga ukuthola imininingwane evela eziphathimandleni zase-Donggala, indawo esenyakatho ye-Palu esondelene nemaphakathi lokuzamazama okungu-7.5.
E-Palu, abantu abangaphezu kuka-16,000 bamukisiwe ngemva kokuhlasela kwalezi zinhlekelele.
Nawa amaqiniso athile abalulekile nge-Palu kanye ne-Donggala, esiqhingini sase-Sulawesi:
I-Palu iyinhloko-dolobha yesifunda sase-Central Sulawesi, isendaweni engasemaphethelweni ogu entshonalanga yesiqhingi sase-Sulawesi, futhi inesilinganiso sabantu abangu-379,800 ngo-2017.
Idolobha beligubha iminyaka engu-40 likhona ngesikhathi kuhlasela i-tsunami.
I-Donggala iyindawo eyibanga elingaphezu kuka-300 km (amamayela angu-180) ngasogwini olusenyakatho-ntshonalanga yesiqhingi sase-Sulawesi.
Le ndawo, isifunda esingaphansi kwesifundazwe, sasinabantu abangaba ngu-299,200 ngo-2017.
Ukudoba nokulima kuyizindlela zokuphila emnothweni wesifunda sase-Central Sulawesi, ikakhulu isifunda esingasogwini se-Donggala.
Izimayini zezinhlamvu zemali nazo zibalulekile kulesi sifunda, zitholakala ngobuningi e-Morowali, ngale kogu lwe-Sulawesi.
I-Palu ne-Donggala ihlaselwe ama-tsunami kaningana eminyakeni engu-100 edlule, ngokuvumelana ne-Disaster Mitigation Agency yase-Indonesia.
Ngo-1938, i-tsunami yabulala abantu abangaphezu kuka-200 yacekela phansi izindlu ezingamakhulu e-Donggala.
I-tsunami yaphinde yahlasela nentshonalanga ye-Donggala ngo-1996, ibulala abantu abangu-9.
I-Indonesia isendaweni enyakazayo ye-Pacific Ring of Fire futhi ivame ukuhlaselwa ukuzamazama komhlaba.
Nazi izindawo ezithile ezahlaselwa ukuzamazama komhlaba okukhulu nama-tsunami eminyakeni yamuva:
Ngo-2004: Ukuzamazama okukhulu entshonalanga yogu lwesifundazwe sase-Indonesia i-Aceh enyakatho ye-Sumatra ngo-Dec. 26 yenza kwaba ne-tsunami eyahlasela amazwe angu-14, yabulala abantu abangu-226,000 eduze nogu lwe-Indian Ocean, nabantu abangaphezu kwengxenye ye-Aceh.
Ngo-2005: Ukuzamazama komhlaba okulandelanayo kwahlasela intshonalanga yogu lwe-Sumatra ngasekupheleni kuka-March kuya ekuqaleni kuka-April.
Abantu abangamakhulu bafa eSiqhingini sase-Nias, ethe ukuqhela ngasogwini lwase-Sumatra.
Ngo-2006: Isilinganiso esingu-6.8 sahlasela iningizimu ye-Java, isiqhingi esinabantu abaningi kunazo zonke sase-Indonesia, kwadaleka i-tsunami eyacekela phansi ugu oluseningizimu, yabulala abantu abangaba ngu-700.
Ngo-2009: Isilinganiso esingu-7.6 sokuzamazama sahlasela eduze nedolobha lase-Padang, inhloko-dolobha yasesifundeni sase-West Sumatra.
Kwafa abantu abangaphezu kuka-1,100.
Ngo-2010: Isilinganiso esingu-7.5 sokuzamazama sahlasela esinye seziqhingi zase-Mentawai, ngase-Sumatra, kwadaleka i-tsunami engamamitha angaba ngu-10 eyacekela phansi izindawo eziningi yabulala nabantu abangu-300.
Ngo-2016: Ukuzamazama okuncane kwahlasela i-Pidie Jaya e-Aceh, yacekela phansi futhi yenza abantu besaba bekhumbula ukuzamazama okubi kwango-2004 ne-tsunami.
Kulokhu akubanga ne-tsunami, kodwa bangaphezu kuka-100 abantu ababulawe izakhiwo ezawa.
Ngo-2018: Ukuzamazama komhlaba okunamandla kwahlasela isiqhingi sezivakashi sase-Indonesia e-Lombok, sabulala abantu abangaphezu kuka-500, ikakhulukazi ingxenye yenyakatho yesiqhingi.
Lokhu kuhlasela kwacekela phansi izakhiwo eziyizinkulungwane futhi zashiya izivakashi eziyizinkulungwane zingenamakhaya.
Indodana Endala Ka-Sarah Palin Iboshelwe Icala Lodlame Lwasekhaya
U-Track Palin, indodana endala yombusi wangaphambili wase-Alaska nekhendidethi yokuba iphini likamongameli u-Sarah Palin, uboshiwe ngamacala okuhlukumeza.
U-Palin, oneminyaka engu-29, wase-Wasilla, e-Alaska, uboshelwe amacala okuhlukumeza, ukuphazamisa umbiko wodlame nokumelana nokuboshwa, ngokuvumelana nombiko okhishwe ngoMgqibelo yi-Alaska State Troopers.
Ngokuvumelana nombiko wamaphoyisa, lapho owesifazane ajwayelene naye ezama ukufonela amaphoyisa ukuze abike lokhu kwephulwa komthetho, wamthathela ucingo.

Uye wavela enkantolo ngoMgqibelo, lapho athi khona "akanacala, ngokuqinisekile" lapho ebuzwa, kubika le nethiwekhi.
U-Palin ubhekene namacala amathathu Esigaba A, okusho ukuthi angase aboshwe isikhathi esingunyaka futhi ahlawuliswe u-$250,000.
Umangalelwe nangecala Lesigaba B, azohlawuliswa lona usuku ejele no-$2,000.
Akuqali ukuba u-Palin amangalelwe ngamacala obugebengu.
Ngo-December 2017, wamangalelwa ngokushaya ubaba wakhe, u-Todd Palin.
Umama wakhe, u-Sarah Palin, wafonela amaphoyisa ukuze abike lesi senzo.
Le ndaba njengamanje isezandleni ze-Veteran's Court yase-Alaska.
Ngo-January 2016 wamangalelwa ngodlame lwasekhaya, ukuphazamisa umbiko wokwephula umthetho wodlame lwasekhaya, nokuba nesikhali ngesikhathi edakiwe ngokuqondene naleso sigameko.
Intombi yakhe yayithe umshaye ngesibhakela ebusweni.
U-Sarah Palin wagxekwa amaqembu ochwepheshe ngo-2016 ngemva kokuthi izenzo zendodana yakhe zodlame zihlobene ne-PTSD ebangelwa umsebenzi wakhe wase-Iraq.

Amanethiwekhi kagesi nokuxhumana awasebenzi futhi inani labafile lingase lande ezinsukwini ezizayo.
Lokhu kuzamazama komhlaba kuhlasele indawo emaphakathi ne-Sulawesi engasenyakatho-mpumalanga yenhloko-dolobha yase-Indonesia, i-Jakarta.
